*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Include          SLIM_USER_CLF_HELP_F01
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form selection_screen_output
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Selection-screen PBO
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM selection_screen_output .

  DATA: lv_pce      TYPE flag,
        lv_tab_name TYPE sobj_name,
        lv_count    TYPE i.

  LOOP AT SCREEN.

    IF gv_pce = space AND screen-name = 'P_PCE'.
      screen-active = 0.
      p_pce = space.
    ENDIF.

    " PCE Ruleset
    IF p_pce = 'X' AND ( screen-group1 = 'PRF' OR
                         screen-group1 = 'PRL' OR
                         screen-group1 = 'PRN' ).
      screen-input = 0.
      p_noeng = 'X'.
    ENDIF.

    " Local Ruleset
    IF p_loc = 'X' AND screen-group1 = 'PRF'.
      screen-input = 0.
    ENDIF.

    " Uploaded Ruleset
    IF p_xls = 'X' AND screen-group1 = 'PRL'.
      screen-input = 0.
    ENDIF.

    IF screen-group1 EQ 'USR'.
      IF rb_user = 'X'.
        screen-active = 1.
      ELSE.
        screen-active = 0.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.

    IF screen-group1 EQ 'ROL'.
      IF rb_role = 'X'.
        screen-active = 1.
      ELSE.
        screen-active = 0.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.

    IF screen-name CS 'SO_ROLE'.
      IF p_role = space.
        screen-input = 0.
      ELSE.
        screen-input = 1.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.

    IF screen-name CS 'SO_PROFN'.
      IF p_profn = space.
        screen-input = 0.
      ELSE.
        screen-input = 1.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.

    IF rb_user = ' ' AND rb_role = ' '.
      IF   screen-group1 = 'PRF' OR screen-group1 = 'PRP' OR screen-group1 = 'PRL'
        OR screen-group1 = 'PRS' OR screen-group1 = 'PRN' OR screen-group1 = 'PRT'.
        screen-active = 0.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.

*    IF rb_role = 'X'. " No User Classification Transfer for Role Validations

    " Hide Transfer Option for the moment
    IF screen-group1 = 'PRT'.
      screen-active = 0.
      CLEAR p_trans.
    ENDIF.
*    ENDIF.

    IF rb_rule = ' '.
      IF screen-group1 = 'PLR'.
        screen-active = 0.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.

    IF screen-group1 EQ 'IMP'.
      IF rb_uplo = 'X'.
        screen-active = 1.
      ELSE.
        screen-active = 0.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.

    IF screen-name = 'P_PWDD' OR
       screen-name = 'P_PWDC' OR
       screen-name = 'P_PWDE'.
      screen-invisible = 1.
    ENDIF.

    MODIFY SCREEN.
  ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.                    "selection_screen_output

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form selection_screen
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Selection-screen PAI
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM selection_screen .

  CASE sy-dynnr.

    WHEN 1000.
      CASE 'X'.
        WHEN rb_user.
          gv_valid_type = gc_valid_type-user_validation.
        WHEN rb_role.
          gv_valid_type = gc_valid_type-role_validation.
        WHEN rb_uplo.
          gv_valid_type = gc_valid_type-previous_execution.
        WHEN rb_rule.
          gv_valid_type = gc_valid_type-rules_n_results.
      ENDCASE.

      PERFORM user_command.

    WHEN 2000.
      IF p_pwde NE p_pwdc.
        " Check whether entered password is equal to confirmed password
        MESSAGE TEXT-e06 TYPE 'E'.
      ENDIF.

  ENDCASE.

ENDFORM.                    "selection_screen

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form init
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Selection-screen initialization and some default values
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM init .

  DATA: ct_rules    TYPE gty_t_rules_file,
        lv_dummy    TYPE c,
        lv_count    TYPE i,
        lv_tab_name TYPE sobj_name.


  " Authorization Check
  AUTHORITY-CHECK OBJECT 'S_USER_GRP' ID 'ACTVT' FIELD '03'
                                      ID 'CLASS' DUMMY.
  IF sy-subrc <> 0.
    MESSAGE 'You do not have S_USER_GRP authorization.' TYPE 'E'. "##NO_TEXT
  ENDIF.

  " Role Validation default values
  p_role  = 'X'.
  p_no_uv = 'X'.

  " Start with User Validation
  gv_valid_type = gc_valid_type-user_validation.

  " Read file name
  GET PARAMETER ID 'DXFILENAME' FIELD p_file.

  " Get the current Note Version
  PERFORM get_note_version USING gv_nvers.
  SPLIT gv_nvers AT ';' INTO gv_nvers lv_dummy.
  SHIFT gv_nvers LEFT DELETING LEADING '0'.
  CONCATENATE 'Note Version:' gv_nvers INTO gv_nvers SEPARATED BY space ##NO_TEXT.

  " Check for local PCE Ruleset
  SELECT SINGLE obj_name FROM tadir INTO lv_tab_name
         WHERE pgmid    = 'R3TR'
           AND object   = 'TABL'
           AND obj_name = 'SLIMPC_RULESET'.

  IF sy-subrc = 0. " PCE ruleset table is present
    " Check whether it's filled
    SELECT COUNT( * ) FROM (lv_tab_name) INTO lv_count.
    IF lv_count > 50.
      p_pce  = 'X'. " Selection Screen Variable
      gv_pce = 'X'. " Global Variable
    ENDIF.
  ELSE.
    CLEAR gv_pce.
    p_loc = 'X'.
  ENDIF.

  " Rulesets & Results (Buttons)
  brulupl = 'Upload'.
  bruldel = 'Delete'.
  bresdel = 'Delete'.
  bresdis = 'Display'.

ENDFORM.                    "init

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form user_command
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& User commands from the selection screen
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM user_command.

  DATA: lv_ucomm     TYPE syucomm,
        lv_objkey    LIKE slim_cluster-cluster_id VALUE space,
        lv_answer(1) TYPE c.

  DATA: lv_filetype    TYPE string,
        lv_file_filter TYPE string,
        lt_files       TYPE filetable,
        lv_file        TYPE text255,
        lv_rc          TYPE i.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_file> TYPE file_table.

  lv_ucomm = sscrfields-ucomm.

  CASE lv_ucomm.

    WHEN 'RESDIS'. " Display Results

      PERFORM run.

    WHEN 'RULUPL'. " Ruleset Upload

      " File Selector
      lv_filetype    = cl_gui_frontend_services=>filetype_excel.
      lv_file_filter = cl_gui_frontend_services=>filetype_excel.

      CALL METHOD cl_gui_frontend_services=>file_open_dialog
        EXPORTING
          default_extension = lv_filetype
          file_filter       = lv_file_filter
        CHANGING
          file_table        = lt_files
          rc                = lv_rc
        EXCEPTIONS
          OTHERS            = 1.

      IF sy-subrc = 0.
        READ TABLE lt_files ASSIGNING <ls_file> INDEX 1.
        IF sy-subrc = 0.
          lv_file = <ls_file>-filename.
        ENDIF.
      ENDIF.

      CHECK lv_file IS NOT INITIAL.

      " Import the ruleset from file system
      PERFORM import_ruleset USING lv_file CHANGING gt_rules_plain.
      SORT  gt_rules_plain.
      CLEAR gt_rules.

      TRY.
          " Get filename only
          CALL METHOD cl_bcs_utilities=>split_path
            EXPORTING
              iv_path = lv_file
            IMPORTING
              ev_name = lv_objkey.

        CATCH cx_bcs.
          lv_objkey = 'STAR_Ruleset'.
      ENDTRY.

      CONCATENATE 'R' lv_objkey INTO lv_objkey.
      DELETE FROM DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.
      EXPORT gt_rules_plain TO DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.

      IF sy-subrc <> 0.
        MESSAGE 'Ruleset could not be saved' TYPE 'I'.
      ELSE.
        MESSAGE 'Ruleset has been uploaded' TYPE 'S'.
      ENDIF.

    WHEN 'RULDEL'.

      CHECK p_locf2 IS NOT INITIAL.

      " Confirmation
      CALL FUNCTION 'POPUP_TO_CONFIRM'
        EXPORTING
          titlebar              = TEXT-t34
          text_question         = 'Do you want to delete the selected Ruleset?'(t37)
          text_button_1         = 'Yes'(t35)
          text_button_2         = 'No'(t36)
          default_button        = '2'
          display_cancel_button = ' '
        IMPORTING
          answer                = lv_answer
        EXCEPTIONS
          text_not_found        = 1
          OTHERS                = 2.

      IF sy-subrc <> 0 OR lv_answer <> '1'.
        " Action was cancelled
        RETURN.
      ENDIF.

      CONCATENATE 'R' p_locf2 INTO lv_objkey.
      DELETE FROM DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.

      MESSAGE 'Ruleset has been deleted' TYPE 'S'.

      CLEAR p_locf2.

    WHEN 'RESDEL'.

      CHECK p_locr IS NOT INITIAL.

      " Confirmation
      CALL FUNCTION 'POPUP_TO_CONFIRM'
        EXPORTING
          titlebar              = TEXT-t34
          text_question         = 'Do you want to delete the selected Result?'(t38)
          text_button_1         = 'Yes'(t35)
          text_button_2         = 'No'(t36)
          default_button        = '2'
          display_cancel_button = ' '
        IMPORTING
          answer                = lv_answer
        EXCEPTIONS
          text_not_found        = 1
          OTHERS                = 2.

      IF sy-subrc <> 0 OR lv_answer <> '1'.
        " Action was cancelled
        RETURN.
      ENDIF.

      CONCATENATE '1' p_locr INTO lv_objkey.
      DELETE FROM DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.

      CONCATENATE '2' p_locr INTO lv_objkey.
      DELETE FROM DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.

      CONCATENATE '3' p_locr INTO lv_objkey.
      DELETE FROM DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.

      CONCATENATE '4' p_locr INTO lv_objkey.
      DELETE FROM DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.

      MESSAGE 'Results have been deleted' TYPE 'S'.

      CLEAR p_locr.

  ENDCASE.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form run
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Run Validation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM run .

  IF gv_valid_type = gc_valid_type-user_validation.
    PERFORM get_rules.
    PERFORM user_validation.
  ELSEIF gv_valid_type = gc_valid_type-role_validation.
    PERFORM get_rules.
    PERFORM role_validation.
  ELSEIF gv_valid_type = gc_valid_type-previous_execution.
    PERFORM import_validation.
  ELSEIF gv_valid_type = gc_valid_type-rules_n_results.
    CHECK p_locr IS NOT INITIAL.
    IF p_locr+3(4) = '_UV_'. " User Validation
      " Reset all necessary variables
      UNASSIGN <gt_total_classif_users>.
      CLEAR: gt_user_data, gt_object_result, gt_role_result.
      IF gr_container400 IS BOUND.
        CALL METHOD gr_container400->free.
        CLEAR: gr_container400, gr_table400.
      ENDIF.

      PERFORM read_user_validation.
      PERFORM get_texts.
      PERFORM prepare_output_user_validation.
      PERFORM display_classification_users.
    ELSE.                " Role Validation
      " Reset all necessary variables
      UNASSIGN <gt_s4_role>.
      IF gr_container500 IS BOUND.
        CALL METHOD gr_container500->free.
        CLEAR: gr_container500, gr_table500.
      ENDIF.

      PERFORM read_role_validation.
      PERFORM get_texts.
      PERFORM prepare_output_role_validation.
      PERFORM display_classification_roles.
    ENDIF.
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    "run

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form user_validation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Validation by Users
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM user_validation.

  DATA: lt_sel_users TYPE gty_t_user_sel.

  CHECK lines( gt_rules_plain ) > 0.

  PERFORM get_users_for_validation USING gc_valid_type-user_validation
                                CHANGING lt_sel_users.
  IF lines( lt_sel_users ) EQ 0.
    MESSAGE TEXT-e01 TYPE 'S' DISPLAY LIKE 'I'.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  PERFORM prepare_data_user_validation USING lt_sel_users.

  IF lines( gt_user_data ) EQ 0.
    MESSAGE TEXT-e01 TYPE 'S' DISPLAY LIKE 'I'.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  PERFORM prepare_output_user_validation.

  IF p_save = 'X'. " Save the result to the cluster table
    PERFORM save_user_validation.
  ENDIF.

  IF p_trans = 'X'. " Transfer the user classifications to USR06
    PERFORM transfer_user_classifications.
  ENDIF.

  IF sy-batch = space.
    PERFORM display_classification_users.
  ENDIF.

  CLEAR lt_sel_users.

ENDFORM.                    "user_validation

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form prepare_data_users
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Prepare data for Validation by Users
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PT_SEL_USERS Users
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM prepare_data_user_validation USING pt_sel_users TYPE gty_t_user_sel.

  CLEAR: gt_user_data, gt_object_result, gt_role_result.

  PERFORM get_data_user_validation USING pt_sel_users.

  PERFORM get_texts.

  PERFORM validate_auth_objects.

  PERFORM validate_users USING pt_sel_users.

  PERFORM get_system_info.

ENDFORM.                    "prepare_data_user_validation

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form display_classif_users
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Display Users by selected Classification
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM display_classif_users .

  CALL SCREEN 0401.

ENDFORM.                    "display_classif_users

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form download_details
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Download the role details + included objects and their classification
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM download_details.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF tys_download,
           agr_name    TYPE agr_name,
           agr_text    TYPE agr_title,
           agr_classif TYPE text40,
           agr_ratio   TYPE char20,
           agr_objects TYPE i,
           agr_users   TYPE i,

           object      TYPE agobject,
           ttext       TYPE xutext,
           field       TYPE agrfield,
           low         TYPE agval,
           high        TYPE agval,
           classif_s4  TYPE text40,
         END OF tys_download.

  DATA: lt_download TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF tys_download,
        ls_download LIKE LINE OF lt_download.

  DATA: lr_selections TYPE REF TO cl_salv_selections,
        lt_rows       TYPE salv_t_row.

  DATA: lv_filename     TYPE string,
        lv_fullpath     TYPE string,
        lv_path         TYPE string,
        lv_action       TYPE i,
        lv_filesize     TYPE i,
        lv_file_name    TYPE string,
        lv_extension    TYPE string VALUE 'xml',
        lv_xstring      TYPE xstring,
        lt_download_bin TYPE solix_tab.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <lt_data>          TYPE STANDARD TABLE,
                 <ls_row>           LIKE LINE OF lt_rows,
                 <ls_record>        TYPE any,

                 <lv_role>          TYPE any,
                 <lv_classif_s4>    TYPE char40,
                 <lv_description>   TYPE agr_title,
                 <lv_users>         TYPE i,
                 <lv_objects>       TYPE i,
                 <lv_ratio>         TYPE char20,

                 <ls_download>      TYPE tys_download,
                 <ls_role_result>   LIKE LINE OF gt_role_result,
                 <ls_object_result> LIKE LINE OF gt_object_result,
                 <ls_object>        TYPE gty_object,
                 <ls_object_text>   LIKE LINE OF gt_object_text.

  " Get the list of selected rows from the table
  CASE sy-dynnr.
    WHEN 500.
      lr_selections = gr_table500->get_selections( ).
      ASSIGN <gt_s4_role> TO <lt_data>.
    WHEN 402.
      lr_selections = gr_table402->get_selections( ).
      ASSIGN <gt_role_classif> TO <lt_data>.
    WHEN OTHERS.
      RETURN.
  ENDCASE.

  " Get row numbers
  lt_rows = lr_selections->get_selected_rows( ).

  " Show error message if no roles have been selected
  IF lines( lt_rows ) = 0.
    MESSAGE TEXT-e10 TYPE 'I'.
    EXIT.
  ENDIF.

  LOOP AT lt_rows ASSIGNING <ls_row>.

    READ TABLE <lt_data> ASSIGNING <ls_record> INDEX <ls_row>.

    CHECK sy-subrc = 0.

    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'AGR_NAME'     OF STRUCTURE <ls_record> TO <lv_role>.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'CLASSIF_S4'   OF STRUCTURE <ls_record> TO <lv_classif_s4>.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'AGR_TEXT'     OF STRUCTURE <ls_record> TO <lv_description>.

    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'USER_NUMBERS' OF STRUCTURE <ls_record> TO <lv_users>.
    IF sy-subrc <> 0.
      ASSIGN COMPONENT 'TOTAL_USR'  OF STRUCTURE <ls_record> TO <lv_users>.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'RATIO'        OF STRUCTURE <ls_record> TO <lv_ratio>.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'OBJECT_COUNT' OF STRUCTURE <ls_record> TO <lv_objects>.

    IF <lv_role> IS ASSIGNED.

      APPEND INITIAL LINE TO lt_download ASSIGNING <ls_download>.
      <ls_download>-agr_name    = <lv_role>.
      <ls_download>-agr_text    = <lv_description>.
      <ls_download>-agr_classif = <lv_classif_s4>.
      <ls_download>-agr_ratio   = <lv_ratio>.
      <ls_download>-agr_objects = <lv_objects>.
      <ls_download>-agr_users   = <lv_users>.

      READ TABLE gt_role_result ASSIGNING <ls_role_result> WITH KEY agr_name = <lv_role>.
      IF sy-subrc = 0.
        LOOP AT <ls_role_result>-objects ASSIGNING <ls_object>.

          READ TABLE gt_object_result ASSIGNING <ls_object_result> INDEX <ls_object>-index_object.
          IF sy-subrc = 0 AND <ls_object_result>-classif_s4 <> TEXT-t07.
            CLEAR ls_download.
            ls_download-agr_name = <lv_role>.
            MOVE-CORRESPONDING <ls_object_result> TO ls_download.

            READ TABLE gt_object_text ASSIGNING <ls_object_text> WITH KEY object = <ls_object_result>-object.
            IF sy-subrc = 0.
              ls_download-ttext = <ls_object_text>-ttext.
            ENDIF.
            APPEND ls_download TO lt_download.
          ENDIF.
        ENDLOOP.

      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.

  ENDLOOP.

  CONCATENATE 'Roles_and_Objects_' sy-sysid '.xml' INTO lv_file_name.

  " Get filename
  CALL METHOD cl_gui_frontend_services=>file_save_dialog
    EXPORTING
      default_extension         = lv_extension
      default_file_name         = lv_file_name
    CHANGING
      filename                  = lv_filename
      path                      = lv_path
      fullpath                  = lv_fullpath
      user_action               = lv_action
    EXCEPTIONS
      cntl_error                = 1
      error_no_gui              = 2
      not_supported_by_gui      = 3
      invalid_default_file_name = 4
      OTHERS                    = 5.

  IF lv_action = cl_gui_frontend_services=>action_cancel OR sy-subrc <> 0.
    MESSAGE 'Action was cancelled' TYPE 'S'.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  " Convert internal table into XML format
  CALL TRANSFORMATION id SOURCE download = lt_download RESULT XML lv_xstring.
  lt_download_bin = cl_bcs_convert=>xstring_to_solix( iv_xstring = lv_xstring ).
  lv_filesize = xstrlen( lv_xstring ).

  " Download file
  CALL METHOD cl_gui_frontend_services=>gui_download
    EXPORTING
      filename                = lv_fullpath
      filetype                = 'BIN'
      bin_filesize            = lv_filesize
    CHANGING
      data_tab                = lt_download_bin
    EXCEPTIONS
      file_write_error        = 1
      no_batch                = 2
      gui_refuse_filetransfer = 3
      invalid_type            = 4
      no_authority            = 5
      unknown_error           = 6
      header_not_allowed      = 7
      separator_not_allowed   = 8
      filesize_not_allowed    = 9
      header_too_long         = 10
      dp_error_create         = 11
      dp_error_send           = 12
      dp_error_write          = 13
      unknown_dp_error        = 14
      access_denied           = 15
      dp_out_of_memory        = 16
      disk_full               = 17
      dp_timeout              = 18
      file_not_found          = 19
      dataprovider_exception  = 20
      control_flush_error     = 21
      not_supported_by_gui    = 22
      error_no_gui            = 23
      OTHERS                  = 24.

  IF sy-subrc <> 0.
    MESSAGE ID sy-msgid TYPE 'S' NUMBER sy-msgno
               WITH sy-msgv1 sy-msgv2 sy-msgv3 sy-msgv4
               DISPLAY LIKE 'E'.
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form save_user_validation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Save the user validation result to local cluster table
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM save_user_validation.

  DATA: lv_date        TYPE sy-datum,
        lv_time        TYPE sy-timlo,
        lv_objkey      LIKE slim_cluster-cluster_id,
        lv_objmdt      TYPE sy-mandt,
        lv_content(20) TYPE c,
        lv_ruleset     TYPE string,
        lv_header(80)  TYPE c,
        lv_dummy       TYPE c,
        lv_version     TYPE string,
        lv_lines       TYPE i.

  lv_date   = sy-datum. " Today
  lv_time   = sy-timlo. " Local Time
  lv_objmdt = sy-mandt.

  " Get the current Note Version
  PERFORM get_note_version USING gv_nvers.
  SPLIT gv_nvers AT ';' INTO gv_nvers lv_dummy.
  SHIFT gv_nvers LEFT DELETING LEADING '0'.
  CONCATENATE 'V' gv_nvers INTO lv_version.
  CONDENSE lv_version NO-GAPS.

  CLEAR gv_percent.
  " Saving User Validation
  PERFORM show_indicator USING TEXT-t32 gv_percent.

  " User Result
  CONCATENATE '2' lv_objmdt '_UV_Result_' lv_date '_' lv_time INTO lv_objkey.
  EXPORT gt_user_data TO DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.

  " Number of Users
  lv_lines = lines( gt_user_data ).
  WRITE lv_lines TO lv_content LEFT-JUSTIFIED NO-ZERO.
  IF lv_lines = 1.
    CONCATENATE lv_content ' User'  INTO lv_content.
  ELSE.
    CONCATENATE lv_content ' Users' INTO lv_content.
  ENDIF.

  " Ruleset
  CASE 'X'.
    WHEN p_pce.
      lv_ruleset = 'PCE Ruleset'.
    WHEN p_loc.
      lv_ruleset = p_locf.
    WHEN p_xls.
      TRY.
          " Get filename for message display
          CALL METHOD cl_bcs_utilities=>split_path
            EXPORTING
              iv_path = p_file
            IMPORTING
              ev_name = lv_ruleset.

        CATCH cx_bcs.
          lv_ruleset = 'STAR_Ruleset'.
      ENDTRY.
  ENDCASE.

  " Header Entry
  CONCATENATE sy-sysid sy-mandt 'U' lv_date lv_time sy-uname lv_ruleset lv_content lv_version INTO lv_header SEPARATED BY ';'.
  CONCATENATE '1' lv_objmdt '_UV_Result_' lv_date '_' lv_time INTO lv_objkey.
  EXPORT lv_header TO DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.

  " Role Result
  CONCATENATE '3' lv_objmdt '_UV_Result_' lv_date '_' lv_time INTO lv_objkey.
  EXPORT gt_role_result TO DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.

  " Object Result
  CONCATENATE '4' lv_objmdt '_UV_Result_' lv_date '_' lv_time INTO lv_objkey.
  EXPORT gt_object_result TO DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form save_role_validation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Save the role validation result to local cluster table
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM save_role_validation.

  DATA: lv_date        TYPE sy-datum,
        lv_time        TYPE sy-timlo,
        lv_objkey      LIKE slim_cluster-cluster_id,
        lv_objmdt      TYPE sy-mandt,
        lv_content(20) TYPE c,
        lv_ruleset     TYPE string,
        lv_header(80)  TYPE c,
        lv_dummy       TYPE c,
        lv_version     TYPE string,
        lv_lines       TYPE i.

  lv_date   = sy-datum. " Today
  lv_time   = sy-timlo. " Local Time
  lv_objmdt = sy-mandt.

  " Get the current Note Version
  PERFORM get_note_version USING gv_nvers.
  SPLIT gv_nvers AT ';' INTO gv_nvers lv_dummy.
  SHIFT gv_nvers LEFT DELETING LEADING '0'.
  CONCATENATE 'V' gv_nvers INTO lv_version.
  CONDENSE lv_version NO-GAPS.

  CLEAR gv_percent.
  " Saving User Validation
  PERFORM show_indicator USING TEXT-t32 gv_percent.

  " Role Data
  CONCATENATE '2' lv_objmdt '_RV_Result_' lv_date '_' lv_time INTO lv_objkey.
  EXPORT gt_role_data TO DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.

  " Number of Roles
  lv_lines = lines( gt_role_data ).
  WRITE lv_lines TO lv_content LEFT-JUSTIFIED NO-ZERO.
  IF lv_lines = 1.
    CONCATENATE lv_content ' Role'  INTO lv_content.
  ELSE.
    CONCATENATE lv_content ' Roles' INTO lv_content.
  ENDIF.

  " Ruleset
  CASE 'X'.
    WHEN p_pce.
      lv_ruleset = 'PCE Ruleset'.
    WHEN p_loc.
      lv_ruleset = p_locf.
    WHEN p_xls.
      TRY.
          " Get filename for message display
          CALL METHOD cl_bcs_utilities=>split_path
            EXPORTING
              iv_path = p_file
            IMPORTING
              ev_name = lv_ruleset.

        CATCH cx_bcs.
          lv_ruleset = 'STAR_Ruleset'.
      ENDTRY.
  ENDCASE.

  " Header Entry
  CONCATENATE sy-sysid sy-mandt 'R' lv_date lv_time sy-uname lv_ruleset lv_content lv_version INTO lv_header SEPARATED BY ';'.
  CONCATENATE '1' lv_objmdt '_RV_Result_' lv_date '_' lv_time INTO lv_objkey.
  EXPORT lv_header TO DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.

  " Role Result
  CONCATENATE '3' lv_objmdt '_RV_Result_' lv_date '_' lv_time INTO lv_objkey.
  EXPORT gt_role_result TO DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.

  " Object Result
  CONCATENATE '4' lv_objmdt '_RV_Result_' lv_date '_' lv_time INTO lv_objkey.
  EXPORT gt_object_result TO DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form read_user_validation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Read the user validation result from local cluster table
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM read_user_validation.

  DATA: lv_objkey     LIKE slim_cluster-cluster_id,
        lv_header(80) TYPE c,
        lv_dummy      TYPE c.

  CHECK p_locr IS NOT INITIAL.

  CLEAR gs_info.
  CLEAR gv_percent.
  " Reading User Validation
  PERFORM show_indicator USING TEXT-t33 gv_percent.

  " Header Entry
  CONCATENATE '1' p_locr INTO lv_objkey.
  IMPORT lv_header FROM DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.

  " User Result
  CONCATENATE '2' p_locr INTO lv_objkey.
  IMPORT gt_user_data FROM DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.

  " Role Result
  CONCATENATE '3' p_locr INTO lv_objkey.
  IMPORT gt_role_result FROM DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.

  " Object Result
  CONCATENATE '4' p_locr INTO lv_objkey.
  IMPORT gt_object_result FROM DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.

  " Check which ruleset has been used...
  SPLIT lv_header AT ';' INTO gs_info-sysid gs_info-client gs_info-type gs_info-date gs_info-time
                              gs_info-user gs_info-ruleset gs_info-content gs_info-version.

  " YI3;000;U;20240611;185001;ANZEIGER;PCE Ruleset;2.522 Users;V79

  IF gs_info-ruleset = 'PCE Ruleset'.
    p_pce = 'X'.
    gv_pce_mode = 'X'.
    p_loc = space.
    p_xls = space.
  ELSE.
    p_pce = space.
    gv_pce_mode = space.
    p_loc = 'X'.
    p_xls = space.
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form show_classif_totals
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Show Roles by selected Users
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PV_ROW Selected row
*&      --> PV_COLUMN Selected column
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM show_classif_totals  USING pv_row    TYPE salv_de_row
                                pv_column TYPE salv_de_column.

  DATA: lv_classif_curr TYPE char40,
        lv_uc_priority  TYPE numc4,
        lv_engine       TYPE boolean.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <lv_field> TYPE any.

  IF pv_row EQ 0.

    " Let the user click on a column total
    lv_classif_curr = 'All'.

  ELSE.

    READ TABLE <gt_total_classif_users> ASSIGNING <gs_total_classif_users> INDEX pv_row.
    IF <gs_total_classif_users> IS NOT ASSIGNED.
      RETURN.
    ENDIF.

    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'CLASSIF_CURR' OF STRUCTURE <gs_total_classif_users> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      lv_classif_curr = <lv_field>+3. " We need to cut off the user ID when navigating
    ENDIF.

  ENDIF.

  lv_uc_priority = pv_column.

  IF pv_column CS 'ENGI'.
    lv_engine = 'X'.
  ENDIF.

  PERFORM show_classif_total_users USING lv_classif_curr lv_uc_priority lv_engine pv_column.

ENDFORM.                    "show_classif_totals

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form read_role_validation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Read the role validation result from local cluster table
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM read_role_validation.

  DATA: lv_objkey  LIKE slim_cluster-cluster_id,
        lv_header(80) TYPE c,
        lv_ruleset    TYPE string.

  CHECK p_locr IS NOT INITIAL.

  CLEAR gs_info.
  CLEAR gv_percent.
  " Reading User Validation
  PERFORM show_indicator USING TEXT-t33 gv_percent.

  " Header Entry
  CONCATENATE '1' p_locr INTO lv_objkey.
  IMPORT lv_header FROM DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.

  " Role Data
  CONCATENATE '2' p_locr INTO lv_objkey.
  IMPORT gt_role_data FROM DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.

  " Role Result
  CONCATENATE '3' p_locr INTO lv_objkey.
  IMPORT gt_role_result FROM DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.

  " Object Result
  CONCATENATE '4' p_locr INTO lv_objkey.
  IMPORT gt_object_result FROM DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.

  " Check which ruleset has been used...
  SPLIT lv_header AT ';' INTO gs_info-sysid gs_info-client gs_info-type gs_info-date gs_info-time
                              gs_info-user gs_info-ruleset gs_info-content gs_info-version.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Display Roles by selected User
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM display_classif_roles .

  CALL SCREEN 0402.

ENDFORM.                    "display_classif_roles

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form show_classif_objects_user
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Show Authorization objects by selected Role (from User Validation)
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PV_ROW Selected row
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM show_classif_objects_user USING pv_row TYPE salv_de_row.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_app_comp,
           obj_name TYPE tadir-obj_name,
           ps_posid TYPE df14l-ps_posid,
           name     TYPE df14t-name,
         END OF lty_app_comp.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_tstca,
           object  TYPE tstca-objct,
           field   TYPE tstca-field,
           value   TYPE tstca-value,
           counter TYPE i,
         END OF lty_tstca.

  DATA: lt_app_comp TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF lty_app_comp,
        lt_tstca    TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF lty_tstca,
        lr_objects  TYPE RANGE OF tadir-obj_name,
        lr_object   LIKE LINE OF lr_objects,
        lv_counter  TYPE i.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_record>   TYPE any,
                 <lv_agr_name> TYPE any,
                 <lv_type>     TYPE any,
                 <ls_app_comp> LIKE LINE OF lt_app_comp.

  READ TABLE <gt_role_classif> ASSIGNING <ls_record> INDEX pv_row.
  IF sy-subrc <> 0.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  UNASSIGN: <lv_agr_name>, <lv_type>.

  ASSIGN COMPONENT 'AGR_NAME' OF STRUCTURE <ls_record> TO <lv_agr_name>.
  ASSIGN COMPONENT 'TYPE'     OF STRUCTURE <ls_record> TO <lv_type>.

  CLEAR gt_object_classif.

  CASE <lv_type>.
    WHEN gc_role_type-role.
      READ TABLE gt_role_result ASSIGNING <gs_role_result>
        WITH TABLE KEY agr_name = <lv_agr_name> " gs_role_classif>-agr_name
                       auth     = space. " <gs_role_classif>-auth.

    WHEN gc_role_type-profile.
      READ TABLE gt_role_result ASSIGNING <gs_role_result>
        WITH TABLE KEY agr_name = space " gs_role_classif>-agr_name
                       auth     = <lv_agr_name>. " <gs_role_classif>-auth.
  ENDCASE.

  IF sy-subrc EQ 0.

    " Collect authorization objects
    CLEAR lr_objects.
    LOOP AT <gs_role_result>-objects ASSIGNING <gs_objects>.
      lr_object-sign   = 'I'.
      lr_object-option = 'EQ'.
      lr_object-low    = <gs_objects>-object.
      APPEND lr_object TO lr_objects.
    ENDLOOP.

    TRY.

        " Collect the executable transactions
    SELECT objct field value COUNT(*) FROM tstca
             INTO TABLE lt_tstca
             WHERE objct IN lr_objects
               AND field = 'ACTVT'
             GROUP BY objct field value                  "#EC CI_BYPASS
             ORDER BY objct field value.

    " Read additional information, e.g. Application Component
    SELECT tadir~obj_name
           df14l~ps_posid
           df14t~name
           INTO TABLE lt_app_comp
           FROM tadir JOIN tdevc ON ( tadir~devclass = tdevc~devclass )
                      JOIN df14l ON ( tdevc~component = df14l~fctr_id )
                      JOIN df14t ON ( df14l~fctr_id = df14t~fctr_id ) "#EC CI_BUFFJOIN
           WHERE tadir~object = 'SUSO'
             AND tadir~obj_name IN lr_objects
             AND df14t~langu  = 'E'
           ORDER BY obj_name.

      CATCH cx_sy_open_sql_db.
        " Catch the exception in case there are too many objects in the role
        REFRESH: lt_tstca,
                 lt_app_comp.

    ENDTRY.

    LOOP AT <gs_role_result>-objects ASSIGNING <gs_objects>.
      APPEND INITIAL LINE TO gt_object_classif ASSIGNING <gs_object_classif>.
      MOVE-CORRESPONDING <gs_objects> TO <gs_object_classif>.

*      <gs_object_classif>-count = 1. " Counter for Totals / Subtotals

      READ TABLE gt_object_result ASSIGNING <gs_object_result>
        INDEX <gs_objects>-index_object.
      IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
        <gs_object_classif>-classif_s4     = <gs_object_result>-classif_s4.
        <gs_object_classif>-engine_classif = <gs_object_result>-engine_classif.
      ENDIF.

      PERFORM read_object_text USING <gs_object_classif>-object
                            CHANGING <gs_object_classif>-ttext.

      READ TABLE lt_app_comp ASSIGNING <ls_app_comp> WITH KEY obj_name = <gs_object_classif>-object BINARY SEARCH.
      IF sy-subrc = 0.
        CONCATENATE '(' <ls_app_comp>-name ')' INTO <gs_object_classif>-ps_posid.
        CONCATENATE <ls_app_comp>-ps_posid <gs_object_classif>-ps_posid INTO <gs_object_classif>-ps_posid SEPARATED BY space.
      ENDIF.

      CLEAR lv_counter.
      LOOP AT lt_tstca TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS
                       WHERE object = <gs_object_classif>-object
                         AND field  = <gs_object_classif>-field
                         AND value  CP <gs_object_classif>-low.

        ADD 1 TO lv_counter.
      ENDLOOP.

      IF lv_counter > 0.
        <gs_object_classif>-icon = '@3A\QTransactions@'.
      ENDIF.

    ENDLOOP.
  ENDIF.

  IF gt_object_classif[] IS INITIAL.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  " Add field and activity descriptions to the output table
  PERFORM add_descriptions TABLES gt_object_classif.

  " Header info for ALV
  CLEAR gv_title.
  CASE <lv_type>.
    WHEN gc_role_type-role.
      gv_title = TEXT-t19.
    WHEN gc_role_type-profile.
      gv_title = TEXT-t30.
  ENDCASE.
  REPLACE '&' IN gv_title WITH <lv_agr_name>.

  PERFORM display_classif_objects.

ENDFORM.                    "show_classif_objects_user

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form display_classif_objects
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Diplay Authorization objects by selected Role(from Role validation)
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM display_classif_objects .

  CALL SCREEN 0403.

ENDFORM.                    "display_classif_objects

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form get_table_components
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Table components
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PT_TABLE             Source table
*&      <-- CT_STRUCT_COMPONENTS Table components
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM get_table_components  USING    pt_table TYPE ANY TABLE
                           CHANGING ct_struct_components TYPE cl_abap_structdescr=>component_table.

  DATA: lo_table_descr  TYPE REF TO cl_abap_tabledescr,
        lo_struct_descr TYPE REF TO cl_abap_structdescr.

  CLEAR ct_struct_components.
  lo_table_descr ?= cl_abap_tabledescr=>describe_by_data( pt_table ).
  lo_struct_descr ?= lo_table_descr->get_table_line_type( ).

  ct_struct_components = lo_struct_descr->get_components( ).

ENDFORM.                    "get_table_components

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form f4_help_file
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Dialog for selection of (a) a ruleset or (b) a result file
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> CT_FILE File name
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM f4_help_file CHANGING cv_file TYPE text255.

  DATA: lv_filetype    TYPE string,
        lv_file_filter TYPE string,
        lt_files       TYPE filetable,
        lv_rc          TYPE i.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_file> TYPE file_table.

  IF gv_valid_type EQ gc_valid_type-previous_execution.
    lv_file_filter = 'All Files (*.*)|*.*|Text files (*.txt)|*.txt|Binary files (*.bin)|*.bin|ZIP archives (*.zip)|*.zip'. " ##NO_TEXT.
  ELSE.
    lv_filetype    = cl_gui_frontend_services=>filetype_excel.
    lv_file_filter = cl_gui_frontend_services=>filetype_excel.
  ENDIF.

  CALL METHOD cl_gui_frontend_services=>file_open_dialog
    EXPORTING
      default_extension = lv_filetype
      file_filter       = lv_file_filter
    CHANGING
      file_table        = lt_files
      rc                = lv_rc
    EXCEPTIONS
      OTHERS            = 1.

  IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
    READ TABLE lt_files ASSIGNING <ls_file> INDEX 1.
    IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
      cv_file =  <ls_file>-filename.
    ENDIF.
  ENDIF.

  CALL FUNCTION 'SAPGUI_SET_FUNCTIONCODE'
    EXPORTING
      functioncode           = 'ENTR'
    EXCEPTIONS
      function_not_supported = 0
      OTHERS                 = 0.

ENDFORM.                    "f4_help_file

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form role_validation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Validation by Roles
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM role_validation.

  CHECK lines( gt_rules_plain ) > 0.

  PERFORM prepare_data_role_validation.

  IF lines( gt_role_data ) = 0.
    MESSAGE TEXT-e01 TYPE 'S' DISPLAY LIKE 'I'.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  PERFORM prepare_output_role_validation.

  IF p_save = 'X'.
    PERFORM save_role_validation.
  ENDIF.

  IF sy-batch = space.
    PERFORM display_classification_roles.
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    "role_validation

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form prepare_data_role_validation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Prepare data for Validation by Roles
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM prepare_data_role_validation .

  DATA: lt_sel_users  TYPE gty_t_user_sel,
        lt_role_users TYPE gty_t_user_sel.

  CLEAR: gt_user_data, gt_object_result, gt_role_result, gt_role_data, gt_s4_role.

  PERFORM get_users_for_validation USING gc_valid_type-role_validation
                                CHANGING lt_sel_users.

  PERFORM get_data_role_validation USING lt_sel_users
                                CHANGING lt_role_users.

  PERFORM get_data_user_validation USING lt_role_users.

  PERFORM set_index_role_objects.

  PERFORM get_texts.

  PERFORM validate_auth_objects.

  PERFORM validate_users USING lt_sel_users.

  PERFORM validate_roles USING lt_sel_users.

  PERFORM get_system_info.

  CLEAR: lt_sel_users, lt_role_users.

ENDFORM.                    "prepare_data_role_validation

FORM display_classification_roles .

         gr_container500, gr_container501.

  CALL SCREEN 0500.

ENDFORM.                    "display_classification_roles

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form show_classif_objects_role
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Show Authorization objects by selected Role (from Role Validation)
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PV_ROW    Selected row
*&      --> PV_COLUMN Selected column
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM show_classif_objects_role  USING pv_row    TYPE salv_de_row
                                      pv_column TYPE salv_de_column.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_app_comp,
           obj_name TYPE tadir-obj_name,
           ps_posid TYPE df14l-ps_posid,
           name     TYPE df14t-name,
         END OF lty_app_comp.

  DATA: lt_app_comp TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF lty_app_comp,
        lr_objects  TYPE RANGE OF tadir-obj_name,
        lr_object   LIKE LINE OF lr_objects.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_record>   TYPE any,
                 <lv_agr_name> TYPE any,
                 <lv_type>     TYPE any,
                 <ls_app_comp> LIKE LINE OF lt_app_comp.

  CASE sy-dynnr.
    WHEN 500.
      READ TABLE <gt_s4_role> ASSIGNING <ls_record> INDEX pv_row.
    WHEN 402.
      READ TABLE <gt_role_classif> ASSIGNING <ls_record> INDEX pv_row.
  ENDCASE.

  IF NOT sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  UNASSIGN: <lv_agr_name>, <lv_type>.

  ASSIGN COMPONENT 'AGR_NAME' OF STRUCTURE <ls_record> TO <lv_agr_name>.
  ASSIGN COMPONENT 'TYPE'     OF STRUCTURE <ls_record> TO <lv_type>.

  CASE pv_column.

    WHEN 'AGR_NAME' OR 'AUTH'.

      CLEAR gt_object_classif.

      CASE <lv_type>.
        WHEN gc_role_type-role.
          READ TABLE gt_role_data ASSIGNING <gs_role_data>
             WITH TABLE KEY agr_name = <lv_agr_name>
                            auth     = space.
        WHEN gc_role_type-profile.
          READ TABLE gt_role_data ASSIGNING <gs_role_data>
             WITH TABLE KEY agr_name = space
                            auth     = <lv_agr_name>.
      ENDCASE.

      IF sy-subrc = 0.

        READ TABLE gt_role_result ASSIGNING <gs_role_result> INDEX <gs_role_data>-index_role.

        IF sy-subrc = 0.

          TRY.

              CLEAR lr_objects.
          LOOP AT <gs_role_result>-objects ASSIGNING <gs_objects>.
            lr_object-sign   = 'I'.
            lr_object-option = 'EQ'.
            lr_object-low    = <gs_objects>-object.
            APPEND lr_object TO lr_objects.
          ENDLOOP.

          " Read additional information, e.g. Application Component
          SELECT tadir~obj_name
                 df14l~ps_posid
                 df14t~name
                 INTO TABLE lt_app_comp
                 FROM tadir JOIN tdevc ON ( tadir~devclass = tdevc~devclass )
                            JOIN df14l ON ( tdevc~component = df14l~fctr_id )
                            JOIN df14t ON ( df14l~fctr_id = df14t~fctr_id ) "#EC CI_BUFFJOIN
                 WHERE tadir~object = 'SUSO'
                   AND tadir~obj_name IN lr_objects
                   AND df14t~langu  = 'E'
                 ORDER BY obj_name.

            CATCH cx_sy_open_sql_db.
              " Catch the exception in case there are too many objects in the role
              REFRESH: lt_app_comp.

          ENDTRY.

          " Collect the relevant entries
          LOOP AT <gs_role_result>-objects ASSIGNING <gs_objects>.
            APPEND INITIAL LINE TO gt_object_classif ASSIGNING <gs_object_classif>.
            MOVE-CORRESPONDING <gs_objects> TO <gs_object_classif>.

*            <gs_object_classif>-count = 1. " Column for Totals / Subtotals

            READ TABLE gt_object_result ASSIGNING <gs_object_result>
              INDEX <gs_objects>-index_object.
            IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
              <gs_object_classif>-classif_s4     = <gs_object_result>-classif_s4.
              <gs_object_classif>-engine_classif = <gs_object_result>-engine_classif.
            ENDIF.

            PERFORM read_object_text USING <gs_object_classif>-object
                                  CHANGING <gs_object_classif>-ttext.

            READ TABLE lt_app_comp ASSIGNING <ls_app_comp> WITH KEY obj_name = <gs_object_classif>-object BINARY SEARCH.
            IF sy-subrc = 0.
              CONCATENATE '(' <ls_app_comp>-name ')' INTO <gs_object_classif>-ps_posid.
              CONCATENATE <ls_app_comp>-ps_posid <gs_object_classif>-ps_posid INTO <gs_object_classif>-ps_posid SEPARATED BY space.
            ENDIF.

          ENDLOOP.
        ENDIF.
      ENDIF.

      IF gt_object_classif[] IS INITIAL.
        RETURN.
      ENDIF.

      " Add field and activity descriptions to the output table
      PERFORM add_descriptions TABLES gt_object_classif.

      " Header info for ALV
      CLEAR gv_title.
      CASE <lv_type>.
        WHEN gc_role_type-role.
          gv_title = TEXT-t19.
        WHEN gc_role_type-profile.
          gv_title = TEXT-t30.
      ENDCASE.

      REPLACE '&' IN gv_title WITH <lv_agr_name>.

      PERFORM display_classif_objects.

    WHEN 'TOTAL_USR'.

      CLEAR gt_role_users.

      LOOP AT gt_user_data ASSIGNING <gs_user_data> WHERE ustyp <> 'L'.

        CASE <lv_type>.
          WHEN gc_role_type-role.
            READ TABLE <gs_user_data>-roles WITH KEY agr_name = <lv_agr_name>
                                                     auth     = space
                                            TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS.
          WHEN gc_role_type-profile.
            READ TABLE <gs_user_data>-roles WITH KEY agr_name = space
                                                     auth     = <lv_agr_name>
                                            TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS.
        ENDCASE.

        IF sy-subrc = 0.
          APPEND INITIAL LINE TO gt_role_users ASSIGNING <gs_role_users>.
          MOVE-CORRESPONDING <gs_user_data> TO <gs_role_users>.

          PERFORM add_ratio_user_list USING    <gs_user_data>
                                      CHANGING <gs_role_users>-ratio.

        ENDIF.
      ENDLOOP.

      IF gt_role_users[] IS INITIAL.
        RETURN.
      ENDIF.

      " Header info for ALV
      CLEAR gv_title.
      gv_title = TEXT-t25.
      REPLACE '&' IN gv_title WITH <lv_agr_name>.

      PERFORM display_role_users.

    WHEN 'USER_NUMBERS'.

      CLEAR gt_role_users.

      CASE <lv_type>.
        WHEN gc_role_type-role.
          READ TABLE gt_role_data ASSIGNING <gs_role_data>
             WITH TABLE KEY agr_name = <lv_agr_name>
                            auth     = space.
        WHEN gc_role_type-profile.
          READ TABLE gt_role_data ASSIGNING <gs_role_data>
             WITH TABLE KEY agr_name = space
                            auth     = <lv_agr_name>.
      ENDCASE.

      IF sy-subrc EQ 0 AND <gs_role_data>-users IS NOT INITIAL.

        LOOP AT <gs_role_data>-users ASSIGNING <gs_users>.
          APPEND INITIAL LINE TO gt_role_users ASSIGNING <gs_role_users>.
          MOVE-CORRESPONDING <gs_users> TO <gs_role_users>.

          READ TABLE gt_user_data ASSIGNING <gs_user_data>
            WITH TABLE KEY bname = <gs_users>-bname.
          IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
            <gs_role_users>-classif_s4   = <gs_user_data>-classif_s4.
            <gs_role_users>-classif_curr = <gs_user_data>-classif_curr.

            PERFORM add_ratio_user_list USING    <gs_user_data>
                                        CHANGING <gs_role_users>-ratio.
          ENDIF.
          " when we run Role validation with Non evaluate Users gt_user_data is empty
          " and no user data in a downloaded file
          " so when we upload a Role validation file via Previous execution
          " and click on that ALV's "Users" column
          " Full name is empty on the next ALV screen
          " we could take a User name from the below table
          IF <gs_role_users>-name_text IS INITIAL.
            READ TABLE gt_hash_users ASSIGNING <gs_hash_users>
              WITH TABLE KEY bname COMPONENTS bname = <gs_users>-bname.
            IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
              <gs_role_users>-name_text = <gs_hash_users>-name_text.
            ENDIF.
          ENDIF.
        ENDLOOP.

      ENDIF.

      IF gt_role_users[] IS INITIAL.
        RETURN.
      ENDIF.

      " Header info for ALV
      CLEAR gv_title.
      gv_title = TEXT-t25.
      REPLACE '&' IN gv_title WITH <lv_agr_name>.

      PERFORM display_role_users.

  ENDCASE.

ENDFORM.                    "show_classif_objects_role

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form show_transactions
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Show transactions which can be executed with a certain object
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PV_ROW    Selected row
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM show_transactions USING pv_row TYPE salv_de_row.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF ty_transactions,
           tcode    TYPE tstca-tcode,
           ttext    TYPE tstct-ttext,
           objct    TYPE tstca-objct,
           field    TYPE tstca-field,
           value    TYPE tstca-value,
           ps_posid TYPE df14l-ps_posid,
           name     TYPE df14t-name,
           counter  TYPE i,
         END OF ty_transactions.

  DATA: lt_transactions TYPE TABLE OF ty_transactions,
        lt_fcat         TYPE slis_t_fieldcat_alv,
        ls_fcat         LIKE LINE OF lt_fcat,
        lv_title        TYPE sy-title,
        lv_string       TYPE string.

  DATA: lr_value TYPE RANGE OF tstca-value,
        ls_value LIKE LINE OF lr_value.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_object> LIKE LINE OF gt_object_classif.

  " Read the selected table row
  READ TABLE gt_object_classif ASSIGNING <ls_object> INDEX pv_row.
  IF sy-subrc = 0.

    lv_title = TEXT-t31.
    REPLACE '&1' WITH <ls_object>-object INTO lv_title.
    REPLACE '&2' WITH <ls_object>-field  INTO lv_title.
    IF <ls_object>-high IS NOT INITIAL.
      CONCATENATE <ls_object>-low <ls_object>-high INTO lv_string SEPARATED BY ' - '.
    ELSE.
      lv_string = <ls_object>-low.
    ENDIF.
    REPLACE '&3' WITH lv_string INTO lv_title.
    CONDENSE lv_title.

    IF <ls_object>-high IS NOT INITIAL.
      ls_value-sign   = 'I'.
      ls_value-option = 'BT'.
      ls_value-low    = <ls_object>-low.
      ls_value-high   = <ls_object>-high.
      APPEND ls_value TO lr_value.
    ELSEIF <ls_object>-low CS '*'.
      ls_value-sign   = 'I'.
      ls_value-option = 'CP'.
      ls_value-low    = <ls_object>-low.
      APPEND ls_value TO lr_value.
    ELSE.
      ls_value-sign   = 'I'.
      ls_value-option = 'EQ'.
      ls_value-low    = <ls_object>-low.
      APPEND ls_value TO lr_value.
    ENDIF.

    " Select the transactions from table TSTCA
    SELECT tstca~tcode
           tstct~ttext
           tstca~objct
           tstca~field
           tstca~value
           df14l~ps_posid
           df14t~name
           COUNT(*)
      INTO TABLE lt_transactions
      FROM tstca JOIN tstct ON ( tstca~tcode = tstct~tcode )
                 JOIN tadir ON ( tstca~tcode = tadir~obj_name )
                 JOIN tdevc ON ( tadir~devclass = tdevc~devclass )
                 JOIN df14l ON ( tdevc~component = df14l~fctr_id )
                 JOIN df14t ON ( df14l~fctr_id = df14t~fctr_id ) "#EC CI_BUFFJOIN
      WHERE tstca~objct = <ls_object>-object
        AND tstca~field = <ls_object>-field
        AND tstca~value IN lr_value
        AND tstct~sprsl  = 'E'
        AND df14t~langu  = 'E'
        AND tadir~object = 'TRAN'
      GROUP BY tstca~tcode tstct~ttext tstca~objct tstca~field tstca~value df14l~ps_posid df14t~name
      ORDER BY tstca~tcode tstca~objct tstca~field tstca~value.

    IF lines( lt_transactions ) = 0.
      MESSAGE s099(bv) WITH 'No transactions found'. " ##NO_TEXT.
      RETURN.
    ENDIF.

    " Output fields
    CLEAR ls_fcat.
    ls_fcat-col_pos   = 1.
    ls_fcat-tabname   = 'LT_TRANSACTIONS'.
    ls_fcat-fieldname = 'TCODE'.
    ls_fcat-seltext_l = 'Transaction'. "##NO_TEXT
    ls_fcat-outputlen = '20'.
    APPEND ls_fcat TO lt_fcat.
    CLEAR ls_fcat.
    ls_fcat-col_pos   = 2.
    ls_fcat-tabname   = 'LT_TRANSACTIONS'.
    ls_fcat-fieldname = 'TTEXT'.
    ls_fcat-seltext_l = 'Description'. "##NO_TEXT
    ls_fcat-outputlen = '35'.
    APPEND ls_fcat TO lt_fcat.
    CLEAR ls_fcat.
    ls_fcat-col_pos   = 3.
    ls_fcat-tabname   = 'LT_TRANSACTIONS'.
    ls_fcat-fieldname = 'OBJCT'.
    ls_fcat-seltext_l = 'Object'. "##NO_TEXT
    ls_fcat-outputlen = '10'.
    APPEND ls_fcat TO lt_fcat.
    CLEAR ls_fcat.
    ls_fcat-col_pos   = 4.
    ls_fcat-tabname   = 'LT_TRANSACTIONS'.
    ls_fcat-fieldname = 'FIELD'.
    ls_fcat-seltext_l = 'Field'. "##NO_TEXT
    ls_fcat-outputlen = '5'.
    APPEND ls_fcat TO lt_fcat.
    CLEAR ls_fcat.
    ls_fcat-col_pos   = 5.
    ls_fcat-tabname   = 'LT_TRANSACTIONS'.
    ls_fcat-fieldname = 'VALUE'.
    ls_fcat-seltext_l = 'Value'. "##NO_TEXT
    ls_fcat-outputlen = '5'.
    APPEND ls_fcat TO lt_fcat.
    CLEAR ls_fcat.
    ls_fcat-col_pos   = 6.
    ls_fcat-tabname   = 'LT_TRANSACTIONS'.
    ls_fcat-fieldname = 'PS_POSID'.
    ls_fcat-seltext_l = 'Appl. Component'."##NO_TEXT
    ls_fcat-outputlen = '24'.
    APPEND ls_fcat TO lt_fcat.
    CLEAR ls_fcat.
    ls_fcat-col_pos   = 7.
    ls_fcat-tabname   = 'LT_TRANSACTIONS'.
    ls_fcat-fieldname = 'NAME'.
    ls_fcat-seltext_l = 'Description'. "##NO_TEXT
    ls_fcat-outputlen = '50'.
    APPEND ls_fcat TO lt_fcat.

    CALL FUNCTION 'REUSE_ALV_POPUP_TO_SELECT'
      EXPORTING
        i_title               = lv_title
        i_selection           = ' '
        i_allow_no_selection  = 'X'
        i_screen_start_column = 1
        i_screen_start_line   = 1
        i_screen_end_column   = 150
        i_screen_end_line     = 25
        i_tabname             = 'LT_TRANSACTIONS'
        it_fieldcat           = lt_fcat
        i_callback_program    = sy-repid
        i_zebra               = 'X'
      TABLES
        t_outtab              = lt_transactions
      EXCEPTIONS
        OTHERS                = 0.

  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*

*& Show Users Classifications from Role validation ALV
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM simulate_users_role_validation .

  PERFORM prepare_output_user_validation.

  PERFORM display_classification_users.

ENDFORM.                    "simulate_users_role_validation

FORM add_ratio_user_list USING    is_user_data TYPE gty_user_data
                         CHANGING cv_ratio     TYPE char20.

  DATA: lv_lines    TYPE i,
        lv_count    TYPE i,
        lv_text(20) TYPE c.


  CLEAR: lv_count.
  " Total number of roles
  lv_lines = lines( is_user_data-roles ).
  IF lv_lines = 0.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  WRITE lv_lines TO cv_ratio LEFT-JUSTIFIED NO-ZERO.

  LOOP AT is_user_data-roles ASSIGNING <gs_user_role>
          WHERE classif_s4 = is_user_data-classif_s4.
    ADD 1 TO lv_count.
  ENDLOOP.

  IF lv_count = 0.
    lv_text = '0'.
  ELSE.
    WRITE lv_count TO lv_text LEFT-JUSTIFIED NO-ZERO.
  ENDIF.
  CONCATENATE lv_text '/' cv_ratio INTO cv_ratio.
  CONDENSE cv_ratio NO-GAPS.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form add_descriptions
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Add field and activity descriptions
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM add_descriptions TABLES ct_object_classif LIKE gt_object_classif.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_fields,
           field TYPE xufield,
           text  TYPE as4text,
         END OF lty_fields.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_tcodes,
           tcode TYPE tcode,
           ttext TYPE ttext_stct,
         END OF lty_tcodes.

  DATA: lr_tcd    TYPE RANGE OF tcode,
        ls_tcd    LIKE LINE OF lr_tcd,
        lt_tcodes TYPE SORTED TABLE OF lty_tcodes WITH UNIQUE KEY tcode,
        ls_tcode  LIKE LINE OF lt_tcodes.

  DATA: lr_fields TYPE RANGE OF authx-fieldname,
        ls_field  LIKE LINE OF lr_fields.

  DATA: ls_object_classif LIKE LINE OF gt_object_classif.

  DATA: lt_fields TYPE SORTED TABLE OF lty_fields WITH UNIQUE KEY field,
        ls_fields TYPE lty_fields.

  DATA: lt_tactt TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF tactt,
        ls_tactt LIKE LINE OF lt_tactt.


  "---------------------------------------------
  " TCODE Descriptions
  "---------------------------------------------
  LOOP AT ct_object_classif ASSIGNING <gs_object_classif> WHERE field CS 'TCD'.
    CLEAR ls_tcd.
    ls_tcd-sign   = 'I'.
    ls_tcd-option = 'EQ'.
    ls_tcd-low    = <gs_object_classif>-low.
    COLLECT ls_tcd INTO lr_tcd.
  ENDLOOP.

  " Read TCODE texts
  SELECT tcode ttext FROM tstct "#EC CI_BUFFJOIN "#EC CI_SGLSELECT
         INTO CORRESPONDING FIELDS OF TABLE lt_tcodes
         WHERE tcode IN lr_tcd
           AND sprsl = 'E'.

  " Update the descriptions in the output table
  LOOP AT lt_tcodes INTO ls_tcode.

    ls_object_classif-low_text  = ls_tcode-ttext.
    ls_object_classif-high_text = ls_tcode-ttext.
    MODIFY ct_object_classif FROM ls_object_classif TRANSPORTING low_text
           WHERE field CS 'TCD' AND low  = ls_tcode-tcode.

    MODIFY ct_object_classif FROM ls_object_classif TRANSPORTING high_text
           WHERE field CS 'TCD' AND high = ls_tcode-tcode.

  ENDLOOP.

  "---------------------------------------------
  " Field Descriptions
  "---------------------------------------------
  LOOP AT ct_object_classif ASSIGNING <gs_object_classif>.
    CLEAR ls_field.
    ls_field-sign   = 'I'.
    ls_field-option = 'EQ'.
    ls_field-low    = <gs_object_classif>-field.
    COLLECT ls_field INTO lr_fields.
  ENDLOOP.

  " Read descriptions
  SELECT authx~fieldname AS field
         dd04v~ddtext    AS text
         INTO TABLE lt_fields
         FROM authx JOIN dd04v ON ( authx~rollname = dd04v~rollname ) "#EC CI_BUFFJOIN
         WHERE authx~fieldname IN lr_fields
           AND dd04v~ddlanguage = 'E'.

  " Update the descriptions in the output table
  LOOP AT lt_fields INTO ls_fields.

    ls_object_classif-field_text = ls_fields-text.
    MODIFY ct_object_classif FROM ls_object_classif TRANSPORTING field_text
           WHERE field = ls_fields-field.

  ENDLOOP.

  "---------------------------------------------
  " Activity Descriptions
  "---------------------------------------------
  SELECT actvt ltext FROM tactt INTO CORRESPONDING FIELDS OF TABLE lt_tactt "#EC CI_BYPASS
         WHERE spras = 'E' ORDER BY actvt.

  ls_tactt-actvt = '*'.
  ls_tactt-ltext = 'ALL'.
  APPEND ls_tactt TO lt_tactt.

  " Update the descriptions in the output table
  LOOP AT lt_tactt INTO ls_tactt.

    ls_object_classif-low_text  = ls_tactt-ltext.
    ls_object_classif-high_text = ls_tactt-ltext.
    MODIFY ct_object_classif FROM ls_object_classif TRANSPORTING low_text  WHERE field = 'ACTVT' AND low  = ls_tactt-actvt.
    MODIFY ct_object_classif FROM ls_object_classif TRANSPORTING high_text WHERE field = 'ACTVT' AND high = ls_tactt-actvt.

  ENDLOOP.

  " Add missing "Not classified" for unconsidered entries
  ls_object_classif-classif_s4 = TEXT-t07.
  MODIFY ct_object_classif FROM ls_object_classif TRANSPORTING classif_s4 WHERE classif_s4 IS INITIAL.

  " Highlight incomplete entries
  ls_object_classif-low_text = '@02\QIncomplete@'.
  MODIFY ct_object_classif FROM ls_object_classif TRANSPORTING low_text WHERE low IS INITIAL.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form f4_help_locf
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Dialog for selection of a local ruleset
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM f4_help_locf USING    iv_field TYPE c
                  CHANGING cv_locf  TYPE text255.

  DATA: BEGIN OF lt_values OCCURS 0,
          cluster_id LIKE slim_cluster-cluster_id,
        END OF lt_values.

  DATA: lv_repid  LIKE sy-repid VALUE syst-repid,
        lt_fields TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF dfies,
        ls_field  LIKE LINE OF lt_fields,
        lt_return TYPE TABLE OF ddshretval.

  " Read available rulesets
  SELECT cluster_id FROM slim_cluster
         INTO TABLE lt_values
         WHERE relid   = 'ZM'
           AND version = 'R'
           AND srtf2        = 0
         ORDER BY cluster_id DESCENDING.

  PERFORM add_field TABLES lt_fields USING 'SLIM_CLUSTER' 'CLUSTER_ID' 'Ruleset' '1' '0'.

  " Show value help
  CALL FUNCTION 'F4IF_INT_TABLE_VALUE_REQUEST'
    EXPORTING
      retfield    = 'CLUSTER_ID'
      dynpprog    = sy-cprog
      dynpnr      = sy-dynnr
      dynprofield = iv_field
      value_org   = 'S'
    TABLES
      value_tab   = lt_values
      field_tab   = lt_fields
      return_tab  = lt_return
    EXCEPTIONS
      OTHERS      = 0.

ENDFORM.                    "f4_help_locf

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form f4_help_locr
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Dialog for selection of a local result
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM f4_help_locr CHANGING cv_locr TYPE text255.

  DATA: BEGIN OF lt_values OCCURS 0,
          cluster_id LIKE slim_cluster-cluster_id,
        END OF lt_values.

  DATA: BEGIN OF lt_result_sets OCCURS 0,
          mandt      TYPE sy-mandt,
          cluster_id LIKE slim_cluster-cluster_id,
          type       TYPE flag,
          date       TYPE tujob-start_date,
          time       TYPE tujob-start_time,
          ernam      TYPE xubname,
          ruleset    TYPE char30,
          content    TYPE char30,
          version    TYPE char8,
        END OF lt_result_sets.

  DATA: ls_data       LIKE LINE OF lt_result_sets,
        lt_return     TYPE TABLE OF ddshretval,
        lt_fields     TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF dfies,
        ls_field      LIKE LINE OF lt_fields,
        lv_objkey     LIKE slim_cluster-cluster_id,
        lv_header(80) TYPE c,
        lv_dummy      TYPE c.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_value> LIKE LINE OF lt_values.


  " Read available header entries
  SELECT DISTINCT cluster_id FROM slim_cluster
         INTO CORRESPONDING FIELDS OF TABLE lt_values
         WHERE relid   = 'ZM'
           AND version = '1'
           AND srtf2        = 0
         ORDER BY cluster_id DESCENDING.

  LOOP AT lt_values ASSIGNING <ls_value>.

    CLEAR ls_data.
    ls_data-cluster_id = <ls_value>-cluster_id.

    " Extract the header entry from the cluster table
    CONCATENATE '1' <ls_value>-cluster_id INTO lv_objkey.
    IMPORT lv_header FROM DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.

    " Put the data into the output structure
    SPLIT lv_header AT ';' INTO lv_dummy
                                ls_data-mandt
                                ls_data-type
                                ls_data-date
                                ls_data-time
                                ls_data-ernam
                                ls_data-ruleset
                                ls_data-content
                                ls_data-version.

    APPEND ls_data TO lt_result_sets.

  ENDLOOP.

  " Define the table headers
  PERFORM add_field TABLES lt_fields USING 'SYST'         'MANDT'      'Cl.'     '1' '0'.
  PERFORM add_field TABLES lt_fields USING 'SLIM_CLUSTER' 'CLUSTER_ID' 'Dataset' '1' '6'.
  PERFORM add_field TABLES lt_fields USING 'TUAPP'        'PERIOD'     'Type'    '2' '206'.
  PERFORM add_field TABLES lt_fields USING 'TUJOB'        'START_DATE' 'Date'    '3' '208'.
  PERFORM add_field TABLES lt_fields USING 'TUJOB'        'START_TIME' 'Time'    '4' '224'.
  PERFORM add_field TABLES lt_fields USING 'TUJOB'        'BNAME'      'User'    '5' '236'.
  PERFORM add_field TABLES lt_fields USING 'TUAPP'        'FUNC_MOD'   'Ruleset' '6' '260'.
  PERFORM add_field TABLES lt_fields USING 'TADIR'        'DEVCLASS'   'Content' '7' '320'.
  PERFORM add_field TABLES lt_fields USING 'TADIR'        'CPROJECT'   'Version' '8' '380'.

  " Show value help
  CALL FUNCTION 'F4IF_INT_TABLE_VALUE_REQUEST'
    EXPORTING
      retfield    = 'CLUSTER_ID'
      dynpprog    = sy-cprog
      dynpnr      = sy-dynnr
      dynprofield = 'P_LOCR'
      value_org   = 'S'
    TABLES
      value_tab   = lt_result_sets
      field_tab   = lt_fields
      return_tab  = lt_return
    EXCEPTIONS
      OTHERS      = 0.

ENDFORM.                    "f4_help_locr

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form get_users_for_validation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Get Users for Validation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PV_TYPE Type(User or Role validation)
*&      <-- CT_SEL_USERS Users
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM get_users_for_validation    USING pv_type      TYPE c
                              CHANGING ct_sel_users TYPE gty_t_user_sel.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_user_data,
           bname      TYPE xubname,
           name_first TYPE ad_namefir,
           name_last  TYPE ad_namelas,
         END OF lty_user_data.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_user_cls,
           bname    TYPE xubname,
           lic_type TYPE usertypen,
         END OF lty_user_cls.

  DATA: lt_refusers TYPE gty_t_refusers,
        lt_rbc      TYPE gty_t_rbc.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_refuser> LIKE LINE OF lt_refusers.

  DATA: lt_excl_user TYPE gty_t_excl_user,
        ls_sel_users TYPE gty_user,
        lv_init_date TYPE d,
        lt_user_cls  TYPE SORTED TABLE OF lty_user_cls  WITH UNIQUE KEY bname,
        lt_user_data TYPE SORTED TABLE OF lty_user_data WITH UNIQUE KEY bname.

  DATA: lr_user  TYPE RANGE OF usr02-bname,
        lr_ustyp TYPE RANGE OF usr02-ustyp,
        lr_ltype TYPE RANGE OF usr06-lic_type,
        ls_ltype LIKE LINE OF lr_ltype,
        lr_class TYPE RANGE OF usr02-class.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_excl_user> LIKE LINE OF lt_excl_user,
                 <ls_sel_users> TYPE gty_user,
                 <ls_user_cls>  TYPE lty_user_cls,
                 <ls_user_data> TYPE lty_user_data,
                 <ls_rbc>       LIKE LINE OF lt_rbc.

  IF pv_type = gc_valid_type-user_validation.
    lr_user[]  = so_user[].
    lr_ustyp[] = so_ustyp[].
    lr_ltype[] = so_ltype[].
    lr_class[] = so_class[].

    " If any user classification was entered, we need to make
    " sure to also select the unclassified users and check again
    " after adding possible classifications from reference users
    IF lr_ltype[] IS NOT INITIAL.
      ls_ltype-sign   = 'I'.
      ls_ltype-option = 'EQ'.
      ls_ltype-low    = '  '.
      APPEND ls_ltype TO lr_ltype.
    ENDIF.

  ENDIF.

  CLEAR ct_sel_users.

  SELECT  usr02~bname usr02~ustyp usr02~trdat usr02~class
    FROM  usr02
    INTO CORRESPONDING FIELDS OF TABLE ct_sel_users     "#EC CI_GENBUFF
    WHERE usr02~bname IN lr_user
      AND usr02~ustyp IN lr_ustyp
      AND usr02~class IN lr_class
      AND usr02~gltgv <= sy-datum
      AND ( usr02~gltgb >= sy-datum OR usr02~gltgb = lv_init_date )
      AND usr02~ustyp <> 'L'.

  " Get and remove excluded users
  PERFORM get_excl_user CHANGING lt_excl_user.

  LOOP AT lt_excl_user ASSIGNING <ls_excl_user>.
    DELETE ct_sel_users WHERE bname = <ls_excl_user>-bname.
  ENDLOOP.

  IF lines( ct_sel_users ) > 0.
    " Read classifications
    " --> doesn't work in the join since USR06 entries are only created if
    "     a manual classification exists. And when you select on that field
    "     the users will not be selected
    " And we select ALL classifications here to not leave the field blank
    " if user is classified
    SELECT bname lic_type
      FROM usr06                                        "#EC CI_GENBUFF
      INTO TABLE lt_user_cls
      FOR ALL ENTRIES IN ct_sel_users
      WHERE bname = ct_sel_users-bname.

    " Read Names
    SELECT usr21~bname adrp~name_first adrp~name_last
      FROM usr21 JOIN adrp ON usr21~persnumber = adrp~persnumber
      INTO TABLE lt_user_data
      FOR ALL ENTRIES IN ct_sel_users
      WHERE bname = ct_sel_users-bname
        AND adrp~date_from EQ gc_date_from
        AND adrp~nation    EQ space.

    " Get the reference user classifications
    PERFORM get_ref_user_classification   USING ct_sel_users lt_refusers.

    " Get role-based classification for users
    PERFORM get_role_based_classification USING ct_sel_users lt_rbc.

  ENDIF.

  " Include the Reference Users into the selection
  LOOP AT lt_refusers ASSIGNING <ls_refuser>.
    CLEAR ls_sel_users.
    ls_sel_users-bname = <ls_refuser>-refuser.
    ls_sel_users-ustyp = 'L'.
    INSERT ls_sel_users INTO TABLE ct_sel_users.
  ENDLOOP.

  LOOP AT ct_sel_users ASSIGNING <ls_sel_users>.

    " Classification
    READ TABLE lt_user_cls ASSIGNING <ls_user_cls>
               WITH KEY bname = <ls_sel_users>-bname
               BINARY SEARCH.

    IF sy-subrc = 0.
      <ls_sel_users>-lic_type = <ls_user_cls>-lic_type.
    ENDIF.

    " Name
    READ TABLE lt_user_data ASSIGNING <ls_user_data>
               WITH KEY bname = <ls_sel_users>-bname
               BINARY SEARCH.

    IF sy-subrc = 0.
      CONCATENATE <ls_user_data>-name_first <ls_user_data>-name_last
             INTO <ls_sel_users>-name_text SEPARATED BY space.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.

  " Take over the classification of the reference user only if the user
  " was not classified manually
  LOOP AT lt_refusers ASSIGNING <ls_refuser>. " WHERE lic_type IS NOT INITIAL.

    " We always need the Reference User
    ls_sel_users-refuser = <ls_refuser>-refuser.
    MODIFY ct_sel_users FROM ls_sel_users TRANSPORTING refuser
           WHERE bname = <ls_refuser>-bname.

    " We transfer the classification if the user was not classified otherwise yet
    IF <ls_refuser>-lic_type IS NOT INITIAL. " Classification of the Ref. user itself
      ls_sel_users-lic_type = <ls_refuser>-lic_type.
      MODIFY ct_sel_users FROM ls_sel_users TRANSPORTING lic_type
             WHERE bname = <ls_refuser>-bname
               AND lic_type IS INITIAL. " Current user classification
    ENDIF.

  ENDLOOP.

  " Role-based classification
  LOOP AT ct_sel_users ASSIGNING <ls_sel_users> WHERE lic_type IS INITIAL.
    READ TABLE lt_rbc ASSIGNING <ls_rbc> WITH KEY uname = <ls_sel_users>-bname BINARY SEARCH.
    IF sy-subrc = 0 AND <ls_rbc>-usertyp <> '##'.
      <ls_sel_users>-lic_type = <ls_rbc>-usertyp.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.

  " Now we remove classifications which haven't been selected
  DELETE ct_sel_users WHERE lic_type NOT IN so_ltype.

  CLEAR: lt_excl_user, lt_refusers, lt_rbc.

ENDFORM.                    "get_users_for_validation

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form get_texts
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Texts for Roles/Profiles/Objects
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM get_texts .

  DATA: lt_langu TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF tys_langu,
        ls_langu LIKE LINE OF lt_langu,
        lr_langu LIKE LINE OF gr_languages.

  CLEAR: gt_agr_text, gt_prof_text, gt_object_text, gt_tutyp, gr_languages.

  " Get preferred language(s)
  SELECT spras COUNT( * )              "#EC CI_BYPASS "#EC CI_SGLSELECT
         FROM agr_texts
         INTO TABLE lt_langu
         WHERE agr_texts~line = '00000'
         GROUP BY spras.

  SORT lt_langu BY counter DESCENDING.

  " We used the 2 frequently used languages...
  LOOP AT lt_langu INTO ls_langu.
    IF sy-tabix > 2.
      EXIT.
    ENDIF.
    lr_langu-sign   = 'I'.
    lr_langu-option = 'EQ'.
    lr_langu-low    = ls_langu-spras.
    COLLECT lr_langu INTO gr_languages.
  ENDLOOP.

  " ... and add the current logon language
  lr_langu-sign   = 'I'.
  lr_langu-option = 'EQ'.
  lr_langu-low    = sy-langu.
  COLLECT lr_langu INTO gr_languages.

  " --------------------------

  " Roles texts
  SELECT agr_name spras text
    FROM agr_texts                                      "#EC CI_GENBUFF
    INTO TABLE gt_agr_text
    FOR ALL ENTRIES IN gt_role_result
   WHERE agr_name = gt_role_result-agr_name
     AND spras IN gr_languages
     AND line = '00000'.

  SORT gt_agr_text BY agr_name spras.

  " Profiles texts
  SELECT profn langu ptext
    FROM usr11                                          "#EC CI_GENBUFF
    INTO TABLE gt_prof_text
    FOR ALL ENTRIES IN gt_role_result
   WHERE profn = gt_role_result-auth
     AND langu IN gr_languages
     AND aktps EQ 'A'.

  SORT gt_prof_text BY profn langu.

  " Objects texts
  SELECT object
         ttext
    FROM tobjt                                          "#EC CI_GENBUFF
      INTO TABLE gt_object_text
     WHERE langu EQ sy-langu.

  " User types
  SELECT *
    FROM tutyp                                          "#EC CI_GENBUFF
    INTO TABLE gt_tutyp
    WHERE langu EQ sy-langu
       OR langu EQ 'E'.

ENDFORM.                    "get_texts

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form read_role_text
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Role text
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PV_AGR_NAME Role
*&      <-- CV_AGR_TEXT Role text
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM read_role_text  USING    pv_agr_name TYPE agr_name
                     CHANGING cv_agr_text TYPE agr_title.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_agr_text> TYPE gty_agr_text.

  READ TABLE gt_agr_text ASSIGNING <ls_agr_text>
       WITH KEY agr_name = pv_agr_name
       BINARY SEARCH.

  IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
    cv_agr_text = <ls_agr_text>-text.
  ELSE.
    cv_agr_text = '<no description>'.
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    "read_role_text

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form read_prof_text
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Profile text
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PV_AUTH Profile
*&      <-- CV_TEXT Profile text
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM read_prof_text  USING    pv_auth  TYPE c " xuauth
                     CHANGING cv_ptext TYPE c. " xutext.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_prof_text> TYPE gty_prof_text.

  READ TABLE gt_prof_text ASSIGNING <ls_prof_text>
       WITH KEY profn = pv_auth
       BINARY SEARCH.

  IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
    cv_ptext = <ls_prof_text>-ptext.
  ELSE.
    cv_ptext = '<no description>'.
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    "read_prof_text

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form read_object_text
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Authorization Object text
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PV_OBJECT Object
*&      <-- CV_TTEXT  Object text
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM read_object_text  USING    pv_object TYPE agobject
                       CHANGING cv_ttext  TYPE xutext.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_object_text> TYPE gty_object_text.

  READ TABLE gt_object_text ASSIGNING <ls_object_text>
    WITH TABLE KEY object = pv_object.
  IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
    cv_ttext = <ls_object_text>-ttext.
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    "read_object_text

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form show_indicator
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Display progress indicator
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PV_TEXT     Text
*&      --> PV_PERCENT  Percent
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM show_indicator  USING    pv_text    TYPE string
                              pv_percent TYPE i.
  CALL FUNCTION 'SAPGUI_PROGRESS_INDICATOR'
    EXPORTING
      percentage = pv_percent
      text       = pv_text.

ENDFORM.                    "show_indicator

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form get_excl_user
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Get excluded users
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      <-- CT_EXCL_USER Excluded users
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM get_excl_user  CHANGING ct_excl_user TYPE gty_t_excl_user.

  CALL FUNCTION 'SLIM_EXCLUDE_USER'
    TABLES
      excl_user = ct_excl_user.
