  DELETE ct_excl_user WHERE client <> sy-mandt.

ENDFORM.                    "get_excl_user

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form display_role_users
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Diplay Users for selected Role/Profile
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM display_role_users.

  CALL SCREEN 0501.

ENDFORM.                    "display_role_users

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form get_data_user_validation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
**& Get data for User Validation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PT_SEL_USERS Users for validation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM get_data_user_validation  USING pt_sel_users TYPE gty_t_user_sel.

  DATA: lr_users TYPE RANGE OF usr02-bname.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_roles,
           agr_name TYPE agr_name,
           counter  TYPE i,
         END OF lty_roles.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_user_agrs,
           bname    TYPE xubname,
           agr_name TYPE agr_name,
           counter  TYPE i,
         END OF lty_user_agrs.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_user_auths,
           bname   TYPE xubname,
           auth    TYPE xuauth,
           counter TYPE i,
         END OF lty_user_auths.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_user_roles,
           user     TYPE xubname,
           agr_name TYPE gty_t_user_role,
         END OF lty_user_roles.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_user_profiles,
           user TYPE xubname,
           auth TYPE gty_t_user_role,
         END OF lty_user_profiles.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_incomplete,
           agr_name TYPE agr_name,
           object   TYPE agobject,
           auth     TYPE agauth,
           counter  TYPE i,
         END OF lty_incomplete.

  DATA: lt_agr_objects   TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF gty_roles,
        ls_role_result   TYPE gty_role,
        lt_user_agrs     TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF lty_user_agrs,
        lt_user_auths    TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF lty_user_auths,
        lt_incomplete    TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF lty_incomplete,
        lt_user_roles    TYPE SORTED TABLE OF lty_user_roles WITH UNIQUE KEY user,
        lt_user_profiles TYPE SORTED TABLE OF lty_user_profiles WITH UNIQUE KEY user,
        ls_user_roles    TYPE lty_user_roles,
        ls_user_profiles TYPE lty_user_profiles,
        ls_object        TYPE gty_object,
        ls_user_data     TYPE gty_user_data,
        ls_agr_name      TYPE gty_user_role,
        lt_profiles      TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF gty_profiles,
        ls_object_result TYPE gty_object_result,
        lv_index         TYPE sytabix,
        lv_lines         TYPE i,
        lv_text          TYPE string,
        lv_users         TYPE char10,
        lv_init_date     TYPE d,
        lv_auth          TYPE agauth.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_agr_objects>   TYPE gty_roles,
                 <ls_profiles>      TYPE gty_profiles,
                 <ls_sel_users>     LIKE LINE OF pt_sel_users,
                 <ls_user_agrs>     TYPE lty_user_agrs,
                 <ls_user_auths>    TYPE lty_user_auths,
                 <ls_user_roles>    TYPE lty_user_roles,
                 <ls_user_profiles> TYPE lty_user_profiles,
                 <lr_user>          LIKE LINE OF lr_users,
                 <ls_incomplete>    LIKE LINE OF lt_incomplete.

  IF pt_sel_users IS INITIAL.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  IF gv_valid_type = gc_valid_type-role_validation AND p_no_uv = 'X'.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  CLEAR gv_percent.
  " Preparing Data for User Validation...
  PERFORM show_indicator USING TEXT-t02 gv_percent.

  " Put the selected users into a range table for easier selection
  LOOP AT pt_sel_users ASSIGNING <ls_sel_users>.
    APPEND INITIAL LINE TO lr_users ASSIGNING <lr_user>.
    <lr_user>-sign   = 'I'.
    <lr_user>-option = 'EQ'.
    <lr_user>-low    = <ls_sel_users>-bname.
  ENDLOOP.

  IF lines( so_ustyp ) > 0.
    " Include Reference Users
    so_ustyp-sign   = 'I'.
    so_ustyp-option = 'EQ'.
    so_ustyp-low    = 'L'.
    APPEND so_ustyp.
  ENDIF.

  IF lines( so_user ) > 0.
    " Add Reference Users to the selection
    LOOP AT pt_sel_users ASSIGNING <ls_sel_users> WHERE ustyp = 'L'.
      so_user-sign   = 'I'.
      so_user-option = 'EQ'.
      so_user-low    = <ls_sel_users>-bname.
      APPEND so_user.
    ENDLOOP.
  ENDIF.

  TRY.
      " Get the ROLES per user for the selected users
      SELECT uname agr_name COUNT( * )                 "#EC CI_BUFFJOIN
             FROM agr_users JOIN usr02 ON agr_users~uname = usr02~bname
             INTO TABLE lt_user_agrs
             WHERE agr_users~uname    IN so_user
               AND agr_users~from_dat LE sy-datum
               AND agr_users~to_dat   GE sy-datum
               AND usr02~ustyp        IN so_ustyp
               AND usr02~class        IN so_class
               AND usr02~gltgv        <= sy-datum
               AND ( usr02~gltgb >= sy-datum OR usr02~gltgb = lv_init_date )
             " AND usr02~ustyp        <> 'L'
             GROUP BY uname agr_name
             ORDER BY uname agr_name.

      " Get Objects/Fields/Values from roles assigned to the selected users
      SELECT agr_1251~agr_name
             agr_1251~object
             agr_1251~auth
             agr_1251~field
             agr_1251~low
             agr_1251~high COUNT(*)
        INTO TABLE lt_agr_objects
        FROM agr_users
        INNER JOIN agr_1251 ON agr_1251~agr_name = agr_users~agr_name "#EC CI_BUFFJOIN
        INNER JOIN usr02 ON agr_users~uname = usr02~bname
       WHERE agr_users~uname  IN so_user " lr_users
          AND agr_users~from_dat LE sy-datum
          AND agr_users~to_dat   GE sy-datum
          AND usr02~ustyp        IN so_ustyp
          AND usr02~class        IN so_class
          AND usr02~gltgv     <= sy-datum
          AND ( usr02~gltgb >= sy-datum OR usr02~gltgb = lv_init_date )
          " AND usr02~ustyp     <> 'L'
         AND agr_1251~deleted EQ space
       GROUP BY agr_1251~agr_name agr_1251~object agr_1251~auth agr_1251~field agr_1251~low agr_1251~high
       ORDER BY agr_1251~agr_name agr_1251~object agr_1251~auth agr_1251~field agr_1251~low agr_1251~high.

    CATCH cx_sy_open_sql_db.

      lv_lines = lines( pt_sel_users ).
      WRITE lv_lines TO lv_users.
      lv_text = 'SQL too big for & users. Please split up the users.'.
      REPLACE '&' WITH lv_users INTO lv_text.
      CONDENSE lv_text.
      MESSAGE lv_text TYPE 'I'.
      RETURN.

  ENDTRY.

  " Add users who do not have any roles assigned
  LOOP AT pt_sel_users ASSIGNING <ls_sel_users>.
    READ TABLE lt_user_agrs WITH KEY bname = <ls_sel_users>-bname BINARY SEARCH TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS.
    IF sy-subrc <> 0.
      APPEND <ls_sel_users>-bname TO lt_user_agrs.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.

  SORT lt_user_agrs BY bname agr_name.

  " Collect incomplete entries
  SELECT agr_name object auth COUNT(*) FROM agr_1251    "#EC CI_GENBUFF
         INTO TABLE lt_incomplete
         WHERE agr_name IN so_role
           AND low      = ''
         GROUP BY agr_name auth object.                  "#EC CI_BYPASS

  " Ignore the authorization torso, the counter is sufficient
  LOOP AT lt_incomplete ASSIGNING <ls_incomplete>.
    CONCATENATE '__________' <ls_incomplete>-auth+10(2) INTO <ls_incomplete>-auth.
  ENDLOOP.

  SORT lt_incomplete BY agr_name auth object.

  " Remove the entire incomplete entry from the roles
  LOOP AT lt_agr_objects ASSIGNING <ls_agr_objects>.

    " Ignore the authorization torso, the counter is sufficient
    CONCATENATE '__________' <ls_agr_objects>-auth+10(2) INTO lv_auth.

    READ TABLE lt_incomplete WITH KEY agr_name = <ls_agr_objects>-agr_name
                                      auth     = lv_auth
                                      object   = <ls_agr_objects>-object
                                      BINARY SEARCH
                                      TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS.

    IF sy-subrc = 0.
      <ls_agr_objects>-incomplete = 'X'.
    ENDIF.

  ENDLOOP.

*  DELETE lt_agr_objects WHERE agr_name IS INITIAL.
  SORT lt_agr_objects BY agr_name object field low high.
  DELETE ADJACENT DUPLICATES FROM lt_agr_objects COMPARING agr_name object field low high.

  CLEAR: lt_incomplete.

  TRY.
      "--------------------------------------------------
      " SINGLE Profiles with Objects
      "--------------------------------------------------
      SELECT sprof~profn AS auth
             auth~objct  AS object
             auth~field
             auth~von    AS low
             auth~bis    AS high
             COUNT( * )
        FROM ust04  AS usr                             "#EC CI_BUFFJOIN
        JOIN usr02           ON usr~bname   = usr02~bname
        JOIN usr10  AS uprof ON uprof~profn = usr~profile
        JOIN ust10s AS sprof ON sprof~profn = usr~profile
        JOIN ust12  AS auth  ON auth~objct  = sprof~objct
                            AND auth~auth   = sprof~auth
        INTO TABLE lt_profiles
        WHERE usr~bname   IN so_user
          AND usr02~ustyp IN so_ustyp
          AND usr02~class IN so_class
          AND usr02~gltgv     <= sy-datum
          AND ( usr02~gltgb >= sy-datum OR usr02~gltgb = lv_init_date )
          AND uprof~aktps EQ gc_active
          AND uprof~typ   EQ gc_single
        GROUP BY sprof~profn auth~objct auth~field auth~von auth~bis
        ORDER BY sprof~profn auth~objct auth~field auth~von auth~bis.

      "--------------------------------------------------
      " COMPOSITE Profiles with Objects
      "--------------------------------------------------
      SELECT cprof~profn AS auth
             auth~objct  AS object
             auth~field
             auth~von    AS low
             auth~bis    AS high
             COUNT( * )
        FROM ust04  AS usr                             "#EC CI_BUFFJOIN
        JOIN usr02           ON usr~bname   = usr02~bname
        JOIN usr10  AS uprof ON uprof~profn = usr~profile
        JOIN ust10c AS cprof ON cprof~profn = usr~profile
        JOIN ust10s AS sprof ON sprof~profn = cprof~subprof
        JOIN ust12  AS auth  ON auth~objct  = sprof~objct
                            AND auth~auth   = sprof~auth
        APPENDING TABLE lt_profiles
        WHERE usr~bname   IN so_user
          AND usr02~ustyp IN so_ustyp
          AND usr02~class IN so_class
          AND usr02~gltgv     <= sy-datum
          AND ( usr02~gltgb >= sy-datum OR usr02~gltgb = lv_init_date )
          AND uprof~aktps EQ gc_active
          AND uprof~typ   EQ gc_composite
        GROUP BY cprof~profn auth~objct auth~field auth~von auth~bis
        ORDER BY cprof~profn auth~objct auth~field auth~von auth~bis.

      SORT lt_profiles BY auth object field low high.

      "--------------------------------------------------
      " SINGLE Profiles for Users
      "--------------------------------------------------
      SELECT usr~bname
             sprof~profn AS auth
             COUNT( * )
        FROM ust04  AS usr                             "#EC CI_BUFFJOIN
        JOIN usr02           ON usr~bname   = usr02~bname
        JOIN usr10  AS uprof ON uprof~profn = usr~profile
        JOIN ust10s AS sprof ON sprof~profn = usr~profile
        INTO TABLE lt_user_auths
        WHERE usr~bname   IN so_user
          AND usr02~ustyp IN so_ustyp
          AND usr02~class IN so_class
          AND usr02~gltgv     <= sy-datum
          AND ( usr02~gltgb >= sy-datum OR usr02~gltgb = lv_init_date )
          AND uprof~aktps EQ gc_active
          AND uprof~typ   EQ gc_single
        GROUP BY usr~bname sprof~profn
        ORDER BY usr~bname sprof~profn.

      "--------------------------------------------------
      " COMPOSITE Profiles for Users
      "--------------------------------------------------
      SELECT usr~bname
             cprof~profn AS auth
             COUNT( * )
        FROM ust04  AS usr                             "#EC CI_BUFFJOIN
        JOIN usr02           ON usr~bname   = usr02~bname
        JOIN usr10  AS uprof ON uprof~profn = usr~profile
        JOIN ust10c AS cprof ON cprof~profn = usr~profile
        APPENDING TABLE lt_user_auths
        WHERE usr~bname   IN so_user
          AND usr02~ustyp IN so_ustyp
          AND usr02~class IN so_class
          AND usr02~gltgv     <= sy-datum
          AND ( usr02~gltgb >= sy-datum OR usr02~gltgb = lv_init_date )
          AND uprof~aktps EQ gc_active
          AND uprof~typ   EQ gc_composite
        GROUP BY usr~bname cprof~profn
        ORDER BY usr~bname cprof~profn.

      SORT lt_user_auths BY bname auth.

    CATCH cx_sy_open_sql_db.

      lv_lines = lines( pt_sel_users ).
      WRITE lv_lines TO lv_users.
      lv_text = 'SQL too big for & users. Please split up the users.'.
      REPLACE '&' WITH lv_users INTO lv_text.
      CONDENSE lv_text.
      MESSAGE lv_text TYPE 'I'.
      RETURN.

  ENDTRY.

  " Collect all Objects
  LOOP AT lt_agr_objects ASSIGNING <ls_agr_objects>.
    CLEAR ls_object_result.
    MOVE-CORRESPONDING <ls_agr_objects> TO ls_object_result.
    INSERT ls_object_result INTO TABLE gt_object_result.
  ENDLOOP.

  LOOP AT lt_profiles ASSIGNING <ls_profiles>.
    CLEAR ls_object_result.
    MOVE-CORRESPONDING <ls_profiles> TO ls_object_result.
    INSERT ls_object_result INTO TABLE gt_object_result.
  ENDLOOP.

  " Now we have to classify the objects right away
  PERFORM validate_auth_objects.
  " Delete the unclassified objects (if selected on the selection screen)
  IF p_skip = 'X'.
    DELETE gt_object_result WHERE uc_priority = '9999'
                               OR uc_priority = '0000'.
  ENDIF.

  "---------------------------------------------
  " Prepare Objects for Roles
  "---------------------------------------------
  LOOP AT lt_agr_objects ASSIGNING <ls_agr_objects>.

    AT NEW agr_name.
      CLEAR ls_role_result.
      ls_role_result-agr_name = <ls_agr_objects>-agr_name.
    ENDAT.

    CLEAR lv_index.
    " We check whether the entry is still in the Object Result List
    " If not, we skip it
    " If yes, we need the table index as a reference
    READ TABLE gt_object_result TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS
      WITH TABLE KEY object = <ls_agr_objects>-object
                     field  = <ls_agr_objects>-field
                     low    = <ls_agr_objects>-low
                     high   = <ls_agr_objects>-high.

    IF sy-subrc = 0.

      lv_index = sy-tabix.
    CLEAR ls_object.
    MOVE-CORRESPONDING <ls_agr_objects> TO ls_object.
    ls_object-index_object = lv_index.
      INSERT ls_object INTO TABLE ls_role_result-objects.

    ENDIF.

    AT END OF agr_name.
      INSERT ls_role_result INTO TABLE gt_role_result.
      " Remove entries related to the current role to reduce the memory consumption
      " --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
      " Remark: Deleting lines of internal tables using DELETE does not usually release
      "         any memory in the internal table. Statements such as CLEAR or FREE must
      "         be used to release this memory.
      " --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
      " DELETE lt_agr_objects WHERE agr_name = ls_role_result-agr_name.
    ENDAT.

  ENDLOOP.

  CLEAR lt_agr_objects.

  "---------------------------------------------
  " Prepare Objects for Profiles
  "---------------------------------------------
  LOOP AT lt_profiles ASSIGNING <ls_profiles>.

    AT NEW auth.
      CLEAR ls_role_result.
      ls_role_result-auth = <ls_profiles>-auth.
    ENDAT.

    CLEAR lv_index.
    " We check whether the entry is still in the Object Result List
    " If not, we skip it
    " If yes, we need the table index as a reference
    READ TABLE gt_object_result TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS
      WITH TABLE KEY object = <ls_profiles>-object
                     field  = <ls_profiles>-field
                     low    = <ls_profiles>-low
                     high   = <ls_profiles>-high.

    IF sy-subrc = 0.

      lv_index = sy-tabix.
    CLEAR ls_object.
    MOVE-CORRESPONDING <ls_profiles> TO ls_object.
    ls_object-index_object = lv_index.
      INSERT ls_object INTO TABLE ls_role_result-objects.

    ENDIF.

    AT END OF auth.
      INSERT ls_role_result INTO TABLE gt_role_result.
      " Remove entries related to the current profile to reduce the memory consumption
      " See comment above
      " DELETE lt_profiles WHERE auth = ls_role_result-auth.
    ENDAT.
  ENDLOOP.

  CLEAR lt_profiles.

  "---------------------------------------------
  " Prepare Roles for Users
  "---------------------------------------------
  LOOP AT lt_user_agrs ASSIGNING <ls_user_agrs> WHERE bname IN lr_users.
    AT NEW bname.
      CLEAR: ls_user_roles.
      ls_user_roles-user = <ls_user_agrs>-bname.
    ENDAT.

    AT NEW agr_name.
      CLEAR lv_index.
      READ TABLE gt_role_result ASSIGNING <gs_role_result>
        WITH TABLE KEY agr_name = <ls_user_agrs>-agr_name
                       auth = space.
      IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
        lv_index = sy-tabix.
        CLEAR ls_agr_name.
        MOVE-CORRESPONDING <gs_role_result> TO ls_agr_name.
        ls_agr_name-index_role = lv_index.
        INSERT ls_agr_name INTO TABLE ls_user_roles-agr_name.
      ENDIF.
    ENDAT.

    AT END OF bname.
      INSERT ls_user_roles INTO TABLE lt_user_roles.
      " Remove entries related to the current user to reduce the memory consumption
      " See comment above
      " DELETE lt_user_agrs WHERE bname = ls_user_roles-user.
    ENDAT.
  ENDLOOP.

  CLEAR lt_user_agrs.

  "---------------------------------------------
  " Prepare Profiles for Users
  "---------------------------------------------
  LOOP AT lt_user_auths ASSIGNING <ls_user_auths> WHERE bname IN lr_users.
    AT NEW bname.
      CLEAR: ls_user_profiles.
      ls_user_profiles-user = <ls_user_auths>-bname.
    ENDAT.

    AT NEW auth.
      CLEAR lv_index.
      READ TABLE gt_role_result ASSIGNING <gs_role_result>
        WITH TABLE KEY agr_name = space
                       auth = <ls_user_auths>-auth.
      IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
        lv_index = sy-tabix.
        CLEAR ls_agr_name.
        MOVE-CORRESPONDING <gs_role_result> TO ls_agr_name.
        ls_agr_name-index_role = lv_index.
        INSERT ls_agr_name INTO TABLE ls_user_profiles-auth.
      ENDIF.
    ENDAT.

    AT END OF bname.
      INSERT ls_user_profiles INTO TABLE lt_user_profiles.
      " Remove entries related to the current user to reduce the memory consumption
      " See comment above
      " DELETE lt_user_auths WHERE bname = ls_user_profiles-user.
    ENDAT.
  ENDLOOP.

  CLEAR lt_user_auths.
  CLEAR lr_users.

  "----------------------------------------------------
  " Prepare final data for Users
  "----------------------------------------------------
  " (1) Roles
  LOOP AT lt_user_roles ASSIGNING <ls_user_roles>.
    CLEAR ls_user_data.
    ls_user_data-bname = <ls_user_roles>-user.
    ls_user_data-roles = <ls_user_roles>-agr_name.
    INSERT ls_user_data INTO TABLE gt_user_data.
  ENDLOOP.

  " (2) Profiles
  LOOP AT lt_user_profiles ASSIGNING <ls_user_profiles>.
    READ TABLE gt_user_data ASSIGNING <gs_user_data>
      WITH TABLE KEY bname = <ls_user_profiles>-user.
    IF sy-subrc <> 0. " User not yet available
      CLEAR ls_user_data.
      ls_user_data-bname = <ls_user_profiles>-user.
      ls_user_data-roles = <ls_user_profiles>-auth.
      INSERT ls_user_data INTO TABLE gt_user_data.
    ELSE. " Add profiles to existing user entry
      INSERT LINES OF <ls_user_profiles>-auth INTO TABLE <gs_user_data>-roles.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.

  CLEAR: lt_agr_objects, lt_user_agrs, lt_profiles,
         lt_user_auths, lt_user_roles, lt_user_profiles.

ENDFORM.                    "get_data_user_validation

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form prepare_output_user_validation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Prepare output data for User validation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM prepare_output_user_validation .

  DATA: ls_s4_user             TYPE gty_s4_user,
        lt_field_cat           TYPE lvc_t_fcat,
        lv_component           TYPE name_feld,
        lt_total_classif_users TYPE REF TO data,
        lr_total_classif_users TYPE REF TO data,
        lt_classif_s4_fields   TYPE gty_t_classif_s4_fields.

  DATA: sort_tab  TYPE abap_sortorder_tab,
        sort_line TYPE abap_sortorder.

  DATA: lr_pce   TYPE RANGE OF usertypen,
        ls_pce   LIKE LINE OF lr_pce,
        ft_color TYPE lvc_t_scol, " slis_t_specialcol_alv.
        fs_color LIKE LINE OF ft_color. "fs_cell TYPE slis_specialcol_alv,

  DATA: lv_classif_curr TYPE string,
        lv_found        TYPE flag.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <lv_total>   TYPE any,
                 <lv_counter> TYPE any,
                 <lv_field>   TYPE any,
                 <ls_entry>   TYPE any.


  CLEAR: gt_s4_user, gt_classif_s4_fields.

  CLEAR gv_percent.
  " Preparing output...
  PERFORM show_indicator USING TEXT-t06 gv_percent.

  " Prepare data for main ALV
  LOOP AT gt_user_data ASSIGNING <gs_user_data> WHERE ustyp <> 'L'.
    CLEAR ls_s4_user.
    ls_s4_user-classif_s4   = <gs_user_data>-classif_s4.
    ls_s4_user-uc_priority  = <gs_user_data>-uc_priority.
    ls_s4_user-user_numbers = 1.

    IF <gs_user_data>-engine = 'X'.
      ls_s4_user-user_engines = 1.
    ENDIF.

    COLLECT ls_s4_user INTO gt_s4_user.
  ENDLOOP.

  SORT gt_s4_user BY uc_priority.
  " Prepare columns of output table
  LOOP AT gt_user_data ASSIGNING <gs_user_data> WHERE ustyp <> 'L'.
    " Classification columns
    IF   <gs_user_data>-uc_priority NE gc_not_classif OR
      " Not classified column only if no Engines
       ( <gs_user_data>-uc_priority EQ gc_not_classif AND <gs_user_data>-engine EQ abap_false ).
      APPEND INITIAL LINE TO gt_classif_s4_fields ASSIGNING <gs_classif_s4_fields>.
      <gs_classif_s4_fields>-fname       = <gs_user_data>-uc_priority.
      <gs_classif_s4_fields>-text        = <gs_user_data>-classif_s4.
      <gs_classif_s4_fields>-header_text = <gs_user_data>-classif_s4.
    ENDIF.

    IF <gs_user_data>-engine IS NOT INITIAL.
      " Engine columns
      APPEND INITIAL LINE TO gt_classif_s4_fields ASSIGNING <gs_classif_s4_fields>.
      CONCATENATE <gs_user_data>-uc_priority 'ENGI' INTO <gs_classif_s4_fields>-fname.
      IF <gs_user_data>-uc_priority NE gc_not_classif.
        <gs_classif_s4_fields>-text  = TEXT-a14.
        CONCATENATE <gs_user_data>-classif_s4 TEXT-a16
          INTO <gs_classif_s4_fields>-header_text SEPARATED BY space.
      ELSE.
        " if Not classified-but there are Engines-Engine only column
        <gs_classif_s4_fields>-text        = TEXT-a15.
        <gs_classif_s4_fields>-header_text = TEXT-a15.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.

  ENDLOOP.

  SORT gt_classif_s4_fields BY fname.
  DELETE ADJACENT DUPLICATES FROM gt_classif_s4_fields COMPARING fname.

  APPEND INITIAL LINE TO lt_classif_s4_fields ASSIGNING <gs_classif_s4_fields>.
  <gs_classif_s4_fields>-fname       = 'TOTAL'.
  <gs_classif_s4_fields>-text        = TEXT-a04.
  <gs_classif_s4_fields>-header_text = TEXT-a04.

  APPEND LINES OF gt_classif_s4_fields TO lt_classif_s4_fields.
  CLEAR gt_classif_s4_fields.
  gt_classif_s4_fields = lt_classif_s4_fields.

  PERFORM prepare_output_fields CHANGING lt_total_classif_users.

  ASSIGN lt_total_classif_users->* TO <gt_total_classif_users>.
  CREATE DATA lr_total_classif_users LIKE LINE OF <gt_total_classif_users>.
  ASSIGN lr_total_classif_users->* TO <gs_total_classif_users>.

  " Count Totals over Users in output format (exclude the Reference Users)
  LOOP AT gt_user_data ASSIGNING <gs_user_data> WHERE ustyp <> 'L'.

    CLEAR <gs_total_classif_users>.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'CLASSIF_CURR' OF STRUCTURE <gs_total_classif_users> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      " Show ID + Description
      CONCATENATE <gs_user_data>-lic_type <gs_user_data>-classif_curr
             INTO <lv_field> SEPARATED BY space RESPECTING BLANKS.
      " Store the current classification
      lv_classif_curr = <lv_field>.
    ENDIF.

    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'TOTAL' OF STRUCTURE <gs_total_classif_users> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = 1.
    ENDIF.
    " S/4 classification columns
    IF <gs_user_data>-uc_priority NE gc_not_classif OR
    " below condition is for Not classified column
   ( <gs_user_data>-uc_priority EQ gc_not_classif AND
     <gs_user_data>-engine EQ abap_false ).
      lv_component = <gs_user_data>-uc_priority.
      ASSIGN COMPONENT lv_component OF STRUCTURE <gs_total_classif_users> TO <lv_field>.
      IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
        <lv_field> = 1.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.

    IF  <gs_user_data>-engine = 'X'.
      " Thereof engine use columns for S/4 classification columns
      " Engine only column is there as well
      CONCATENATE <gs_user_data>-uc_priority 'ENGI' INTO lv_component.
      ASSIGN COMPONENT lv_component OF STRUCTURE <gs_total_classif_users> TO <lv_field>.
      IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
        <lv_field> = 1.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.

    CLEAR lv_found.

    IF p_pce = space.
      " If we are not "PCE mode", we can do a regular COLLECT
      COLLECT <gs_total_classif_users> INTO <gt_total_classif_users>.
    ELSE.
      " ... otherwise we cannot do a COLLECT due to the data structure
      LOOP AT <gt_total_classif_users> ASSIGNING <ls_entry>.
        ASSIGN COMPONENT 'CLASSIF_CURR' OF STRUCTURE <ls_entry> TO <lv_field>.
        IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED AND <lv_field> = lv_classif_curr. " from current classification above
          " We already have a line for the current user classification
          lv_found = 'X'.
          " Collect the data into the table
          LOOP AT lt_classif_s4_fields ASSIGNING <gs_classif_s4_fields>.
            ASSIGN COMPONENT <gs_classif_s4_fields>-fname OF STRUCTURE <ls_entry> TO <lv_total>.
            ASSIGN COMPONENT <gs_classif_s4_fields>-fname OF STRUCTURE <gs_total_classif_users> TO <lv_counter>.
            <lv_total> = <lv_total> + <lv_counter>.
          ENDLOOP.
        ENDIF.
      ENDLOOP.

      IF lv_found = space. " Add a new line for the new user type
        APPEND <gs_total_classif_users> TO <gt_total_classif_users>.
      ENDIF.

    ENDIF.

  ENDLOOP.

  IF p_pce = 'X'.

    CLEAR ls_pce.

    " Relevant PCE User Types
    SELECT usertyp FROM tutyppl INTO ls_pce-low WHERE pricelist = '06'.
      ls_pce-sign   = 'I'.
      ls_pce-option = 'EQ'.
      APPEND ls_pce TO lr_pce.
    ENDSELECT.

    IF lines( lr_pce ) > 0.
      " Coloring scheme
      fs_color-fname     = 'CLASSIF_CURR'.
      fs_color-color-col = 6.
      APPEND fs_color TO ft_color.

      " Highlight the entries with inconsistent classification
      LOOP AT <gt_total_classif_users> ASSIGNING <gs_total_classif_users>.

        ASSIGN COMPONENT 'CLASSIF_CURR' OF STRUCTURE <gs_total_classif_users> TO <lv_field>.
        IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED AND <lv_field>(2) NOT IN lr_pce. " No PCE User Type
          " Set the pre-defined coloring
          ASSIGN COMPONENT 'COLOR' OF STRUCTURE <gs_total_classif_users> TO <lv_field>.
          IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
            <lv_field> = ft_color.
          ENDIF.
        ENDIF.

      ENDLOOP.
    ENDIF.
  ENDIF.

  REFRESH sort_tab.
  sort_line-name   = 'CLASSIF_CURR'.
  sort_line-astext = 'X'.
  APPEND sort_line TO sort_tab.

  SORT <gt_total_classif_users> BY (sort_tab).

ENDFORM.                    "prepare_output_user_validation

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form prepare_output_role_validation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Prepare output data for Role validation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM prepare_output_role_validation.

  DATA: lt_field_cat    TYPE lvc_t_fcat,
        lv_component    TYPE name_feld,
        lt_s4_role      TYPE REF TO data,
        lr_s4_role      TYPE REF TO data,
        ls_role_classif TYPE gty_role_classif.

  DATA: sort_tab  TYPE abap_sortorder_tab,
        sort_line TYPE abap_sortorder.

  DATA: ls_agr_flag  LIKE LINE OF gt_agr_flags.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <lv_field>   TYPE any,
                 <ls_s4_role> TYPE any.

  CLEAR gv_percent.
  " Preparing output...
  PERFORM show_indicator USING TEXT-t06 gv_percent.

  REFRESH gt_agr_flags.

  " Read role classifications
  IF lines( gt_role_data ) > 0.
    SELECT a~agr_name a~flag_value b~utyptext
           INTO CORRESPONDING FIELDS OF TABLE gt_agr_flags
           FROM agr_flags AS a INNER JOIN tutyp AS b   "#EC CI_BUFFJOIN
           ON a~flag_value = b~usertyp
           FOR ALL ENTRIES IN gt_role_data
           WHERE a~agr_name = gt_role_data-agr_name
           AND a~flag_type = 'LICENSE_01'
           AND b~langu     = 'E'.
  ENDIF.

  " Roles
  LOOP AT gt_role_data ASSIGNING <gs_role_data> WHERE agr_name IS NOT INITIAL.

    APPEND INITIAL LINE TO gt_s4_role ASSIGNING <gs_s4_role>.
    <gs_s4_role>-type       = gc_role_type-role.
    <gs_s4_role>-agr_name   = <gs_role_data>-agr_name.
    <gs_s4_role>-classif_s4 = <gs_role_data>-classif_s4.

    " Current role classification
    READ TABLE gt_agr_flags INTO ls_agr_flag
         WITH KEY agr_name = <gs_role_data>-agr_name
         BINARY SEARCH.
    IF sy-subrc = 0.
      CONCATENATE ls_agr_flag-flag_value ls_agr_flag-utyptext
             INTO <gs_s4_role>-classif_curr SEPARATED BY space.
    ENDIF.

    " Number of assigned users
    <gs_s4_role>-user_numbers = lines( <gs_role_data>-users ).

    " Role description
    PERFORM read_role_text USING <gs_s4_role>-agr_name
                        CHANGING <gs_s4_role>-agr_text.

    " Total number of objects and the target classification ratio
    CLEAR ls_role_classif.
    MOVE-CORRESPONDING <gs_s4_role> TO ls_role_classif.
    PERFORM add_ratio_role CHANGING ls_role_classif.
    <gs_s4_role>-ratio        = ls_role_classif-ratio.
    <gs_s4_role>-object_count = ls_role_classif-object_count.

    " Engines for Roles
    PERFORM add_role_engines USING <gs_role_data>-agr_name <gs_role_data>-auth <gs_role_data>-index_role.

  ENDLOOP.

  " Profiles
  LOOP AT gt_role_data ASSIGNING <gs_role_data> WHERE auth IS NOT INITIAL.

    APPEND INITIAL LINE TO gt_s4_role ASSIGNING <gs_s4_role>.
    <gs_s4_role>-type         = gc_role_type-profile.
    <gs_s4_role>-agr_name     = <gs_role_data>-auth.
    <gs_s4_role>-classif_s4   = <gs_role_data>-classif_s4.
    <gs_s4_role>-user_numbers = lines( <gs_role_data>-users ).

    " Profile description
    PERFORM read_prof_text USING <gs_s4_role>-agr_name
                        CHANGING <gs_s4_role>-agr_text.


    " Total number of objects and the target classification ratio
    CLEAR ls_role_classif.
    MOVE-CORRESPONDING <gs_s4_role> TO ls_role_classif.
    PERFORM add_ratio_role CHANGING ls_role_classif.
    <gs_s4_role>-ratio        = ls_role_classif-ratio.
    <gs_s4_role>-object_count = ls_role_classif-object_count.

    " Engines for Roles
    PERFORM add_role_engines USING <gs_role_data>-auth <gs_role_data>-agr_name <gs_role_data>-index_role.

  ENDLOOP.

  " Create a dynamic table for Role validation ALV
  PERFORM prepare_role_classif_fields USING gc_valid_type-role_validation CHANGING lt_field_cat.

  CALL METHOD cl_alv_table_create=>create_dynamic_table
    EXPORTING
      it_fieldcatalog           = lt_field_cat
    IMPORTING
      ep_table                  = lt_s4_role
    EXCEPTIONS
      generate_subpool_dir_full = 1
      OTHERS                    = 2.

  IF sy-subrc = 0.
    ASSIGN lt_s4_role->* TO <gt_s4_role>.

    CREATE DATA lr_s4_role LIKE LINE OF <gt_s4_role>.
    ASSIGN lr_s4_role->* TO <ls_s4_role>.
  ENDIF.

  " Prepare data for Role validation ALV
  LOOP AT gt_s4_role ASSIGNING <gs_s4_role>.

    CLEAR <ls_s4_role>.

    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'AGR_NAME' OF STRUCTURE <ls_s4_role> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_s4_role>-agr_name.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'AGR_TEXT' OF STRUCTURE <ls_s4_role> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_s4_role>-agr_text.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'TYPE' OF STRUCTURE <ls_s4_role> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_s4_role>-type.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'CLASSIF_CURR' OF STRUCTURE <ls_s4_role> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_s4_role>-classif_curr.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'CLASSIF_S4' OF STRUCTURE <ls_s4_role> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_s4_role>-classif_s4.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'USER_NUMBERS' OF STRUCTURE <ls_s4_role> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_s4_role>-user_numbers.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'RATIO' OF STRUCTURE <ls_s4_role> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_s4_role>-ratio.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'OBJECT_COUNT' OF STRUCTURE <ls_s4_role> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_s4_role>-object_count.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'COUNT' OF STRUCTURE <ls_s4_role> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = 1.
    ENDIF.

    " Engine columns
    LOOP AT gt_role_engines ASSIGNING <gs_role_engines> WHERE agr_name EQ <gs_s4_role>-agr_name.
      lv_component = <gs_role_engines>-engine_priority.
      ASSIGN COMPONENT lv_component OF STRUCTURE <ls_s4_role> TO <lv_field>.
      IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
        <lv_field> = 1.
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.

    APPEND <ls_s4_role> TO <gt_s4_role>.

  ENDLOOP.

  " Sort the output table by number of assigned users descending
  REFRESH sort_tab.
  sort_line-name       = 'USER_NUMBERS'.
  sort_line-descending = 'X'.
  APPEND sort_line TO sort_tab.

  SORT <gt_s4_role> BY (sort_tab).

ENDFORM.                    "prepare_output_role_validation

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form get_data_role_validation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
**& Get data for Role Validation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PT_SEL_USERS       Users
*&      <-- CT_SEL_USERS_ROLE  Users from Roles
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM get_data_role_validation  USING pt_sel_users      TYPE gty_t_user_sel
                            CHANGING ct_sel_users_role TYPE gty_t_user_sel.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_agr_users,
           agr_name TYPE agr_name,
           bname    TYPE xubname,
           counter  TYPE i,
         END OF lty_agr_users.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_auth_users,
           auth  TYPE xuauth,
           bname TYPE xubname,
           counter TYPE i,
         END OF lty_auth_users.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_role_users,
           agr_name TYPE agr_name,
           users    TYPE gty_t_role_user,
         END OF lty_role_users.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_profile_users,
           auth  TYPE xuauth,
           users TYPE gty_t_role_user,
         END OF lty_profile_users.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_incomplete,
           agr_name TYPE agr_name,
           object   TYPE agobject,
           auth     TYPE agauth,
           counter  TYPE i,
         END OF lty_incomplete.

  DATA: lt_roles          TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF gty_roles,
        lt_agr_users      TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF lty_agr_users,
        lt_auth_users     TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF lty_auth_users,
        lt_incomplete     TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF lty_incomplete,
        lt_role_users     TYPE SORTED TABLE OF lty_role_users  WITH UNIQUE KEY agr_name,
        lt_profile_users  TYPE SORTED TABLE OF lty_profile_users  WITH UNIQUE KEY auth,
        ls_role_users     TYPE lty_role_users,
        ls_profile_users  TYPE lty_profile_users,
        ls_object_result  TYPE gty_object_result,
        ls_sel_users_role TYPE gty_user,
        ls_user           TYPE gty_role_user,
        ls_role_data      TYPE gty_role_data,
        ls_role_result    TYPE gty_role,
        ls_object         TYPE gty_object,
        lt_profiles       TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF gty_profiles,
        lv_include        TYPE boolean,
        lv_index          TYPE sytabix,
        lv_init_date      TYPE d,
        lv_auth           TYPE agauth.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_agr_users>     TYPE lty_agr_users,
                 <ls_auth_users>    TYPE lty_auth_users,
                 <ls_roles>         TYPE gty_roles,
                 <ls_role_users>    TYPE lty_role_users,
                 <ls_user>          TYPE gty_role_user,
                 <ls_profiles>      TYPE gty_profiles,
                 <ls_profile_users> TYPE lty_profile_users,
                 <ls_incomplete>    LIKE LINE OF lt_incomplete.

  CLEAR ct_sel_users_role.

  CLEAR gv_percent.
  " Preparing Data for Role Validation...
  PERFORM show_indicator USING TEXT-t08 gv_percent.

  IF p_role EQ 'X'.

    IF p_empty = space.
      " Read the ASSIGNED ROLES with the included objects as per the selection
      SELECT agr_1251~agr_name agr_1251~object agr_1251~auth agr_1251~field agr_1251~low agr_1251~high COUNT(*)
             FROM agr_1251 "#EC CI_BYPASS "#EC CI_GENBUFF "#EC CI_BUFFJOIN
                  JOIN agr_users ON agr_1251~agr_name = agr_users~agr_name
                  JOIN usr02     ON agr_users~uname   = usr02~bname
             INTO TABLE lt_roles
            WHERE agr_1251~agr_name  IN so_role
              AND agr_1251~deleted   EQ space
              AND agr_users~from_dat LE sy-datum
              AND agr_users~to_dat   GE sy-datum
              AND usr02~gltgv        <= sy-datum
              AND ( usr02~gltgb >= sy-datum OR usr02~gltgb = lv_init_date )
            GROUP BY agr_1251~agr_name agr_1251~object agr_1251~auth agr_1251~field agr_1251~low agr_1251~high.
    ELSE.
      " Read the ALL ROLES with the included objects as per the selection
      SELECT agr_1251~agr_name agr_1251~object agr_1251~auth agr_1251~field agr_1251~low agr_1251~high COUNT(*)
             FROM agr_1251               "#EC CI_BYPASS "#EC CI_GENBUFF
             INTO TABLE lt_roles
            WHERE agr_1251~agr_name  IN so_role
              AND agr_1251~deleted   EQ space
            GROUP BY agr_1251~agr_name agr_1251~object agr_1251~auth agr_1251~field agr_1251~low agr_1251~high.
    ENDIF.

    IF lines( lt_roles ) > 0.
      " Select the corresponding users for the Roles selected above
      SELECT agr_name uname COUNT(*)
             FROM agr_users              "#EC CI_BYPASS "#EC CI_GENBUFF
             INTO TABLE lt_agr_users
             WHERE agr_name IN so_role
               AND from_dat <= sy-datum
               AND to_dat   >= sy-datum
             GROUP BY agr_name uname
             ORDER BY agr_name uname.
    ENDIF.

  ENDIF.

  " Read the incomplete entries from the selected roles
  SELECT agr_name object auth COUNT(*)
         FROM agr_1251                   "#EC CI_BYPASS "#EC CI_GENBUFF
         INTO TABLE lt_incomplete
         WHERE agr_name IN so_role
           AND low      = ''
         GROUP BY agr_name auth object.

  " Ignore the authorization torso, the counter is sufficient
  LOOP AT lt_incomplete ASSIGNING <ls_incomplete>.
    CONCATENATE '__________' <ls_incomplete>-auth+10(2) INTO <ls_incomplete>-auth.
  ENDLOOP.

  SORT lt_incomplete BY agr_name auth object.

  IF p_profn = 'X'.
    " Profiles with Objects
    SELECT sprof~profn AS auth
           auth~objct  AS object
           auth~field
           auth~von    AS low
           auth~bis    AS high
           COUNT(*)
     FROM usr10    AS uprof                            "#EC CI_BUFFJOIN
      JOIN ust10s AS sprof ON sprof~profn = uprof~profn
      JOIN ust12  AS auth  ON auth~objct  = sprof~objct
                          AND auth~auth   = sprof~auth
      INTO TABLE lt_profiles
   WHERE uprof~profn IN so_profn
     AND uprof~aktps EQ gc_active
     AND uprof~typ   EQ gc_single
     GROUP BY sprof~profn auth~objct auth~field auth~von auth~bis
     ORDER BY sprof~profn auth~objct auth~field auth~von auth~bis.

    "-------------------------------------------------
    " COMPOSITE Profiles with Objects
    "-------------------------------------------------
    SELECT cprof~profn AS auth
           auth~objct  AS object
           auth~field
           auth~von    AS low
           auth~bis    AS high
           COUNT(*)
      FROM usr10  AS uprof                             "#EC CI_BUFFJOIN
      JOIN ust10c AS cprof ON cprof~profn = uprof~profn
      JOIN ust10s AS sprof ON sprof~profn = cprof~subprof
      JOIN ust12  AS auth  ON auth~objct  = sprof~objct
                          AND auth~auth   = sprof~auth
      APPENDING TABLE lt_profiles
   WHERE uprof~profn IN so_profn
     AND uprof~aktps EQ gc_active
     AND uprof~typ   EQ gc_composite
     GROUP BY cprof~profn auth~objct auth~field auth~von auth~bis
     ORDER BY cprof~profn auth~objct auth~field auth~von auth~bis.

    IF sy-subrc = 0.
      " Users for Profiles
      SELECT sprof~profn AS auth
             usr~bname
             COUNT( * )
      FROM ust04  AS usr                               "#EC CI_BUFFJOIN
        JOIN usr02           ON usr~bname   = usr02~bname
        JOIN usr10  AS uprof ON uprof~profn = usr~profile
        JOIN ust10s AS sprof ON sprof~profn = usr~profile
*        JOIN ust12  AS auth  ON auth~objct  = sprof~objct
*                            AND auth~auth   = sprof~auth
          INTO TABLE lt_auth_users
       WHERE usr~bname   IN so_user
         AND usr02~ustyp IN so_ustyp
         AND usr02~class IN so_class
         AND usr02~gltgv     <= sy-datum
         AND ( usr02~gltgb >= sy-datum OR usr02~gltgb = lv_init_date )
         AND usr~profile IN so_profn
         AND uprof~aktps EQ gc_active
         AND uprof~typ   EQ gc_single
       GROUP BY usr~bname sprof~profn
       ORDER BY usr~bname sprof~profn.

      " Users for COMPOSITE Profiles
      SELECT cprof~profn AS auth
             usr~bname
             COUNT( * )
      FROM ust04  AS usr                               "#EC CI_BUFFJOIN
        JOIN usr02           ON usr~bname   = usr02~bname
        JOIN usr10  AS uprof ON uprof~profn = usr~profile
        JOIN ust10c AS cprof ON cprof~profn = usr~profile
          APPENDING TABLE lt_auth_users
       WHERE usr~bname   IN so_user
         AND usr02~ustyp IN so_ustyp
         AND usr02~class IN so_class
         AND usr02~gltgv     <= sy-datum
         AND ( usr02~gltgb >= sy-datum OR usr02~gltgb = lv_init_date )
         AND usr~profile IN so_profn
         AND uprof~aktps EQ gc_active
         AND uprof~typ   EQ gc_composite
       GROUP BY usr~bname cprof~profn
       ORDER BY usr~bname cprof~profn.

    ENDIF.

  ENDIF.

  " Remove the incomplete entries from the role data
  LOOP AT lt_roles ASSIGNING <ls_roles>.

    " Ignore the authorization torso, the counter is sufficient
    CONCATENATE '__________' <ls_roles>-auth+10(2) INTO lv_auth.

    READ TABLE lt_incomplete WITH KEY agr_name = <ls_roles>-agr_name
                                      auth     = lv_auth
                                      object   = <ls_roles>-object
                                      BINARY SEARCH
                                      TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS.
    IF sy-subrc = 0.
      <ls_roles>-incomplete = 'X'.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.

*  DELETE lt_roles WHERE agr_name IS INITIAL.
  SORT lt_roles BY agr_name object field low high.
  DELETE ADJACENT DUPLICATES FROM lt_roles COMPARING agr_name object field low high.

  " Users for Roles
  LOOP AT lt_agr_users ASSIGNING <ls_agr_users>.

    AT NEW agr_name.
      CLEAR: ls_role_users.
      ls_role_users-agr_name = <ls_agr_users>-agr_name.
    ENDAT.

    " Check Reference User
    READ TABLE pt_sel_users WITH KEY bname = <ls_agr_users>-bname ustyp = 'L' TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS.
    IF sy-subrc <> 0.
      " Regular User: Insert the user itself
      ls_user-bname = <ls_agr_users>-bname.
      INSERT ls_user INTO TABLE ls_role_users-users.
    ELSE.
      " Reference User: Add the users from which the Ref. User is referenced
      LOOP AT pt_sel_users ASSIGNING <gs_sel_users> WHERE refuser = <ls_agr_users>-bname.
        ls_user-bname = <gs_sel_users>-bname.
        INSERT ls_user INTO TABLE ls_role_users-users.
      ENDLOOP.
    ENDIF.

    AT END OF agr_name.
      INSERT ls_role_users INTO TABLE lt_role_users.
    ENDAT.

  ENDLOOP.

  " Users for Profiles
  LOOP AT lt_auth_users ASSIGNING <ls_auth_users>.
    AT NEW auth.
      CLEAR: ls_profile_users.
      ls_profile_users-auth = <ls_auth_users>-auth.
    ENDAT.

    " Check Reference User
    READ TABLE pt_sel_users WITH KEY bname = <ls_auth_users>-bname ustyp = 'L' TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS.
    IF sy-subrc <> 0.
      " Regular User: Insert the user itself
      ls_user-bname = <ls_auth_users>-bname.
      INSERT ls_user INTO TABLE ls_profile_users-users.
    ELSE.
      " Reference User: Add the users from which the Ref. User is referenced
      LOOP AT pt_sel_users ASSIGNING <gs_sel_users> WHERE refuser = <ls_auth_users>-bname.
        ls_user-bname = <gs_sel_users>-bname.
        INSERT ls_user INTO TABLE ls_profile_users-users.
      ENDLOOP.
    ENDIF.

    AT END OF auth.
      INSERT ls_profile_users INTO TABLE lt_profile_users.
    ENDAT.
  ENDLOOP.

  " Collect all Objects
  LOOP AT lt_roles ASSIGNING <ls_roles>.
    CLEAR ls_object_result.
    MOVE-CORRESPONDING <ls_roles> TO ls_object_result.
    INSERT ls_object_result INTO TABLE gt_object_result.
  ENDLOOP.

  LOOP AT lt_profiles ASSIGNING <ls_profiles>.
    CLEAR ls_object_result.
    MOVE-CORRESPONDING <ls_profiles> TO ls_object_result.
    INSERT ls_object_result INTO TABLE gt_object_result.
  ENDLOOP.

  " Now we have to classify the objects right away
  PERFORM validate_auth_objects.
  IF p_skip = 'X'.
    DELETE gt_object_result WHERE uc_priority = '9999'
                               OR uc_priority = '0000'.
  ENDIF.

  " Prepare final data for Roles
  LOOP AT lt_roles ASSIGNING <ls_roles>.

    AT NEW agr_name.
      lv_include = 'X'.
      CLEAR: ls_role_data, ls_role_result.

      ls_role_data-agr_name = <ls_roles>-agr_name.
      READ TABLE lt_role_users ASSIGNING <ls_role_users>
        WITH TABLE KEY agr_name = <ls_roles>-agr_name.
      IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
        ls_role_data-users = <ls_role_users>-users.

        LOOP AT ls_role_data-users ASSIGNING <ls_user>.
          ls_sel_users_role-bname = <ls_user>-bname.
          INSERT ls_sel_users_role INTO TABLE ct_sel_users_role.
        ENDLOOP.
      ELSE.
        IF p_empty IS INITIAL. " not show not assigned Roles
          CLEAR lv_include.
        ENDIF.
      ENDIF.
    ENDAT.

    IF lv_include EQ 'X'.

      READ TABLE gt_object_result TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS
           WITH TABLE KEY object = <ls_roles>-object
                          field  = <ls_roles>-field
                          low    = <ls_roles>-low
                          high   = <ls_roles>-high.

      IF sy-subrc = 0.

        lv_index = sy-tabix.
        CLEAR ls_object.
        MOVE-CORRESPONDING <ls_roles> TO ls_object.
        ls_object-index_object = lv_index.
        INSERT ls_object INTO TABLE ls_role_result-objects.

      ENDIF.

    ENDIF.

    AT END OF agr_name.
      IF lv_include EQ 'X'.
        INSERT ls_role_data INTO TABLE gt_role_data.

        MOVE-CORRESPONDING ls_role_data TO ls_role_result.
        INSERT ls_role_result INTO TABLE gt_role_result.
      ENDIF.
    ENDAT.

  ENDLOOP.

  " Prepare final data for Profiles
  LOOP AT lt_profiles ASSIGNING <ls_profiles>.

    AT NEW auth.
      lv_include = 'X'.
      CLEAR: ls_role_data, ls_role_result.

      ls_role_data-auth = <ls_profiles>-auth.
      READ TABLE lt_profile_users ASSIGNING <ls_profile_users>
        WITH TABLE KEY auth = <ls_profiles>-auth.
      IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
        ls_role_data-users = <ls_profile_users>-users.

        LOOP AT ls_role_data-users ASSIGNING <ls_user>.
          ls_sel_users_role-bname = <ls_user>-bname.
          INSERT ls_sel_users_role INTO TABLE ct_sel_users_role.
        ENDLOOP.
      ELSE.
        IF p_empty IS INITIAL. " not show not assigned Profiles
          CLEAR lv_include.
        ENDIF.
      ENDIF.
    ENDAT.

    IF lv_include EQ 'X'.

      READ TABLE gt_object_result TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS
           WITH TABLE KEY object = <ls_profiles>-object
                          field  = <ls_profiles>-field
                          low    = <ls_profiles>-low
                          high   = <ls_profiles>-high.

      IF sy-subrc = 0.

        lv_index = sy-tabix.
        CLEAR ls_object.
        MOVE-CORRESPONDING <ls_profiles> TO ls_object.
        ls_object-index_object = lv_index.
        INSERT ls_object INTO TABLE ls_role_result-objects.

      ENDIF.

    ENDIF.

    AT END OF auth.
      IF lv_include EQ 'X'.
        INSERT ls_role_data INTO TABLE gt_role_data.

        MOVE-CORRESPONDING ls_role_data TO ls_role_result.
        INSERT ls_role_result INTO TABLE gt_role_result.
      ENDIF.
    ENDAT.

  ENDLOOP.

  CLEAR: lt_profiles, lt_roles, lt_auth_users, lt_incomplete,
         lt_profile_users, lt_agr_users, lt_role_users.

ENDFORM.                    "get_data_role_validation

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form validate_objects
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Validate Authorization Objects
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM validate_auth_objects.

  DATA: lt_role_result TYPE gty_t_result.

  DATA: lr_objects TYPE RANGE OF xuobject,
        ls_object  LIKE LINE OF lr_objects,
        lr_fields  TYPE RANGE OF xufield,
        ls_field   LIKE LINE OF lr_fields.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_rules_plain> LIKE LINE OF gt_rules_plain,
                 <ls_result>      TYPE gty_result.

  " Classification of all authorization objects

  CLEAR gv_percent.
  " Validation of Authorization Objects...
  PERFORM show_indicator USING TEXT-t03 gv_percent.

  " Collect all relevant objects and fields to reduce the
  " the number of loops to the necessary minimum.
  LOOP AT gt_rules_plain ASSIGNING <ls_rules_plain>.

    ls_object-low    = <ls_rules_plain>-objct.
    ls_object-sign   = 'I'.
    IF ls_object-low CS '*'.
      ls_object-option = 'CP'.
    ELSE.
      ls_object-option = 'EQ'.
    ENDIF.
    COLLECT ls_object INTO lr_objects.

    ls_field-low    = <ls_rules_plain>-field.
    ls_field-sign   = 'I'.
    IF ls_field-low CS '*'.
      ls_field-option = 'CP'.
    ELSE.
      ls_field-option = 'EQ'.
    ENDIF.
    COLLECT ls_field INTO lr_fields.

  ENDLOOP.

  " Just loop over the necessary entries
  LOOP AT gt_object_result ASSIGNING <gs_object_result> WHERE object IN lr_objects
                                                          AND field  IN lr_fields.

    " Rules
    " Split check in AUTH and ENGI. AUTH can be stopped after first hit.
    " ------------------------------------------------------------
    " (1) Use Types via type AUTH
    " ------------------------------------------------------------
    LOOP AT gt_rules_plain ASSIGNING <gs_rules_plain> WHERE type = 'AUTH'
      AND objct     = <gs_object_result>-object
      AND field     = <gs_object_result>-field.
      IF  ( <gs_object_result>-low    CP <gs_rules_plain>-von
        OR  <gs_rules_plain>-von      CP <gs_object_result>-low ).

        APPEND INITIAL LINE TO <gs_object_result>-result ASSIGNING <ls_result>.
        <ls_result>-uc_result   = <gs_rules_plain>-check_rule.
        <ls_result>-uc_priority = <gs_rules_plain>-step.

        " Stop after first hit
        EXIT.
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.

    " ------------------------------------------------------------
    " (2) Engine Indicators via type ENGI
    " ------------------------------------------------------------
    LOOP AT gt_rules_plain ASSIGNING <gs_rules_plain> WHERE type = 'ENGI'
      AND objct     = <gs_object_result>-object
      AND field     = <gs_object_result>-field.
      IF  ( <gs_object_result>-low    CP <gs_rules_plain>-von
        OR  <gs_rules_plain>-von      CP <gs_object_result>-low ).

        APPEND INITIAL LINE TO <gs_object_result>-engines ASSIGNING <ls_result>.
        <ls_result>-uc_result   = <gs_rules_plain>-check_rule.
        <ls_result>-uc_priority = <gs_rules_plain>-step.
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.

    SORT <gs_object_result>-result BY uc_priority.     "#EC CI_SORTLOOP
    READ TABLE <gs_object_result>-result ASSIGNING <ls_result> INDEX 1.
    IF sy-subrc = 0.
      <gs_object_result>-classif_s4  = <ls_result>-uc_result.
      <gs_object_result>-uc_priority = <ls_result>-uc_priority.
    ELSE.
      <gs_object_result>-classif_s4  = TEXT-t07.
      <gs_object_result>-uc_priority = gc_not_classif.
    ENDIF.

    IF <gs_object_result>-engines IS NOT INITIAL.
      " Engine object
      SORT <gs_object_result>-engines BY uc_priority.  "#EC CI_SORTLOOP
      READ TABLE <gs_object_result>-engines ASSIGNING <ls_result> INDEX 1.
      IF sy-subrc = 0.
        <gs_object_result>-engine_classif  = <ls_result>-uc_result.
        <gs_object_result>-engine_priority = <ls_result>-uc_priority.
      ENDIF.
      IF <gs_object_result>-uc_priority = gc_not_classif.
        <gs_object_result>-classif_s4   = TEXT-t24.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.

  ENDLOOP.

  " Classification of all Roles

  CLEAR gv_percent.
  " Validation of Roles/Profiles...
  PERFORM show_indicator USING TEXT-t01 gv_percent.

  LOOP AT gt_role_result ASSIGNING <gs_role_result>.

    CLEAR lt_role_result.

    LOOP AT <gs_role_result>-objects ASSIGNING <gs_objects>.
      READ TABLE gt_object_result ASSIGNING <gs_object_result>
        INDEX <gs_objects>-index_object.
      IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
        APPEND LINES OF <gs_object_result>-result TO lt_role_result.
        IF <gs_object_result>-engine_priority IS NOT INITIAL.
          <gs_role_result>-engine = 'X'.
        ENDIF.
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.

    SORT lt_role_result BY uc_priority.                "#EC CI_SORTLOOP
    READ TABLE lt_role_result ASSIGNING <ls_result> INDEX 1.
    IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
      <gs_role_result>-classif_s4 = <ls_result>-uc_result.
      <gs_role_result>-uc_priority = <ls_result>-uc_priority.
    ELSE.
      <gs_role_result>-classif_s4  = TEXT-t07.
      <gs_role_result>-uc_priority = gc_not_classif.
    ENDIF.
    " Engine Role
    IF <gs_role_result>-uc_priority = gc_not_classif AND
       <gs_role_result>-engine = 'X'.
      <gs_role_result>-classif_s4  = TEXT-t24.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.                    "validate_auth_objects

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form get_rules
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Get Rules data from Excel file
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM get_rules.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF tys_pce,
           step  TYPE char2,
           objct TYPE xuobject,
           field TYPE xufield,
           von   TYPE xuval,
         END OF tys_pce.

  DATA: lt_pce     TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF tys_pce,
        ls_pce     LIKE LINE OF lt_pce,
        lv_version TYPE char01 VALUE 'R',
        lv_objkey  LIKE slim_cluster-cluster_id VALUE space.

  DATA: lt_rules_plain TYPE gty_t_rules_file,
        ls_rules       LIKE LINE OF gt_rules_plain,
        lv_tab_name    TYPE sobj_name VALUE 'SLIMPC_RULESET'.

  CLEAR: gt_rules_plain.

  IF p_pce = 'X'.

    SELECT * FROM (lv_tab_name) INTO TABLE lt_pce.
    LOOP AT lt_pce INTO ls_pce. " MOVE-CORRESPONDING LT_PCE[] doesn't work below 7.40
      CLEAR ls_rules.
      MOVE-CORRESPONDING ls_pce TO ls_rules.
      APPEND ls_rules TO gt_rules_plain.
    ENDLOOP.

    CLEAR ls_rules.
    ls_rules-type = 'AUTH'.
    MODIFY gt_rules_plain FROM ls_rules TRANSPORTING type WHERE step > 0.

    ls_rules-check_rule = 'GB Advanced Use'.
    MODIFY gt_rules_plain FROM ls_rules TRANSPORTING check_rule WHERE step = '0020'.

    ls_rules-check_rule = 'GC Core Use'.
    MODIFY gt_rules_plain FROM ls_rules TRANSPORTING check_rule WHERE step = '0030'.

    ls_rules-check_rule = 'GD Self-Service Use'.
    MODIFY gt_rules_plain FROM ls_rules TRANSPORTING check_rule WHERE step = '0040'.

  ELSEIF p_loc = 'X'.
    " Import the ruleset from the cluster table
    CONCATENATE lv_version p_locf INTO lv_objkey.
    IMPORT gt_rules_plain FROM DATABASE slim_cluster(zm) ID lv_objkey.
  ELSE.
    " Import the ruleset from Excel
    PERFORM import_ruleset USING p_file CHANGING lt_rules_plain.
    gt_rules_plain[] = lt_rules_plain[].
  ENDIF.

  DELETE gt_rules_plain
    WHERE type  <> 'AUTH'
      AND type  <> 'ENGI'.

  IF p_noeng = 'X'.
    " Don't care about Engines (as per selection screen)
    DELETE gt_rules_plain WHERE type = 'ENGI'.

    IF lines( gt_rules_plain ) = 0.
      " No rules left
      MESSAGE TEXT-e09 TYPE 'I'.
      REFRESH gt_rules_plain.
      RETURN.
    ENDIF.

  ENDIF.

  SORT  gt_rules_plain.
  CLEAR: gt_rules.

ENDFORM.                    "get_rules

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form validate_users
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Validation of Roles and Users
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PT_SEL_USERS Users
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM validate_users USING pt_sel_users TYPE gty_t_user_sel.

  DATA: lt_user_result       TYPE gty_t_result,
        lv_default_user_type TYPE usertypen.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_role>          TYPE gty_user_role,
                 <ls_user_result>   TYPE gty_result,
                 <ls_tutyp>         TYPE tutyp,
                 <ls_ref_user_data> LIKE LINE OF gt_user_data.


  CLEAR gv_percent.
  " Processing Users...
  PERFORM show_indicator USING TEXT-t05 gv_percent.

  " Get the default user type
  CALL FUNCTION 'SLIM_GET_DEFAULT_USER_TYPE'
    EXPORTING
      client            = sy-mandt
    IMPORTING
      default_user_type = lv_default_user_type.

  LOOP AT gt_user_data ASSIGNING <gs_user_data>.

    " User details
    READ TABLE pt_sel_users ASSIGNING <gs_sel_users>
      WITH TABLE KEY bname = <gs_user_data>-bname.

    IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
      <gs_user_data>-ustyp = <gs_sel_users>-ustyp.
      <gs_user_data>-trdat = <gs_sel_users>-trdat.
      <gs_user_data>-class = <gs_sel_users>-class.

      " Current classification
      <gs_user_data>-lic_type = <gs_sel_users>-lic_type.

      READ TABLE gt_tutyp ASSIGNING <ls_tutyp>
        WITH TABLE KEY langu   = sy-langu
                       usertyp = <gs_sel_users>-lic_type.
      IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
        <gs_user_data>-classif_curr = <ls_tutyp>-utyptext.
      ELSE.
        READ TABLE gt_tutyp ASSIGNING <ls_tutyp>
          WITH TABLE KEY langu   = 'E'
                         usertyp = <gs_sel_users>-lic_type.
        IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
          " Show User Type Description
          <gs_user_data>-classif_curr = <ls_tutyp>-utyptext.
        ELSE.
          <gs_user_data>-classif_curr = TEXT-t04.
        ENDIF.
      ENDIF.

      <gs_user_data>-name_text = <gs_sel_users>-name_text.

      IF <gs_sel_users>-refuser IS NOT INITIAL.
        " Insert the Reference User ID
        <gs_user_data>-refuser = <gs_sel_users>-refuser.

        " Add the assigned roles and profiles from the Reference User
        READ TABLE gt_user_data ASSIGNING <ls_ref_user_data> WITH KEY bname = <gs_sel_users>-refuser.
        IF sy-subrc = 0.
          " Don't insert all at once, duplicates result in Short Dump

          " INSERT LINES OF <ls_ref_user_data>-roles INTO TABLE <gs_user_data>-roles.

          LOOP AT <ls_ref_user_data>-roles ASSIGNING <ls_role>.
            READ TABLE <gs_user_data>-roles WITH KEY agr_name = <ls_role>-agr_name TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS.
            IF sy-subrc <> 0.
              <ls_role>-referenced = 'X'.
              INSERT <ls_role> INTO TABLE <gs_user_data>-roles.
            ENDIF.
          ENDLOOP.

        ENDIF.
      ENDIF.

    ENDIF.

    CLEAR lt_user_result.

    LOOP AT <gs_user_data>-roles ASSIGNING <ls_role>.
      " Roles classification
      READ TABLE gt_role_result ASSIGNING <gs_role_result>
        INDEX <ls_role>-index_role.
      IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
        APPEND INITIAL LINE TO lt_user_result ASSIGNING <ls_user_result>.
        <ls_user_result>-uc_result   = <gs_role_result>-classif_s4.
        <ls_user_result>-uc_priority = <gs_role_result>-uc_priority.

        <ls_role>-classif_s4  = <gs_role_result>-classif_s4.
        <ls_role>-uc_priority = <gs_role_result>-uc_priority.
        " Engine user
        IF <gs_role_result>-engine EQ 'X'.
          <gs_user_data>-engine = 'X'.
        ENDIF.
      ELSE.
        <ls_role>-classif_s4  = TEXT-t07.
        <ls_role>-uc_priority = gc_not_classif.
      ENDIF.

    ENDLOOP.

    " User classification
    SORT lt_user_result BY uc_priority.                "#EC CI_SORTLOOP
    READ TABLE lt_user_result ASSIGNING <ls_user_result> INDEX 1.
    IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
      <gs_user_data>-classif_s4  = <ls_user_result>-uc_result.
      <gs_user_data>-uc_priority = <ls_user_result>-uc_priority.
      IF <gs_user_data>-uc_priority = gc_not_classif AND
         <gs_user_data>-engine = 'X'.
        <gs_user_data>-classif_s4  = TEXT-t24.
      ENDIF.
    ELSE.
      <gs_user_data>-classif_s4  = TEXT-t07.
      <gs_user_data>-uc_priority = gc_not_classif.
    ENDIF.


  ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.                    "validate_users

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form validate_roles
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Validate Roles/Profiles
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PT_SEL_USERS Users
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM validate_roles USING pt_sel_users TYPE gty_t_user_sel.

  CLEAR gv_percent.
  " Processing Roles...
  PERFORM show_indicator USING TEXT-t09 gv_percent.

  LOOP AT gt_role_data ASSIGNING <gs_role_data>.

    " Role classification
    READ TABLE gt_role_result ASSIGNING <gs_role_result>
      INDEX <gs_role_data>-index_role.
    IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
      <gs_role_data>-classif_s4  = <gs_role_result>-classif_s4.
    ELSE.
      <gs_role_data>-classif_s4  = TEXT-t07.
    ENDIF.

    " User full name
    LOOP AT <gs_role_data>-users ASSIGNING <gs_users>.
      READ TABLE pt_sel_users ASSIGNING <gs_sel_users>
        WITH TABLE KEY bname = <gs_users>-bname.
      IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
        <gs_users>-name_text    = <gs_sel_users>-name_text.
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.

  ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.                    "validate_roles

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form check_selection_parameters
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Check user input on a selection-screen
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM check_selection_parameters.

  CHECK sscrfields-ucomm = 'ONLI'.

  IF gv_valid_type = gc_valid_type-role_validation AND
     ( p_role IS INITIAL AND p_profn IS INITIAL ).
    MESSAGE TEXT-e03 TYPE 'E'.
  ENDIF.

  IF gv_valid_type = gc_valid_type-previous_execution AND
    p_imprt IS INITIAL.
    MESSAGE TEXT-e04 TYPE 'E'.
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    "check_selection_parameters

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form export_validation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Export User/Role validation dataset to a file
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PV_TYPE Validation type
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM export_validation  USING pv_type TYPE c.

  DATA: lt_dataset      TYPE gty_t_dataset,
        lt_dataset_bin  TYPE solix_tab,
        lt_dataset_comp TYPE stringtab.

  DATA: lv_filename  TYPE string,
        lv_fullpath  TYPE string,
        lv_path      TYPE string,
        lv_action    TYPE i,
        lv_date      TYPE char15,
        lv_file_name TYPE string,
        lv_extension TYPE string VALUE 'zip',
        lv_filesize  TYPE i,
        lv_filetype  TYPE char10  VALUE 'BIN',
        lv_zip       TYPE xstring,
        lv_zip_encr  TYPE xstring,
        lv_error     TYPE flag.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <lt_dataset> TYPE ANY TABLE.

  CONCATENATE sy-datum sy-uzeit
    INTO lv_date SEPARATED BY '_'.

  " File name for a proper dataset
  IF pv_type EQ gc_valid_type-user_validation.

    IF gv_export_type = gc_export_type-user.
      CONCATENATE 'User_Validation' lv_date
        INTO lv_file_name SEPARATED BY '_'.
    ELSEIF gv_export_type = gc_export_type-sap.
      CONCATENATE '4SAP_User_Validation' lv_date
        INTO lv_file_name SEPARATED BY '_'.
    ENDIF.

  ELSEIF pv_type EQ gc_valid_type-role_validation.

    IF gv_export_type = gc_export_type-user.
      CONCATENATE 'Role_Validation' lv_date
        INTO lv_file_name SEPARATED BY '_'.
    ELSEIF gv_export_type = gc_export_type-sap.
      CONCATENATE '4SAP_Role_Validation' lv_date
        INTO lv_file_name SEPARATED BY '_'.
    ENDIF.
  ENDIF.

  IF gv_key IS NOT INITIAL.
    lv_extension = 'bin'.
  ENDIF.

  CALL METHOD cl_gui_frontend_services=>file_save_dialog
    EXPORTING
      default_extension         = lv_extension
      default_file_name         = lv_file_name
    CHANGING
      filename                  = lv_filename
      path                      = lv_path
      fullpath                  = lv_fullpath
      user_action               = lv_action
    EXCEPTIONS
      cntl_error                = 1
      error_no_gui              = 2
      not_supported_by_gui      = 3
      invalid_default_file_name = 4
      OTHERS                    = 5.

  IF sy-subrc <> 0.
    MESSAGE 'Action was cancelled' TYPE 'S'.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  IF lv_action <> 0.
    MESSAGE 'Action was cancelled' TYPE 'S'.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  IF gc_dataset_ver CS 'V3.'.
    IF pv_type EQ gc_valid_type-user_validation.
      PERFORM add_header USING gc_dataset_type-user_based
                        CHANGING lt_dataset.
    ELSEIF pv_type EQ gc_valid_type-role_validation.
      IF gv_export_type = gc_export_type-sap.
        " Prepare data for Export Role validation for SAP
        PERFORM reassign_role_valid_objects.
      ENDIF.
      PERFORM add_header USING gc_dataset_type-role_based
                        CHANGING lt_dataset.
    ELSE.
      MESSAGE e099(bv) WITH 'Invalid Type'. "##NO_TEXT
    ENDIF.
  ELSE.
    IF pv_type EQ gc_valid_type-user_validation.
      " Prepare User validation dataset
      PERFORM export_user_valid_dataset USING 'X' pv_type
                                   CHANGING lt_dataset.
    ELSEIF pv_type EQ gc_valid_type-role_validation.
      " Prepare Role validation dataset
      PERFORM export_role_valid_dataset USING pv_type
                                     CHANGING lt_dataset.
    ELSE.
      MESSAGE e099(bv) WITH 'Invalid Type'. "##NO_TEXT
    ENDIF.
  ENDIF.

  " Compress dataset
  PERFORM compress_data USING lt_dataset
                     CHANGING lt_dataset_comp.
  " Archive dataset
  PERFORM zip_data USING pv_type lt_dataset_comp lv_filename
                CHANGING lv_zip lv_error.

  IF lv_error IS NOT INITIAL.
    MESSAGE 'Export was terminated' TYPE 'S'.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  IF gv_key IS NOT INITIAL.
    " Encrypt dataset
    PERFORM encrypt_dataset USING lv_zip
                         CHANGING lv_zip_encr.
    CLEAR lv_zip.
    lv_zip = lv_zip_encr.
  ENDIF.

  lt_dataset_bin = cl_bcs_convert=>xstring_to_solix( iv_xstring = lv_zip ).
  ASSIGN lt_dataset_bin TO <lt_dataset>.
  lv_filesize = xstrlen( lv_zip ).

  " Download dataset
  CALL METHOD cl_gui_frontend_services=>gui_download
    EXPORTING
      filename                = lv_fullpath
      filetype                = lv_filetype
      bin_filesize            = lv_filesize
    CHANGING
      data_tab                = <lt_dataset>
    EXCEPTIONS
      file_write_error        = 1
      no_batch                = 2
      gui_refuse_filetransfer = 3
      invalid_type            = 4
      no_authority            = 5
      unknown_error           = 6
      header_not_allowed      = 7
      separator_not_allowed   = 8
      filesize_not_allowed    = 9
      header_too_long         = 10
      dp_error_create         = 11
      dp_error_send           = 12
      dp_error_write          = 13
      unknown_dp_error        = 14
      access_denied           = 15
      dp_out_of_memory        = 16
      disk_full               = 17
      dp_timeout              = 18
      file_not_found          = 19
      dataprovider_exception  = 20
      control_flush_error     = 21
      not_supported_by_gui    = 22
      error_no_gui            = 23
      OTHERS                  = 24.

  IF sy-subrc <> 0.
    MESSAGE ID sy-msgid TYPE 'S' NUMBER sy-msgno
               WITH sy-msgv1 sy-msgv2 sy-msgv3 sy-msgv4
               DISPLAY LIKE 'E'.
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    "export_validation

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form export_user_valid_dataset
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Prepare a dataset with Users validation data for downloading
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PV_ADD_HEADER   Flag for Header data
*&      --> PV_TYPE         Validation type
*&      <-- CT_DATASET      Dataset
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM export_user_valid_dataset USING VALUE(pv_add_header)
                                        pv_type    TYPE c
                               CHANGING ct_dataset TYPE gty_t_dataset.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_objects,
           object TYPE agobject,
           oclss  TYPE xuobjclass,
         END OF lty_objects.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_fields,
           field TYPE xufield,
           text  TYPE as4text,
         END OF lty_fields.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_agr_name,
           agr_name TYPE agr_name,
         END OF lty_agr_name.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_prof,
           profn TYPE xuprofname,
         END OF lty_prof.
  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_value_text,
           actvt TYPE activ_auth,
           ltext TYPE xutxt30,
         END OF lty_value_text.

  DATA: lt_objects_class TYPE SORTED TABLE OF lty_objects
          WITH UNIQUE KEY object,
        lt_fields        TYPE SORTED TABLE OF lty_fields
          WITH UNIQUE KEY field,
        lt_value_text    TYPE SORTED TABLE OF lty_value_text
          WITH UNIQUE KEY actvt,
        ls_fields        TYPE lty_fields,
        lt_agr_name      TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF lty_agr_name,
        lt_agr_text      TYPE gty_t_agr_text,
        lt_prof_text     TYPE gty_t_prof_text,
        lt_prof          TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF lty_prof,
        lt_object_text   TYPE gty_t_object_text,
        lt_object_result TYPE gty_t_object_result,
        lt_role_result   TYPE gty_t_role.

  DATA: lv_total1         TYPE i,
        lv_total2         TYPE i,
        lv_total3         TYPE i,
        lv_bname          TYPE xubname,
        lv_tabix          TYPE sytabix,
        lv_selected_roles TYPE boolean.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_roles>       TYPE gty_user_role,
                 <ls_agr_name>    TYPE lty_agr_name,
                 <ls_prof>        TYPE lty_prof,
                 <ls_objects>     TYPE lty_objects,
                 <ls_fields>      TYPE lty_fields,
                 <ls_agr_text>    TYPE gty_agr_text,
                 <ls_prof_text>   TYPE gty_prof_text,
                 <ls_object_text> TYPE gty_object_text,
                 <ls_value_text>  TYPE lty_value_text.

  IF pv_type        EQ gc_valid_type-role_validation AND
     gv_export_type EQ gc_export_type-sap.
    lt_role_result    = gt_role_result_rv.
    lt_object_result  = gt_object_result_rv.
    lv_selected_roles = 'X'.
  ELSE.
    lt_role_result   = gt_role_result.
    lt_object_result = gt_object_result.
    DESCRIBE TABLE gt_user_data LINES lv_total1.
  ENDIF.

  DESCRIBE TABLE lt_role_result LINES lv_total2.
  DESCRIBE TABLE lt_object_result LINES lv_total3.
  gv_total = lv_total1 + lv_total2 + lv_total3.

  IF pv_add_header EQ 'X'.
    " Header data
    PERFORM add_header USING gc_dataset_type-user_based
                    CHANGING ct_dataset.
  ENDIF.

  " Roles/Profiles texts
  LOOP AT lt_role_result ASSIGNING <gs_role_result>.
    IF <gs_role_result>-agr_name IS NOT INITIAL.
      APPEND INITIAL LINE TO lt_agr_name ASSIGNING <ls_agr_name>.
      <ls_agr_name>-agr_name = <gs_role_result>-agr_name.
    ELSEIF <gs_role_result>-auth IS NOT INITIAL.
      APPEND INITIAL LINE TO lt_prof ASSIGNING <ls_prof>.
      <ls_prof>-profn = <gs_role_result>-auth.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.

  IF lt_agr_name[] IS NOT INITIAL.
    " Read Profile Texts
    SELECT agr_name spras text
      INTO TABLE lt_agr_text
      FROM agr_texts                                    "#EC CI_GENBUFF
        FOR ALL ENTRIES IN lt_agr_name
     WHERE agr_name EQ lt_agr_name-agr_name
       AND spras IN gr_languages
       AND line = '00000'.

    SORT lt_agr_text BY agr_name spras.

  ENDIF.

  IF lt_prof[] IS NOT INITIAL.

    SELECT profn langu ptext
      INTO TABLE lt_prof_text
      FROM usr11                                        "#EC CI_GENBUFF
        FOR ALL ENTRIES IN lt_prof
     WHERE langu IN gr_languages
       AND profn EQ lt_prof-profn
       AND aktps EQ 'A'.

    SORT lt_prof_text BY profn langu.

  ENDIF.

  " Values texts
  SELECT actvt ltext
    FROM tactt
    INTO TABLE lt_value_text
   WHERE spras EQ 'E'.

  " Additional data for authorization objects
  IF lt_object_result[] IS NOT INITIAL.
    " Authorization Object class
    SELECT objct AS object
           oclss
      INTO TABLE lt_objects_class
      FROM tobj AS obj
        FOR ALL ENTRIES IN lt_object_result
     WHERE obj~objct EQ lt_object_result-object.

    " Authorization Object texts
    SELECT object
           ttext
      FROM tobjt                                        "#EC CI_GENBUFF
        INTO TABLE lt_object_text
          FOR ALL ENTRIES IN lt_object_result
       WHERE langu  EQ 'E'
         AND object EQ lt_object_result-object.
  ENDIF.

  " Authorization fields description
  LOOP AT lt_object_result ASSIGNING <gs_object_result>.
    CLEAR ls_fields.
    ls_fields-field = <gs_object_result>-field.
    INSERT ls_fields INTO TABLE lt_fields.
  ENDLOOP.

  LOOP AT lt_fields ASSIGNING <ls_fields>.
    CALL FUNCTION 'AUTH_FIELD_GET_INFO'
      EXPORTING
        fieldname = <ls_fields>-field
        langu     = 'E'
      IMPORTING
        text      = <ls_fields>-text.
  ENDLOOP.

  gv_percent = 30.
  " Preparing User Validation Dataset... 30%
  PERFORM show_indicator USING TEXT-t11 gv_percent.

  " Users data
  LOOP AT gt_user_data ASSIGNING <gs_user_data>.

    IF gv_export_type EQ gc_export_type-sap.
      " Export result for SAP
      " Hashed user
      lv_bname = <gs_user_data>-bname.
      PERFORM hash_data USING lv_bname
                     CHANGING gv_hash_bname.
    ENDIF.

    IF lv_selected_roles EQ 'X'.
      " For Export Role validation results for SAP
      " only selected roles should be downloaded
      LOOP AT <gs_user_data>-roles ASSIGNING <ls_roles>.
        READ TABLE gt_role_result_rv ASSIGNING <gs_role_result>
          WITH TABLE KEY agr_name = <ls_roles>-agr_name
                             auth = <ls_roles>-auth.
        IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
          lv_tabix = sy-tabix.
          APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_dataset ASSIGNING <gs_dataset>.
          MOVE-CORRESPONDING: <gs_user_data> TO <gs_dataset>.

          <gs_dataset>-index_role = lv_tabix.

          IF gv_export_type = gc_export_type-sap.
            <gs_dataset>-bname = gv_hash_bname.
            CLEAR <gs_dataset>-name_text.
          ENDIF.
        ENDIF.
      ENDLOOP.
    ELSE.
      IF lines( <gs_user_data>-roles ) = 0.
        " User without roles assigned
        APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_dataset ASSIGNING <gs_dataset>.
        MOVE-CORRESPONDING: <gs_user_data> TO <gs_dataset>.
        IF gv_export_type = gc_export_type-sap.
          <gs_dataset>-bname = gv_hash_bname.
          CLEAR <gs_dataset>-name_text.
        ENDIF.
        <gs_dataset>-lic_type = <gs_user_data>-lic_type.
      ELSE.
        LOOP AT <gs_user_data>-roles ASSIGNING <ls_roles>.
          APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_dataset ASSIGNING <gs_dataset>.
          MOVE-CORRESPONDING: <gs_user_data> TO <gs_dataset>.

          IF gv_export_type = gc_export_type-sap.
            <gs_dataset>-bname = gv_hash_bname.
            CLEAR <gs_dataset>-name_text.
          ENDIF.

          <gs_dataset>-index_role = <ls_roles>-index_role.
          <gs_dataset>-lic_type   = <gs_user_data>-lic_type.

        ENDLOOP.
      ENDIF.

    ENDIF.

  ENDLOOP.

  gv_percent = 60.
  " Preparing User Validation Dataset... 60%
  PERFORM show_indicator USING TEXT-t11 gv_percent.

  " All Roles/Profiles
  LOOP AT lt_role_result ASSIGNING <gs_role_result>.

    LOOP AT <gs_role_result>-objects ASSIGNING <gs_objects>.
      APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_dataset ASSIGNING <gs_dataset>.

      CONCATENATE <gs_role_result>-agr_name <gs_role_result>-auth
        INTO <gs_dataset>-agr_name_auth SEPARATED BY gc_separator.
      <gs_dataset>-classif_s4_agr  = <gs_role_result>-classif_s4.
      <gs_dataset>-index_object    = <gs_objects>-index_object.
