      <gs_dataset>-uc_priority_agr = <gs_role_result>-uc_priority.

      IF <gs_role_result>-agr_name IS NOT INITIAL.
        READ TABLE lt_agr_text ASSIGNING <ls_agr_text>
             WITH KEY agr_name = <gs_role_result>-agr_name
             BINARY SEARCH.

        IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
          <gs_dataset>-roletext = <ls_agr_text>-text.
        ENDIF.
      ELSEIF <gs_role_result>-auth IS NOT INITIAL.
        READ TABLE lt_prof_text ASSIGNING <ls_prof_text>
             WITH KEY profn = <gs_role_result>-auth
             BINARY SEARCH.

        IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
          <gs_dataset>-roletext = <ls_prof_text>-ptext.
        ENDIF.
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.
  ENDLOOP.

  gv_percent = 75.
  " Preparing User Validation Dataset... 75%
  PERFORM show_indicator USING TEXT-t11 gv_percent.

  " All authorization objects
  LOOP AT lt_object_result ASSIGNING <gs_object_result>.

    APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_dataset ASSIGNING <gs_dataset>.
    MOVE-CORRESPONDING: <gs_object_result> TO <gs_dataset>.
    <gs_dataset>-classif_s4_object  = <gs_object_result>-classif_s4.
    <gs_dataset>-uc_priority_object = <gs_object_result>-uc_priority.

    READ TABLE lt_objects_class ASSIGNING <ls_objects>
      WITH TABLE KEY object = <gs_object_result>-object.
    IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
      <gs_dataset>-oclass = <ls_objects>-oclss.
    ENDIF.

    READ TABLE lt_fields ASSIGNING <ls_fields>
      WITH TABLE KEY field = <gs_object_result>-field.
    IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
      <gs_dataset>-fieldtext = <ls_fields>-text.
    ENDIF.

    READ TABLE lt_object_text ASSIGNING <ls_object_text>
      WITH TABLE KEY object = <gs_object_result>-object.
    IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
      <gs_dataset>-objecttext = <ls_object_text>-ttext.
    ENDIF.

    READ TABLE lt_value_text ASSIGNING <ls_value_text>
      WITH TABLE KEY actvt = <gs_object_result>-low.
    IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
      <gs_dataset>-valuetext = <ls_value_text>-ltext.
    ENDIF.

  ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.                    "export_user_valid_dataset

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form export_role_valid_dataset
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Prepare a dataset with Roles validation data(including Users Validation)
*& for downloading
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PV_TYPE    Validation type
*&      <-- CT_DATASET Dataset with Roles validation data
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM export_role_valid_dataset USING pv_type     TYPE c
                            CHANGING ct_dataset  TYPE gty_t_dataset.

  DATA: lt_dataset_users TYPE gty_t_dataset,
        lv_bname         TYPE xubname.

  IF gv_export_type = gc_export_type-sap.
    " Prepare data for Export Role validation for SAP
    PERFORM reassign_role_valid_objects.
  ENDIF.

  " Header data
  PERFORM add_header USING gc_dataset_type-role_based
                  CHANGING ct_dataset.

  CLEAR gv_percent.
  " Preparing Role Validation Dataset...
  PERFORM show_indicator USING TEXT-t12 gv_percent.

  LOOP AT gt_role_data ASSIGNING <gs_role_data>.

    IF <gs_role_data>-users IS NOT INITIAL.
      LOOP AT <gs_role_data>-users ASSIGNING <gs_users>.
        APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_dataset ASSIGNING <gs_dataset>.
        MOVE-CORRESPONDING: <gs_role_data> TO <gs_dataset>.
        CLEAR <gs_dataset>-classif_s4.

        IF gv_export_type EQ gc_export_type-sap.
          " Export result for SAP
          " Hashed user
          lv_bname = <gs_users>-bname.
          PERFORM hash_data USING lv_bname
                         CHANGING gv_hash_bname.
          <gs_dataset>-bname = gv_hash_bname.
        ELSE.
          <gs_dataset>-bname = <gs_users>-bname.
        ENDIF.

        CONCATENATE <gs_role_data>-agr_name <gs_role_data>-auth
          INTO <gs_dataset>-agr_name_auth SEPARATED BY gc_separator.
        <gs_dataset>-classif_s4_agr = <gs_role_data>-classif_s4.
      ENDLOOP.
    ELSE.
      APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_dataset ASSIGNING <gs_dataset>.
      MOVE-CORRESPONDING: <gs_role_data> TO <gs_dataset>.
      CLEAR <gs_dataset>-classif_s4.

      CONCATENATE <gs_role_data>-agr_name <gs_role_data>-auth
        INTO <gs_dataset>-agr_name_auth SEPARATED BY gc_separator.
      <gs_dataset>-classif_s4_agr = <gs_role_data>-classif_s4.
    ENDIF.

  ENDLOOP.

  " Additional data for User validation
  PERFORM export_user_valid_dataset USING abap_false pv_type
                                 CHANGING lt_dataset_users.

  IF lt_dataset_users IS NOT INITIAL.
    " Label-end of all Roles validation rows
    APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_dataset ASSIGNING <gs_dataset>.
    <gs_dataset>-bname = cl_abap_char_utilities=>form_feed.

    LOOP AT lt_dataset_users ASSIGNING <gs_dataset>.
      APPEND <gs_dataset> TO ct_dataset.
    ENDLOOP.
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    "export_role_valid_dataset

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form import_validation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Import User/Role validation dataset from a file
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM import_validation.

  DATA: lt_dataset      TYPE gty_t_dataset,
        lt_dataset_comp TYPE stringtab,
        lt_dataset_bin  TYPE solix_tab,
        lv_type         TYPE c,
        lv_key          TYPE string,
        lv_filename     TYPE string,
        lv_filename2    TYPE string,
        lv_filetype     TYPE char10  VALUE 'ASC',
        lv_extension    TYPE string,
        lv_decrypt      TYPE boolean,
        lv_filelength   TYPE i,
        lv_data_upl     TYPE xstring,
        lv_data_encr    TYPE xstring,
        lv_data         TYPE xstring,
        lv_dataset      TYPE xstring.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <lt_dataset> TYPE ANY TABLE.

  CLEAR: gt_user_data, gt_role_data, gt_role_result, gt_object_result.

  " Key for decryption
  IF p_pwdd IS NOT INITIAL.
    lv_key = p_pwdd.
    PERFORM generate_key USING lv_key.
  ENDIF.

  lv_filename = p_imprt.

  CALL METHOD cl_bcs_utilities=>split_name
    EXPORTING
      iv_name      = lv_filename
    IMPORTING
      ev_extension = lv_extension.

  TRANSLATE lv_extension TO UPPER CASE.

  IF lv_extension CS 'TXT'.
    ASSIGN lt_dataset_comp TO <lt_dataset>.
  ELSEIF lv_extension CS 'BIN' OR lv_extension CS 'ZIP'.
    lv_filetype = 'BIN'.
    IF lv_extension CS 'BIN'.
      lv_decrypt = 'X'.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN lt_dataset_bin TO <lt_dataset>.
  ENDIF.

  TRY.
      " Get filename for message display
      CALL METHOD cl_bcs_utilities=>split_path
        EXPORTING
          iv_path = lv_filename
        IMPORTING
          ev_name = lv_filename2.

      " Loading <filename>
      CONCATENATE 'Loading' lv_filename2 INTO lv_filename2 SEPARATED BY space.

    CATCH cx_bcs. " stay with 'Loading file...'
      lv_filename2 = TEXT-t15.
  ENDTRY.

  CLEAR gv_percent.
  " Loading file...
  PERFORM show_indicator USING lv_filename2 gv_percent.

  CALL METHOD cl_gui_frontend_services=>gui_upload
    EXPORTING
      filename                = lv_filename
      filetype                = lv_filetype
    IMPORTING
      filelength              = lv_filelength
    CHANGING
      data_tab                = <lt_dataset>
    EXCEPTIONS
      file_open_error         = 1
      file_read_error         = 2
      no_batch                = 3
      gui_refuse_filetransfer = 4
      invalid_type            = 5
      no_authority            = 6
      unknown_error           = 7
      bad_data_format         = 8
      header_not_allowed      = 9
      separator_not_allowed   = 10
      header_too_long         = 11
      unknown_dp_error        = 12
      access_denied           = 13
      dp_out_of_memory        = 14
      disk_full               = 15
      dp_timeout              = 16
      not_supported_by_gui    = 17
      error_no_gui            = 18
      OTHERS                  = 19.

  IF sy-subrc <> 0.
    MESSAGE ID sy-msgid TYPE 'S' NUMBER sy-msgno
               WITH sy-msgv1 sy-msgv2 sy-msgv3 sy-msgv4
               DISPLAY LIKE 'E'.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  IF lt_dataset_bin IS NOT INITIAL.
    " uploaded data: encrypted txt/zip or simple zip
    lv_data_upl  = cl_bcs_convert=>solix_to_xstring( it_solix = lt_dataset_bin ).
    lv_data = lv_data_upl(lv_filelength).
  ENDIF.

  IF lv_decrypt = 'X'.
    " encrypted data here: txt or zip
    lv_data_encr = lv_data.

    IF gv_key IS NOT INITIAL.

      CLEAR gv_percent.
      " Decrypt file...
      PERFORM show_indicator USING TEXT-t28 gv_percent.

      " Decrypt dataset
      PERFORM decrypt_dataset USING lv_data_encr
                           CHANGING lv_data.
    ENDIF.
  ENDIF.

  PERFORM prepare_hashed_users.

  IF lv_data IS NOT INITIAL.

    CLEAR gv_percent.
    " Decompress file...
    PERFORM show_indicator USING TEXT-t29 gv_percent.

    " try to unzip decrypted data
    " if there is no zip content in the source data
    " after perform we have decrypted txt data
    PERFORM unzip_data USING lv_data
                    CHANGING lv_dataset.
  ENDIF.

  IF lv_dataset IS NOT INITIAL.
    PERFORM  convert_to_dataset USING lv_dataset
                             CHANGING lt_dataset_comp.
  ENDIF.

  PERFORM uncompress_dataset USING lt_dataset_comp
                          CHANGING lt_dataset.

  PERFORM get_dataset_type CHANGING lt_dataset lv_type.

  IF lv_type IS INITIAL.
    MESSAGE TEXT-e05 TYPE 'S' DISPLAY LIKE 'E'.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  CASE lv_type.

    WHEN gc_valid_type-user_validation.

      PERFORM import_user_valid_dataset USING lt_dataset.
      PERFORM get_texts.
      PERFORM prepare_output_user_validation.
      PERFORM display_classification_users.

    WHEN gc_valid_type-role_validation.

      PERFORM import_role_valid_dataset USING lt_dataset.
      PERFORM get_texts.
      PERFORM prepare_output_role_validation.
      PERFORM display_classification_roles.

  ENDCASE.

ENDFORM.                    "import_validation

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form import_user_valid_dataset
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Prepare User validation data from uploaded dataset
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PT_DATASET       Dataset for User Validation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM import_user_valid_dataset  USING pt_dataset TYPE gty_t_dataset.

  DATA: lt_dataset       TYPE gty_t_dataset,
        lt_dataset_tmp   TYPE gty_t_dataset,
        ls_object_result TYPE gty_object_result,
        ls_role_result   TYPE gty_role,
        ls_user_role     TYPE gty_user_role,
        ls_object        TYPE gty_object,
        ls_user_data     TYPE gty_user_data.

  lt_dataset[] = pt_dataset[].

  " Split uploaded dataset for:
  " 1. Users data
  " 2. Roles/Profiles data
  " 3. Authorization objects data

  " Part 3. Authorization objects data
  LOOP AT lt_dataset ASSIGNING <gs_dataset>
    WHERE object IS NOT INITIAL.

    CLEAR ls_object_result.
    MOVE-CORRESPONDING <gs_dataset> TO ls_object_result.
    INSERT ls_object_result INTO TABLE gt_object_result.

    DELETE lt_dataset.
  ENDLOOP.

  " Part 2. Roles/Profiles data
  LOOP AT lt_dataset ASSIGNING <gs_dataset>
    WHERE agr_name_auth IS NOT INITIAL.

    APPEND <gs_dataset> TO lt_dataset_tmp.

    DELETE lt_dataset.
  ENDLOOP.

  LOOP AT lt_dataset_tmp ASSIGNING <gs_dataset>.
    AT NEW agr_name_auth.
      CLEAR ls_role_result.
      SPLIT <gs_dataset>-agr_name_auth AT gc_separator
        INTO ls_role_result-agr_name ls_role_result-auth.
      ls_role_result-classif_s4 = <gs_dataset>-classif_s4_agr.
    ENDAT.

    READ TABLE gt_object_result ASSIGNING <gs_object_result>
      INDEX  <gs_dataset>-index_object.
    IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
      CLEAR ls_object.
      MOVE-CORRESPONDING <gs_object_result> TO ls_object.
      ls_object-index_object = <gs_dataset>-index_object.
      INSERT ls_object INTO TABLE ls_role_result-objects.

      IF <gs_object_result>-engine_priority IS NOT INITIAL.
        ls_role_result-engine = 'X'.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.

    AT END OF agr_name_auth.
      INSERT ls_role_result INTO TABLE gt_role_result.
    ENDAT.
  ENDLOOP.

  " Part 1. Users data
  CLEAR lt_dataset_tmp.
  LOOP AT lt_dataset ASSIGNING <gs_dataset>
    WHERE bname IS NOT INITIAL.
    APPEND <gs_dataset> TO lt_dataset_tmp.
  ENDLOOP.

  LOOP AT lt_dataset_tmp ASSIGNING <gs_dataset>.
    AT NEW bname.
      CLEAR ls_user_data.
      MOVE-CORRESPONDING <gs_dataset> TO ls_user_data.
      " it might be a dataset from SAP side
      " there UserID has a hashed value
      " try to find original UserID for a hashed User
      READ TABLE gt_hash_users ASSIGNING <gs_hash_users>
        WITH TABLE KEY hash_bname = ls_user_data-bname.
      IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
        ls_user_data-bname      = <gs_hash_users>-bname.
        ls_user_data-name_text  = <gs_hash_users>-name_text.
        ls_user_data-hash_bname = <gs_hash_users>-hash_bname.
      ENDIF.

    ENDAT.

    READ TABLE gt_role_result ASSIGNING <gs_role_result>
      INDEX  <gs_dataset>-index_role.
    IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
      CLEAR ls_user_role.
      MOVE-CORRESPONDING <gs_role_result> TO ls_user_role.
      ls_user_role-index_role = <gs_dataset>-index_role.
      INSERT ls_user_role INTO TABLE ls_user_data-roles.

      IF <gs_role_result>-engine EQ 'X'.
        ls_user_data-engine = 'X'.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.

    AT END OF bname.
      INSERT ls_user_data INTO TABLE gt_user_data.
    ENDAT.
  ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.                    "import_user_valid_dataset

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form import_role_valid_dataset
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Prepare Role validation data from uploaded dataset
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PT_DATA_ROLES    Dataset for Role Validation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM import_role_valid_dataset  USING pt_dataset TYPE gty_t_dataset.

  DATA: lt_dataset    TYPE gty_t_dataset,
        lt_data_roles TYPE gty_t_data_roles,
        ls_role_data  TYPE gty_role_data,
        ls_users      TYPE gty_role_user.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_data_roles> TYPE gty_data_roles.

  lt_dataset[] = pt_dataset[].

  " Split uploaded dataset for Roles data(Roles+Users) and Users data(for User simulation)
  LOOP AT lt_dataset ASSIGNING <gs_dataset>.
    IF <gs_dataset>-bname NE cl_abap_char_utilities=>form_feed.
      APPEND INITIAL LINE TO lt_data_roles ASSIGNING <ls_data_roles>.
      MOVE-CORRESPONDING <gs_dataset> TO <ls_data_roles>.
      DELETE lt_dataset.
    ELSE.
      DELETE lt_dataset.
      EXIT.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.

  " Users data and some additional tables(Roles and Authorization objects)
  PERFORM import_user_valid_dataset USING lt_dataset.

  " Prepare Roles data
  LOOP AT lt_data_roles ASSIGNING <ls_data_roles>.

    AT NEW agr_name_auth.
      CLEAR ls_role_data.
      MOVE-CORRESPONDING <ls_data_roles> TO ls_role_data.
      SPLIT <ls_data_roles>-agr_name_auth AT gc_separator
        INTO ls_role_data-agr_name ls_role_data-auth.
      ls_role_data-classif_s4 = <ls_data_roles>-classif_s4_agr.
    ENDAT.

    " Roles Users
    IF <ls_data_roles>-bname IS NOT INITIAL.
      CLEAR ls_users.
      ls_users-bname = <ls_data_roles>-bname.

      READ TABLE gt_hash_users ASSIGNING <gs_hash_users>
        WITH TABLE KEY hash_bname = <ls_data_roles>-bname.
      IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
        ls_users-bname      = <gs_hash_users>-bname.
        ls_users-name_text  = <gs_hash_users>-name_text.
        ls_users-hash_bname = <gs_hash_users>-hash_bname.
      ENDIF.

      INSERT ls_users INTO TABLE ls_role_data-users.
    ENDIF.

    AT END OF agr_name_auth.
      INSERT ls_role_data INTO TABLE gt_role_data.
    ENDAT.

  ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.                    "import_role_valid_dataset

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form get_dataset_type
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Get uploaded dataset type
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      <-- CT_DATASET Dataset
*&      <-- CV_TYPE    Validation type
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM get_dataset_type  CHANGING ct_dataset TYPE gty_t_dataset
                                cv_type    TYPE c.

  " First row - Dataset type
  " Second row - System details
  READ TABLE ct_dataset ASSIGNING <gs_dataset>
    INDEX 1.
  IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
    IF <gs_dataset>-bname = gc_dataset_type-user_based.
      cv_type = gc_valid_type-user_validation.
    ELSEIF <gs_dataset>-bname = gc_dataset_type-role_based.
      cv_type = gc_valid_type-role_validation.
    ENDIF.
    DELETE ct_dataset INDEX 1.
  ENDIF.

  " System details
  DELETE ct_dataset INDEX 1.

ENDFORM.                    "get_dataset_type

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form check_file_parameter
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Check user input for a file with rules
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM check_file_parameter .

  CHECK sscrfields-ucomm = 'ONLI'.

  IF ( rb_user = 'X' OR rb_role = 'X' ).
    " User Validation / Role Validation
    IF ( p_xls = 'X' AND p_file IS INITIAL ) OR
       ( p_loc = 'X' AND p_locf IS INITIAL ).
      " Select a valid ruleset file
      MESSAGE TEXT-e02 TYPE 'I' DISPLAY LIKE 'E'.
      LEAVE SCREEN.
    ENDIF.

  ELSEIF rb_rule = 'X'. " Rulesets & Results
    " Rulesets & Results
    IF p_locr IS INITIAL.
      " Select a valid result file
      MESSAGE TEXT-e04 TYPE 'I' DISPLAY LIKE 'E'.
    ENDIF.

  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    "check_file_parameter

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form set_index_role_objects
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Set technical indicies for Objects in Roles
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM set_index_role_objects .
  DATA: lv_tabix TYPE sytabix.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_role_result_object> TYPE gty_object .

  LOOP AT gt_role_data ASSIGNING <gs_role_data>.
    READ TABLE gt_role_result ASSIGNING <gs_role_result>
      WITH TABLE KEY agr_name = <gs_role_data>-agr_name
                     auth     = <gs_role_data>-auth.
    IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
      <gs_role_data>-index_role = <gs_role_result>-index_role = sy-tabix.

      LOOP AT <gs_role_result>-objects ASSIGNING <ls_role_result_object>.
        READ TABLE gt_object_result ASSIGNING <gs_object_result>
          WITH TABLE KEY object = <ls_role_result_object>-object
                         field  = <ls_role_result_object>-field
                         low    = <ls_role_result_object>-low
                         high   = <ls_role_result_object>-high.
        IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
          lv_tabix = sy-tabix.
          <ls_role_result_object>-index_object = lv_tabix.
        ENDIF.

      ENDLOOP.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.                    "set_index_role_objects

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form prepare_output_fields
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Prepare fields for dynamic output table creation
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM prepare_output_fields CHANGING er_output TYPE REF TO data.

  DATA: lt_component TYPE cl_abap_structdescr=>component_table,
        ls_component TYPE cl_abap_structdescr=>component,
        tys_output   TYPE REF TO cl_abap_structdescr,
        lr_output    TYPE REF TO cl_abap_datadescr.

  DATA: lv_col_pos           TYPE lvc_colpos,
        lt_classif_s4_fields TYPE gty_t_classif_s4_fields,
        lt_key_fields        TYPE abap_keydescr_tab.

  IF p_pce = 'X'.

    " Add color table to OUTPUT structure in "PCE mode"
    REFRESH lt_component.
    ls_component-name = 'COLOR'.
    ls_component-type ?= cl_abap_datadescr=>describe_by_name( 'LVC_T_SCOL' ).
    APPEND ls_component TO lt_component.

  ENDIF.

  ls_component-name = 'CLASSIF_CURR'.
  ls_component-type ?= cl_abap_datadescr=>describe_by_name( 'TEXT50' ).
  APPEND ls_component TO lt_component.

  " Collect and sort fields for the output table
  LOOP AT gt_classif_s4_fields ASSIGNING <gs_classif_s4_fields>.
    IF <gs_classif_s4_fields>-fname CS gc_not_classif.
      " Park the entry to append it as last column
      APPEND <gs_classif_s4_fields> TO lt_classif_s4_fields.
    ELSE.
      ls_component-name = <gs_classif_s4_fields>-fname.
      ls_component-type ?= cl_abap_datadescr=>describe_by_name( 'INT4' ).
      APPEND ls_component TO lt_component.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.

  SORT lt_classif_s4_fields BY fname DESCENDING.

  " Add the remaining parked entries
  LOOP AT lt_classif_s4_fields ASSIGNING <gs_classif_s4_fields>.
    ls_component-name = <gs_classif_s4_fields>-fname.
    ls_component-type ?= cl_abap_datadescr=>describe_by_name( 'INT4' ).
    APPEND ls_component TO lt_component.
  ENDLOOP.

  " Collect the key fields (since we need to do a COLLECT later on)
  APPEND 'CLASSIF_CURR' TO lt_key_fields.

  " Create the internal table
  tys_output = cl_abap_structdescr=>get( p_components = lt_component
                                         p_strict     = abap_false ).
  lr_output = cl_abap_tabledescr=>create( p_line_type = tys_output
                                          p_key       = lt_key_fields ).
  CREATE DATA er_output TYPE HANDLE lr_output.

ENDFORM.                    "prepare_output_fields

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form show_classif_roles
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Show Roles classification by selected Total Users
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PV_BUTTON Flag for button Role display
*&      --> PV_ROW    Selected row with User
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM show_classif_roles USING VALUE(pv_button)
                                    pv_row TYPE salv_de_row.

  DATA: lt_role_classif     TYPE gty_t_role_classif,
        ls_role_classif     TYPE gty_role_classif,
        lt_user_classif     TYPE gty_t_user_classif,
        ls_user_classif     TYPE gty_user_classif,
        lt_field_cat        TYPE lvc_t_fcat,
        lv_component        TYPE name_feld,
        lt_role_classif_dyn TYPE REF TO data,
        lr_role_classif_dyn TYPE REF TO data,
        ls_agr_flags        LIKE LINE OF gt_agr_flags,
        lv_cond             TYPE string.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_roles>            TYPE gty_user_role,
                 <ls_role_classif>     TYPE gty_role_classif,
                 <lv_field>            TYPE any,
                 <ls_role_classif_dyn> TYPE any,
                 <ls_record>           TYPE any,
                 <lv_bname>            TYPE any.

  CLEAR: gt_role_classif, gt_role_engines, gt_engine_fields,
         gv_title, gv_single_user.

  IF pv_button EQ 'X'.
    " Button Role display pressed
    " Roles for all users to be displayed
    lt_user_classif = gt_user_classif.
    " Header info for ALV
    gv_title = TEXT-t21.
    " selected users from previous ALV
    CONCATENATE gv_title gv_sel_users INTO gv_title SEPARATED BY space.
  ELSE.
    " Click on a user
    gv_single_user = 'X'.
    " Header info for ALV
    gv_title = TEXT-t23.
    " Only Roles for a selected User
    READ TABLE <gt_user_classif> ASSIGNING <ls_record> INDEX pv_row.

    IF sy-subrc = 0.
      UNASSIGN <lv_bname>.
      ASSIGN COMPONENT 'BNAME' OF STRUCTURE <ls_record> TO <lv_bname>.
      ls_user_classif-bname = <lv_bname>.
      APPEND ls_user_classif TO lt_user_classif.
      CONCATENATE gv_title <lv_bname> INTO gv_title SEPARATED BY space.

      " See whether there is a Reference User reference to be considered as well...
      ASSIGN COMPONENT 'REFUSER' OF STRUCTURE <ls_record> TO <lv_bname>.
      IF <lv_bname> IS NOT INITIAL.
        CONCATENATE gv_title <lv_bname> INTO gv_title SEPARATED BY '/'.
      ENDIF.

    ENDIF.
  ENDIF.

  LOOP AT lt_user_classif ASSIGNING <gs_user_classif>.
    READ TABLE gt_user_data ASSIGNING <gs_user_data>
      WITH TABLE KEY bname = <gs_user_classif>-bname.
    IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
      LOOP AT <gs_user_data>-roles ASSIGNING <ls_roles>.
        CLEAR ls_role_classif.
        MOVE-CORRESPONDING <ls_roles> TO ls_role_classif.
        ls_role_classif-total_usr = 1.

        IF <ls_roles>-agr_name IS NOT INITIAL.
          ls_role_classif-type = gc_role_type-role.
        ELSE.
          ls_role_classif-type = gc_role_type-profile.
          ls_role_classif-agr_name = <ls_roles>-auth.
        ENDIF.

        COLLECT ls_role_classif INTO lt_role_classif.

        " Engines for Roles
        IF <gs_user_data>-engine EQ 'X'.
          PERFORM add_role_engines USING <ls_roles>-agr_name <ls_roles>-auth <ls_roles>-index_role.
        ENDIF.
      ENDLOOP.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.

  SORT lt_role_classif BY agr_name ASCENDING total_usr DESCENDING.

  REFRESH gt_agr_flags.

  " Read role classifications
  IF lines( lt_role_classif ) > 0.
    SELECT a~agr_name a~flag_value b~utyptext
           INTO CORRESPONDING FIELDS OF TABLE gt_agr_flags
           FROM agr_flags AS a INNER JOIN tutyp AS b   "#EC CI_BUFFJOIN
           ON a~flag_value = b~usertyp
           FOR ALL ENTRIES IN lt_role_classif
           WHERE a~agr_name = lt_role_classif-agr_name
           AND a~flag_type = 'LICENSE_01'
           AND b~langu     = 'E'.
  ENDIF.

  " Roles
  LOOP AT lt_role_classif ASSIGNING <ls_role_classif>.
    CASE <ls_role_classif>-type.
      WHEN gc_role_type-role.
        PERFORM read_role_text USING <ls_role_classif>-agr_name
                            CHANGING <ls_role_classif>-agr_text.
      WHEN gc_role_type-profile.
        PERFORM read_prof_text USING <ls_role_classif>-agr_name
                            CHANGING <ls_role_classif>-agr_text.
    ENDCASE.

    READ TABLE gt_agr_flags INTO ls_agr_flags
         WITH KEY agr_name = <ls_role_classif>-agr_name.
    IF sy-subrc = 0.
      CONCATENATE ls_agr_flags-flag_value ls_agr_flags-utyptext
             INTO <ls_role_classif>-classif_curr SEPARATED BY space.
    ENDIF.

    " Add the total number of objects and the target classification ratio
    PERFORM add_ratio_role CHANGING <ls_role_classif>.

    APPEND <ls_role_classif> TO gt_role_classif.
  ENDLOOP.

  SORT gt_role_classif BY total_usr DESCENDING.

  CLEAR: lt_role_classif.

  IF gt_role_classif[] IS INITIAL.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  " Create a dynamic table for Role classification ALV
  PERFORM prepare_role_classif_fields USING gc_valid_type-user_validation
                                   CHANGING lt_field_cat.

  CALL METHOD cl_alv_table_create=>create_dynamic_table
    EXPORTING
      it_fieldcatalog           = lt_field_cat
    IMPORTING
      ep_table                  = lt_role_classif_dyn
    EXCEPTIONS
      generate_subpool_dir_full = 1
      OTHERS                    = 2.
  IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
    ASSIGN lt_role_classif_dyn->* TO <gt_role_classif>.

    CREATE DATA lr_role_classif_dyn LIKE LINE OF <gt_role_classif>.
    ASSIGN lr_role_classif_dyn->* TO <ls_role_classif_dyn>.
  ENDIF.

  " Prepare data for Role classification ALV
  LOOP AT gt_role_classif ASSIGNING <gs_role_classif>.
    CLEAR <ls_role_classif_dyn>.

    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'AGR_NAME' OF STRUCTURE <ls_role_classif_dyn> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_role_classif>-agr_name.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'AGR_TEXT' OF STRUCTURE <ls_role_classif_dyn> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_role_classif>-agr_text.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'TYPE' OF STRUCTURE <ls_role_classif_dyn> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      " R = Role; P = Profile
      <lv_field> = <gs_role_classif>-type.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'CLASSIF_CURR' OF STRUCTURE <ls_role_classif_dyn> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_role_classif>-classif_curr.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'CLASSIF_S4' OF STRUCTURE <ls_role_classif_dyn> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_role_classif>-classif_s4.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'TOTAL_USR' OF STRUCTURE <ls_role_classif_dyn> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_role_classif>-total_usr.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'RATIO' OF STRUCTURE <ls_role_classif_dyn> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_role_classif>-ratio.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'OBJECT_COUNT' OF STRUCTURE <ls_role_classif_dyn> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_role_classif>-object_count.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'COUNT' OF STRUCTURE <ls_role_classif_dyn> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = 1.
    ENDIF.

    IF gv_single_user = 'X'.
      ASSIGN COMPONENT 'REFERENCED' OF STRUCTURE <ls_role_classif_dyn> TO <lv_field>.
      IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED AND <gs_role_classif>-referenced = 'X'.
        <lv_field> = '@ID@'.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.

    CASE <gs_role_classif>-type.
      WHEN 'R'. " Role
        lv_cond = 'agr_name EQ <gs_role_classif>-agr_name'. "##NO_TEXT
      WHEN 'P'. " Profile
        lv_cond = 'auth EQ <gs_role_classif>-agr_name'. "##NO_TEXT
    ENDCASE.

    " Engine columns
    LOOP AT gt_role_engines ASSIGNING <gs_role_engines> WHERE (lv_cond).

      lv_component = <gs_role_engines>-engine_priority.
      ASSIGN COMPONENT lv_component OF STRUCTURE <ls_role_classif_dyn> TO <lv_field>.
      IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
        <lv_field> = 1.

        " Set the Engine flag so that we can easily filter on engines
        ASSIGN COMPONENT 'ENGINE' OF STRUCTURE <ls_role_classif_dyn> TO <lv_field>.
        IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
          <lv_field> = 'X'.
        ENDIF.

      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.

    APPEND <ls_role_classif_dyn> TO <gt_role_classif>.

  ENDLOOP.

  PERFORM display_classif_roles.

ENDFORM.                    "show_classif_roles

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form show_classif_total_users
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Show Users classification by selected Total Users
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PV_CLASSIF_CURR Existing User Classification
*&      --> PV_UC_PRIORITY  S/4 Classification
*&      --> PV_ENGINE       Flag for engine column
*&      --> PV_COLUMN       Selected column
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM show_classif_total_users  USING  pv_classif_curr TYPE char40
                                      pv_uc_priority  TYPE numc4
                                      pv_engine       TYPE boolean
                                      pv_column       TYPE salv_de_column.

  DATA: lv_cond         TYPE string,
        lt_field_cat    TYPE lvc_t_fcat,
        lv_component    TYPE name_feld,
        lt_user_classif TYPE REF TO data,
        lr_user_classif TYPE REF TO data.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <lv_field>        TYPE any,
                 <ls_user_classif> TYPE any.

  CLEAR: gt_user_classif, gt_user_engines, gt_engine_fields.

  IF pv_uc_priority IS INITIAL.
    " Click on a Total column
    IF pv_classif_curr = 'All'.
      CLEAR lv_cond.
    ELSE.
      lv_cond = 'classif_curr EQ pv_classif_curr'. "##NO_TEXT
    ENDIF.

    LOOP AT gt_user_data ASSIGNING <gs_user_data> WHERE (lv_cond).
      APPEND INITIAL LINE TO gt_user_classif ASSIGNING <gs_user_classif>.
      MOVE-CORRESPONDING <gs_user_data> TO <gs_user_classif>.
      IF <gs_user_data>-engine EQ 'X'.
        PERFORM add_user_engines.
      ENDIF.

      PERFORM add_ratio_user USING <gs_user_data>
                          CHANGING <gs_user_classif>.

    ENDLOOP.
  ELSE.
    IF pv_engine IS INITIAL.
      " Click on S/4 classification column
      IF pv_classif_curr = 'All'.
        lv_cond = 'uc_priority  EQ pv_uc_priority'. "##NO_TEXT
      ELSE.
        CONCATENATE 'classif_curr EQ pv_classif_curr AND' "##NO_TEXT
                    'uc_priority EQ pv_uc_priority' "##NO_TEXT
               INTO lv_cond SEPARATED BY space.
      ENDIF.

      LOOP AT gt_user_data ASSIGNING <gs_user_data> WHERE (lv_cond).
        IF <gs_user_data>-uc_priority NE gc_not_classif OR
          " below condition is for Not classified column
           ( <gs_user_data>-uc_priority EQ gc_not_classif AND
             <gs_user_data>-engine EQ abap_false ).

          APPEND INITIAL LINE TO gt_user_classif ASSIGNING <gs_user_classif>.
          MOVE-CORRESPONDING <gs_user_data> TO <gs_user_classif>.

          PERFORM add_ratio_user USING <gs_user_data>
                              CHANGING <gs_user_classif>.

          IF <gs_user_data>-engine EQ 'X'.
            PERFORM add_user_engines.
          ENDIF.

        ENDIF.
      ENDLOOP.
    ELSE.
      " Click on Engine column
      IF pv_classif_curr = 'All'.
        CONCATENATE 'uc_priority EQ pv_uc_priority AND' "##NO_TEXT
                    'engine EQ abap_true' "##NO_TEXT
               INTO lv_cond SEPARATED BY space.
      ELSE.
        CONCATENATE 'classif_curr EQ pv_classif_curr AND' "##NO_TEXT
                    'uc_priority  EQ pv_uc_priority AND' "##NO_TEXT
                    'engine EQ abap_true' "##NO_TEXT
               INTO lv_cond SEPARATED BY space.
      ENDIF.

      LOOP AT gt_user_data ASSIGNING <gs_user_data> WHERE (lv_cond).
        APPEND INITIAL LINE TO gt_user_classif ASSIGNING <gs_user_classif>.
        MOVE-CORRESPONDING <gs_user_data> TO <gs_user_classif>.

        PERFORM add_ratio_user USING <gs_user_data>
                            CHANGING <gs_user_classif>.

        PERFORM add_user_engines.
      ENDLOOP.
    ENDIF.
  ENDIF.

  " Don't show the Reference Users
  DELETE gt_user_classif WHERE ustyp = 'L'.

  IF gt_user_classif[] IS INITIAL.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  " Create a dynamic table for User classification ALV
  PERFORM prepare_user_classif_fields CHANGING lt_field_cat.

  CALL METHOD cl_alv_table_create=>create_dynamic_table
    EXPORTING
      it_fieldcatalog           = lt_field_cat
    IMPORTING
      ep_table                  = lt_user_classif
    EXCEPTIONS
      generate_subpool_dir_full = 1
      OTHERS                    = 2.
  IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
    ASSIGN lt_user_classif->* TO <gt_user_classif>.

    CREATE DATA lr_user_classif LIKE LINE OF <gt_user_classif>.
    ASSIGN lr_user_classif->* TO <ls_user_classif>.
  ENDIF.

  " Prepare data for User classification ALV
  LOOP AT gt_user_classif ASSIGNING <gs_user_classif>.
    CLEAR <ls_user_classif>.

    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'BNAME' OF STRUCTURE <ls_user_classif> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_user_classif>-bname.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'HASH_BNAME' OF STRUCTURE <ls_user_classif> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_user_classif>-hash_bname.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'NAME_TEXT' OF STRUCTURE <ls_user_classif> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_user_classif>-name_text.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'CLASSIF_CURR' OF STRUCTURE <ls_user_classif> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_user_classif>-classif_curr.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'CLASSIF_S4' OF STRUCTURE <ls_user_classif> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_user_classif>-classif_s4.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'CLASS' OF STRUCTURE <ls_user_classif> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_user_classif>-class.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'TRDAT' OF STRUCTURE <ls_user_classif> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_user_classif>-trdat.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'LIC_TYPE' OF STRUCTURE <ls_user_classif> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_user_classif>-lic_type.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'RATIO' OF STRUCTURE <ls_user_classif> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_user_classif>-ratio.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'REFUSER' OF STRUCTURE <ls_user_classif> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = <gs_user_classif>-refuser.
    ENDIF.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 'COUNT' OF STRUCTURE <ls_user_classif> TO <lv_field>.
    IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
      <lv_field> = 1.
    ENDIF.

    " Engine columns
    IF <gs_user_classif>-engine EQ 'X'.
      LOOP AT gt_user_engines ASSIGNING <gs_user_engines>
        WHERE bname EQ <gs_user_classif>-bname.
        lv_component = <gs_user_engines>-engine_priority.
        ASSIGN COMPONENT lv_component OF STRUCTURE <ls_user_classif> TO <lv_field>.
        IF <lv_field> IS ASSIGNED.
          <lv_field> = 1.
        ENDIF.
      ENDLOOP.
    ENDIF.

    APPEND <ls_user_classif> TO <gt_user_classif>.
  ENDLOOP.

  " Header info for ALV
  CLEAR: gv_title, gv_sel_users.
  gv_title = TEXT-t18.
  gv_sel_users = TEXT-t20.
  REPLACE '&1' IN gv_sel_users WITH pv_classif_curr.

  READ TABLE gt_classif_s4_fields ASSIGNING <gs_classif_s4_fields>
    WITH KEY fname = pv_column.
  IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
    REPLACE '&2' IN gv_sel_users WITH <gs_classif_s4_fields>-header_text.
  ENDIF.
  CONCATENATE gv_title gv_sel_users
    INTO gv_title SEPARATED BY space.

  " Display ALV with User classification
  PERFORM display_classif_users.

ENDFORM.                    "show_classif_total_users

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form display_classification_users
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Display Total Users by Classifications
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM display_classification_users.

  CLEAR: gr_table400, gr_table401, gr_table402, gr_table403,
         gr_container400, gr_container401, gr_container402, gr_container403.

  CALL SCREEN 400.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form pbo_0400
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& PBO of screen 0400
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM pbo_0400 .

  DATA: lr_functions        TYPE REF TO cl_salv_functions_list,
        lr_display_settings TYPE REF TO cl_salv_display_settings,
        lr_layout           TYPE REF TO cl_salv_layout,
        lr_events           TYPE REF TO lcl_handle_events,
        lr_table_events     TYPE REF TO cl_salv_events_table,
        lr_aggrs            TYPE REF TO cl_salv_aggregations,
        lr_column           TYPE REF TO cl_salv_column_table,
        lr_columns          TYPE REF TO cl_salv_columns_table,
        lt_columns          TYPE salv_t_column_ref,
        lv_title            TYPE lvc_title,
        lv_text             TYPE string,
        lv_icon             TYPE string,
        lv_color            TYPE lvc_s_colo,
        lv_edit_mask        TYPE lvc_edtmsk,
        lv_key              TYPE salv_s_layout_key.

  SET PF-STATUS ' '.

  IF gr_container400 IS NOT BOUND.
    IF cl_salv_table=>is_offline( ) EQ if_salv_c_bool_sap=>false.
      CREATE OBJECT gr_container400
        EXPORTING
          container_name = 'CONTAINER400'.
    ENDIF.

    TRY.
        cl_salv_table=>factory(
          EXPORTING
            r_container    = gr_container400
            container_name = 'CONTAINER400'
          IMPORTING
            r_salv_table   = gr_table400
          CHANGING
            t_table        = <gt_total_classif_users> ).
      CATCH cx_salv_msg.                                "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    lr_functions = gr_table400->get_functions( ).
    lr_functions->set_all( 'X' ).

    " Title for saved datasets
    IF gv_valid_type = gc_valid_type-rules_n_results.
      CONCATENATE gs_info-sysid '/' gs_info-client INTO lv_text.
      CONDENSE lv_text NO-GAPS.

      WRITE gs_info-date TO lv_title LEFT-JUSTIFIED.
      CONCATENATE lv_text lv_title INTO lv_text SEPARATED BY space.

      WRITE gs_info-time TO lv_title LEFT-JUSTIFIED.
      CONCATENATE lv_text lv_title(5) INTO lv_text SEPARATED BY space.

      IF gs_info-version IS NOT INITIAL.
        CONCATENATE lv_text gs_info-version INTO lv_text SEPARATED BY space.
      ENDIF.

      CONCATENATE lv_text gs_info-ruleset INTO lv_text SEPARATED BY space.

      lv_title = lv_text.
    ELSE.
      lv_title = TEXT-t22.
    ENDIF.
    lr_display_settings = gr_table400->get_display_settings( ).
    lr_display_settings->set_list_header( lv_title ).
    lr_display_settings->set_striped_pattern( 'X' ).

    lv_text = TEXT-b01.
    lv_icon = icon_export.

    lv_color-col = 1.
    lv_color-int = 0.
    lv_color-inv = 0.

    TRY.
        lr_functions->add_function(
          name     = '&EXP_UV'
          icon     = lv_icon
          text     = lv_text
          tooltip  = lv_text
          position = if_salv_c_function_position=>right_of_salv_functions ).
      CATCH cx_salv_existing cx_salv_wrong_call.        "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    lv_text = TEXT-b03.
    lv_icon = icon_export.
    TRY.
        lr_functions->add_function(
          name     = '&EXP_SAP'
          icon     = lv_icon
          text     = lv_text
          tooltip  = lv_text
          position = if_salv_c_function_position=>right_of_salv_functions ).
      CATCH cx_salv_existing cx_salv_wrong_call.        "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    lr_layout = gr_table400->get_layout( ).
    lv_key-report = sy-repid.
    lv_key-handle = sy-dynnr.
    lr_layout->set_key( lv_key ).
    lr_layout->set_save_restriction( ).

    lr_table_events = gr_table400->get_event( ).

    CREATE OBJECT lr_events.
    SET HANDLER lr_events->on_single_click_alv1 FOR lr_table_events.
    SET HANDLER lr_events->on_user_command FOR lr_table_events.

    TRY.
        gr_table400->get_columns( )->set_color_column( 'COLOR' ).
      CATCH cx_salv_data_error cx_salv_invalid_input.
        " Don't do anything if the color table cannot be created
    ENDTRY.

    lr_columns = gr_table400->get_columns( ).
    lt_columns = lr_columns->get( ).

    lr_aggrs = gr_table400->get_aggregations( ).
    lr_aggrs->set_aggregation_before_items( ).

    LOOP AT lt_columns ASSIGNING <gs_column>.
      TRY.
          lr_column ?= lr_columns->get_column( <gs_column>-columnname ).
          CLEAR: gv_l_text, gv_m_text, gv_s_text.
          CASE <gs_column>-columnname.
            WHEN 'CLASSIF_CURR'.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
              lr_column->set_optimized( 'X' ).
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a12.
              gv_m_text = TEXT-a11.
              gv_s_text = TEXT-a10.

            WHEN 'TOTAL'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a04.
              gv_m_text = TEXT-a04.
              gv_s_text = TEXT-a04.
              lr_column->set_cell_type( if_salv_c_cell_type=>hotspot ).

              lv_color-col = 5.
              lv_color-int = 0.
              lv_color-inv = 0.
              lr_column->set_color( lv_color ).

              TRY.
                  CALL METHOD lr_aggrs->add_aggregation
                    EXPORTING
                      columnname  = <gs_column>-columnname
                      aggregation = if_salv_c_aggregation=>total.
                CATCH cx_salv_data_error .              "#EC NO_HANDLER
                CATCH cx_salv_not_found .               "#EC NO_HANDLER
                CATCH cx_salv_existing .                "#EC NO_HANDLER
              ENDTRY.

            WHEN 'UC_PRIORITY'.
              lr_column->set_technical( if_salv_c_bool_sap=>true ).

            WHEN OTHERS.
              lr_column->set_cell_type( if_salv_c_cell_type=>hotspot ).

              TRY.
                  CALL METHOD lr_aggrs->add_aggregation
                    EXPORTING
                      columnname  = <gs_column>-columnname
                      aggregation = if_salv_c_aggregation=>total.
                CATCH cx_salv_data_error .              "#EC NO_HANDLER
                CATCH cx_salv_not_found .               "#EC NO_HANDLER
                CATCH cx_salv_existing .                "#EC NO_HANDLER
              ENDTRY.

              READ TABLE gt_classif_s4_fields ASSIGNING <gs_classif_s4_fields>
                WITH KEY fname = <gs_column>-columnname.
              IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
                gv_l_text = <gs_classif_s4_fields>-text.
                gv_m_text = <gs_classif_s4_fields>-text.
                gv_s_text = <gs_classif_s4_fields>-text.
              ENDIF.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
              lr_column->set_optimized( 'X' ).

              IF <gs_column>-columnname CS 'ENGI' AND <gs_column>-columnname(4) <> '9999'.
                lv_edit_mask = 'RR(_____)'.
                lr_column->set_edit_mask( lv_edit_mask ).
              ENDIF.

          ENDCASE.

          lr_column->set_short_text( gv_s_text ).
          lr_column->set_medium_text( gv_m_text ).
          lr_column->set_long_text( gv_l_text ).

        CATCH cx_salv_not_found.                        "#EC NO_HANDLER
      ENDTRY.
    ENDLOOP.

    gr_table400->display( ).
  ELSE.
    gr_table400->refresh( ).
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form add_ratio_role
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Add the ratio of assigned objects to object with target classification
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM add_ratio_role CHANGING cs_role_classif TYPE gty_role_classif.

  DATA: lv_lines    TYPE i,
        lv_total    TYPE i,
        lv_text(20) TYPE c.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_object> TYPE gty_object.

  " Read classified role entry
  CASE cs_role_classif-type.
    WHEN gc_role_type-role.
      READ TABLE gt_role_result ASSIGNING <gs_role_result>
                 WITH KEY agr_name = cs_role_classif-agr_name
                          auth     = space
                 BINARY SEARCH.
    WHEN gc_role_type-profile.
      READ TABLE gt_role_result ASSIGNING <gs_role_result>
                 WITH KEY agr_name = space
                          auth     = cs_role_classif-agr_name
                 BINARY SEARCH.
  ENDCASE.

  CHECK sy-subrc = 0.

  " Total number of objects included in the role
  cs_role_classif-object_count = lines( <gs_role_result>-objects ).

  " Continue only with classified roles
  CHECK cs_role_classif-classif_s4 <> TEXT-t07.
  CHECK cs_role_classif-classif_s4 <> TEXT-t24.

  " Number of objects / with target classification
  LOOP AT <gs_role_result>-objects ASSIGNING <ls_object>.
    READ TABLE gt_object_result ASSIGNING <gs_object_result>
         WITH KEY object = <ls_object>-object
                  field  = <ls_object>-field
                  low    = <ls_object>-low
                  high   = <ls_object>-high.
    IF sy-subrc = 0.
      " Count only classified objects as total number for the ratio
      IF <gs_object_result>-classif_s4 <> TEXT-t07 AND
         <gs_object_result>-classif_s4 <> TEXT-t24 AND
         <gs_object_result>-classif_s4 IS NOT INITIAL.
        ADD 1 TO lv_total.
      ENDIF.
      " Count objects with target classification
      IF <gs_object_result>-classif_s4 = cs_role_classif-classif_s4.
        ADD 1 TO lv_lines.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.

  WRITE lv_total TO cs_role_classif-ratio LEFT-JUSTIFIED NO-ZERO.
  WRITE lv_lines TO lv_text               LEFT-JUSTIFIED NO-ZERO.
  CONCATENATE lv_text '/' cs_role_classif-ratio INTO cs_role_classif-ratio.
  CONDENSE cs_role_classif-ratio NO-GAPS.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form exit_screen
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*  Exit from screen
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM exit_screen .

  DATA: lv_okcode TYPE sy-ucomm.

  lv_okcode = gv_okcode.
  CLEAR gv_okcode.

  CASE lv_okcode.

    WHEN '%EX' OR 'BACK' OR 'RW'.

      CASE sy-dynnr.

        WHEN 401. " User List
          REFRESH gt_user_classif.
          IF gr_container401 IS BOUND.
            CALL METHOD gr_container401->free.
            CLEAR: gr_container401, gr_table401.
          ENDIF.

        WHEN 402. " Roles of selected users
          REFRESH gt_role_classif.
          IF gr_container402 IS BOUND.
            CALL METHOD gr_container402->free.
            CLEAR: gr_container402, gr_table402.
          ENDIF.

        WHEN 403.      " Roles details
          REFRESH gt_object_classif.
          IF gr_container403 IS BOUND.
            CALL METHOD gr_container403->free.
            CLEAR: gr_container403, gr_table403.
          ENDIF.

        WHEN 501. " Role Validation User List
          REFRESH gt_role_users.
          IF gr_container501 IS BOUND.
            gr_container501->free( ).
            CLEAR: gr_container501, gr_table501.
          ENDIF.

      ENDCASE.

      cl_gui_cfw=>flush( ).

      " Now we can leave the screen
      SET SCREEN 0.
      LEAVE SCREEN.

  ENDCASE.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form add_ratio_user
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Add the ratio of assigned roles to roles with target classification
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM add_ratio_user USING cs_user_data    TYPE gty_user_data
                 CHANGING cs_user_classif TYPE gty_user_classif.

  DATA: lv_lines    TYPE i,
        lv_total    TYPE i,
        lv_text(20) TYPE c.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_role> TYPE gty_user_role.

  " Total number of roles
  lv_total = lines( cs_user_data-roles ).
  IF lv_total = 0.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  WRITE lv_total TO cs_user_classif-ratio LEFT-JUSTIFIED NO-ZERO.

  " Number of roles with target classification
  LOOP AT cs_user_data-roles ASSIGNING <ls_role>
          WHERE classif_s4 = cs_user_classif-classif_s4.
    ADD 1 TO lv_lines.
  ENDLOOP.

  IF lv_lines = 0.
    lv_text = '0'.
  ELSE.
    WRITE lv_lines TO lv_text LEFT-JUSTIFIED NO-ZERO.
  ENDIF.
  CONCATENATE lv_text '/' cs_user_classif-ratio INTO cs_user_classif-ratio.
  CONDENSE cs_user_classif-ratio NO-GAPS.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form pbo_0401
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& PBO of screen 0401
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM pbo_0401 .

  DATA: lr_functions        TYPE REF TO cl_salv_functions_list,
        lr_display_settings TYPE REF TO cl_salv_display_settings,
        lr_layout           TYPE REF TO cl_salv_layout,
        lr_selections       TYPE REF TO cl_salv_selections,
        lr_events           TYPE REF TO lcl_handle_events,
        lr_table_events     TYPE REF TO cl_salv_events_table,
        lr_aggrs            TYPE REF TO cl_salv_aggregations,
        lr_sorts            TYPE REF TO cl_salv_sorts,
        lr_column           TYPE REF TO cl_salv_column_table,
        lr_columns          TYPE REF TO cl_salv_columns_table,
        lt_columns          TYPE salv_t_column_ref,
        lv_title            TYPE lvc_title,
        lv_length           TYPE i,
        lv_title_len        TYPE i,
        lv_records          TYPE string,
        lv_records_len      TYPE i,
        lv_lines            TYPE i,
        lv_text             TYPE string,
        lv_icon             TYPE string,
        lv_key              TYPE salv_s_layout_key.

  IF gv_title IS INITIAL.
    lv_text  = 'Text Elements are not properly maintained!'. "##NO_TEXT
    MESSAGE lv_text TYPE 'W'.
    gv_title = 'MISSING TEXT ELEMENTS'.  "##NO_TEXT
  ENDIF.

  " Add Number of Records to the title
  lv_title_len   = strlen( gv_title ).
  lv_records     = lines( <gt_user_classif> ).
  lv_records_len = strlen( lv_records ) + 2.
  lv_length      = lv_records_len + lv_title_len.

  " Put together the title
  lv_lines = lines( <gt_user_classif> ).
  WRITE lv_lines TO lv_title.
  CONCATENATE '(' lv_title ')' INTO lv_text.
  CONDENSE lv_text NO-GAPS.

  IF lv_length > 70.
    " ... and shorten it if necessary so that the number of entries can be added
    lv_title_len = lv_title_len - lv_records_len - 4.
    CONCATENATE gv_title(lv_title_len) '...' INTO lv_title.
  ELSE.
    " ... no shortening required
    lv_title = gv_title.
  ENDIF.

  " concatenate the final title text
  CONCATENATE lv_title lv_text INTO lv_title SEPARATED BY space.

  IF gr_container401 IS BOUND.
    gr_container401->free( ).
    cl_gui_cfw=>flush( ).
    CLEAR: gr_container401, gr_table401.
  ENDIF.

  IF gr_container401 IS NOT BOUND.
    IF cl_salv_table=>is_offline( ) EQ if_salv_c_bool_sap=>false.
      CREATE OBJECT gr_container401
        EXPORTING
          container_name = 'CONTAINER401'.
    ENDIF.
    TRY.
        cl_salv_table=>factory(
          EXPORTING
            r_container    = gr_container401
            container_name = 'CONTAINER401'
          IMPORTING
            r_salv_table = gr_table401
          CHANGING
            t_table      = <gt_user_classif> ).
      CATCH cx_salv_msg.                                "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    lr_functions = gr_table401->get_functions( ).
    lr_functions->set_all( 'X' ).

    lr_display_settings = gr_table401->get_display_settings( ).
    lr_display_settings->set_list_header( lv_title ).
    lr_display_settings->set_striped_pattern( 'X' ).

    lr_selections = gr_table401->get_selections( ).
    lr_selections->set_selection_mode( if_salv_c_selection_mode=>multiple ).

    lv_text = TEXT-b04.
    lv_icon = icon_other_object.
    TRY.
        lr_functions->add_function(
          name     = '&ROLES'
          icon     = lv_icon
          text     = lv_text
          tooltip  = lv_text
          position = if_salv_c_function_position=>right_of_salv_functions ).
      CATCH cx_salv_existing cx_salv_wrong_call.        "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    " Transfer the user classification to USR06
    lv_text = TEXT-b08.
    lv_icon = icon_other_object.
    TRY.
        lr_functions->add_function(
          name     = '&USERCLASS'
          icon     = lv_icon
          text     = lv_text
          tooltip  = lv_text
          position = if_salv_c_function_position=>right_of_salv_functions ).
      CATCH cx_salv_existing cx_salv_wrong_call.        "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    " Check whether the user is authorized to change the classification
    AUTHORITY-CHECK OBJECT 'S_USER_GRP'
    ID 'CLASS' DUMMY
    ID 'ACTVT'     FIELD '02'.

    IF sy-subrc <> 0.
      " Disable the Transfer Function if the user is not authorized
      TRY.
          CALL METHOD lr_functions->enable_function
            EXPORTING
              name    = '&USERCLASS'
              boolean = abap_false.

        CATCH cx_salv_wrong_call.
        CATCH cx_salv_not_found.
      ENDTRY.
    ENDIF.



    lr_layout = gr_table401->get_layout( ).
    lv_key-report = sy-repid.
    lv_key-handle = sy-dynnr.
    lr_layout->set_key( lv_key ).
    lr_layout->set_save_restriction( ).

    lr_table_events = gr_table401->get_event( ).

    CREATE OBJECT lr_events.
    SET HANDLER lr_events->on_user_command FOR lr_table_events.
    SET HANDLER lr_events->on_single_click_alv4 FOR lr_table_events.

    lr_sorts = gr_table401->get_sorts( ).

    TRY.
        lr_sorts->add_sort(
                EXPORTING
                  columnname = 'BNAME'
                  sequence   = if_salv_c_sort=>sort_up ).
      CATCH cx_salv_not_found.                          "#EC NO_HANDLER
      CATCH cx_salv_existing.                           "#EC NO_HANDLER
      CATCH cx_salv_data_error.                         "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    TRY.
        lr_sorts->add_sort(
                EXPORTING
                  columnname = 'NAME_TEXT'
                  sequence   = if_salv_c_sort=>sort_up ).
      CATCH cx_salv_not_found.                          "#EC NO_HANDLER
      CATCH cx_salv_existing.                           "#EC NO_HANDLER
      CATCH cx_salv_data_error.                         "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    lr_aggrs = gr_table401->get_aggregations( ).
    lr_aggrs->set_aggregation_before_items( ).

    lr_columns = gr_table401->get_columns( ).
    lt_columns = lr_columns->get( ).
    lr_columns->set_optimize( 'X' ).

    PERFORM get_table_components USING <gt_user_classif>
                              CHANGING gt_struct_components.

    LOOP AT lt_columns ASSIGNING <gs_column>.
      TRY.
          lr_column ?= lr_columns->get_column( <gs_column>-columnname ).
          CLEAR: gv_l_text, gv_m_text, gv_s_text.
          CASE <gs_column>-columnname.

            WHEN 'COUNT'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a30.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).

            WHEN 'TRDAT'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a29.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).

            WHEN 'REFUSER'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a27.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).

            WHEN 'RATIO'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a03.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
              lr_column->set_alignment( if_salv_c_alignment=>centered ).
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).

            WHEN 'CLASSIF_S4'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a01.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).

            WHEN 'LIC_TYPE'.
              gv_s_text = TEXT-a06.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'S' ).

            WHEN 'CLASS'.
              gv_s_text = TEXT-a28.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'M' ).

            WHEN 'CLASSIF_CURR'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a12.
              gv_m_text = TEXT-a11.
              gv_s_text = TEXT-a10.

            WHEN 'BNAME'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a08.
              gv_m_text = TEXT-a08.
              gv_s_text = TEXT-a08.

              lr_column->set_cell_type( if_salv_c_cell_type=>hotspot ).

            WHEN 'NAME_TEXT'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a09.
              gv_m_text = TEXT-a09.
              gv_s_text = TEXT-a09.

            WHEN 'HASH_BNAME'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a13.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).

              " Check whether hashed user IDs are included.
              LOOP AT gt_user_classif TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS WHERE hash_bname <> ' '.
                EXIT.
              ENDLOOP.
              IF sy-subrc <> 0.
                " If not, we can hide the column
                lr_column->set_visible( abap_false ).
              ENDIF.

            WHEN OTHERS.
              " Engine columns
              lr_column->set_zero( abap_false ).
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).

              TRY.
                  CALL METHOD lr_aggrs->add_aggregation
                    EXPORTING
                      columnname  = <gs_column>-columnname
                      aggregation = if_salv_c_aggregation=>total.
                CATCH cx_salv_data_error .              "#EC NO_HANDLER
                CATCH cx_salv_not_found .               "#EC NO_HANDLER
                CATCH cx_salv_existing .                "#EC NO_HANDLER
              ENDTRY.

              READ TABLE gt_engine_fields ASSIGNING <gs_engine_fields>
              WITH KEY fname = <gs_column>-columnname.
              IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
                gv_l_text = <gs_engine_fields>-text.
              ELSE.
                gv_l_text = <gs_column>-columnname.
              ENDIF.

          ENDCASE.

          lr_column->set_short_text( gv_s_text ).
          lr_column->set_medium_text( gv_m_text ).
          lr_column->set_long_text( gv_l_text ).

        CATCH cx_salv_not_found.                        "#EC NO_HANDLER
      ENDTRY.
    ENDLOOP.

    gr_table401->display( ).

  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form pbo_0402
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& PBO of screen 0402
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM pbo_0402 .

  DATA: lr_functions        TYPE REF TO cl_salv_functions_list,
        lr_display_settings TYPE REF TO cl_salv_display_settings,
        lr_layout           TYPE REF TO cl_salv_layout,
        lr_selections       TYPE REF TO cl_salv_selections,
        lr_events           TYPE REF TO lcl_handle_events,
        lr_table_events     TYPE REF TO cl_salv_events_table,
        lr_aggrs            TYPE REF TO cl_salv_aggregations,
        lr_column           TYPE REF TO cl_salv_column_table,
        lr_columns          TYPE REF TO cl_salv_columns_table,
        lt_columns          TYPE salv_t_column_ref,
        lv_text             TYPE string,
        lv_tooltip          TYPE string,
        lv_icon             TYPE string,
        lv_key              TYPE salv_s_layout_key.

  IF gr_container402 IS NOT BOUND.
    IF cl_salv_table=>is_offline( ) EQ if_salv_c_bool_sap=>false.
      CREATE OBJECT gr_container402
        EXPORTING
          container_name = 'CONTAINER402'.
    ENDIF.
    TRY.
        cl_salv_table=>factory(
          EXPORTING
            r_container    = gr_container402
            container_name = 'CONTAINER402'
          IMPORTING
            r_salv_table = gr_table402
          CHANGING
            t_table      = <gt_role_classif> ).
      CATCH cx_salv_msg.                                "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    " Reset filter for unclassified entries
    gv_402_filtered = abap_false.

    lr_functions = gr_table402->get_functions( ).
    lr_functions->set_all( 'X' ).

    lv_text = TEXT-b05.
    lv_icon = icon_other_object.
    TRY.
        lr_functions->add_function(
          name     = '&ROLECLASS'
          icon     = lv_icon
          text     = lv_text
          tooltip  = lv_text
          position = if_salv_c_function_position=>right_of_salv_functions ).
      CATCH cx_salv_existing cx_salv_wrong_call.        "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    " Check whether the user is authorized to change the role classification
    AUTHORITY-CHECK OBJECT 'S_USER_AGR'
    ID 'ACT_GROUP' DUMMY
    ID 'ACTVT'     FIELD '02'.

    IF sy-subrc <> 0.
      " Disable the Transfer Function if the user is not authorized
      TRY.
          CALL METHOD lr_functions->enable_function
            EXPORTING
              name    = '&ROLECLASS'
              boolean = abap_false.

        CATCH cx_salv_wrong_call.
        CATCH cx_salv_not_found.
      ENDTRY.
    ENDIF.

    lv_text    = TEXT-b06.
    lv_icon    = icon_toggle_display.
    TRY.
        lr_functions->add_function(
          name     = '&TOGGLE'
          icon     = lv_icon
          text     = lv_text
          tooltip  = lv_text
          position = if_salv_c_function_position=>right_of_salv_functions ).
      CATCH cx_salv_existing cx_salv_wrong_call.        "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    lv_icon    = icon_export.
    lv_tooltip = TEXT-tt8.
    TRY.
        lr_functions->add_function(
          name     = '&DETAILS'
          icon     = lv_icon
          tooltip  = lv_tooltip
          position = if_salv_c_function_position=>right_of_salv_functions ).
      CATCH cx_salv_existing cx_salv_wrong_call.        "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    lr_display_settings = gr_table402->get_display_settings( ).
    lr_display_settings->set_list_header( gv_title ).
    lr_display_settings->set_striped_pattern( 'X' ).

    lr_selections = gr_table402->get_selections( ).
    lr_selections->set_selection_mode( if_salv_c_selection_mode=>multiple ).

    lr_layout = gr_table402->get_layout( ).
    lv_key-report = sy-repid.
    lv_key-handle = sy-dynnr.
    lr_layout->set_key( lv_key ).
    lr_layout->set_save_restriction( ).

    lr_table_events = gr_table402->get_event( ).

    CREATE OBJECT lr_events.
    SET HANDLER lr_events->on_single_click_alv2 FOR lr_table_events.
    SET HANDLER lr_events->on_user_command FOR lr_table_events.

    lr_columns = gr_table402->get_columns( ).
    lt_columns = lr_columns->get( ).
    lr_columns->set_optimize( 'X' ).

    lr_aggrs = gr_table402->get_aggregations( ).
    lr_aggrs->set_aggregation_before_items( ).

    " Pre-set the filter to classified entries
    PERFORM show_hide_unclassified_entries USING sy-dynnr CHANGING gv_402_filtered.

    PERFORM get_table_components USING gt_role_classif
                              CHANGING gt_struct_components.

    LOOP AT lt_columns ASSIGNING <gs_column>.
      TRY.
          lr_column ?= lr_columns->get_column( <gs_column>-columnname ).
          CLEAR: gv_l_text, gv_m_text, gv_s_text.
          CASE <gs_column>-columnname.

            WHEN 'REFERENCED'.
              IF gv_single_user = 'X'.
                gv_l_text = TEXT-a27.
                lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
                lr_column->set_alignment( if_salv_c_alignment=>centered ).
                lr_column->set_optimized( ).
              ELSE.
                lr_column->set_technical( 'X' ). " Hide the column
              ENDIF.

            WHEN 'COUNT'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a30.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).

            WHEN 'OBJECT_COUNT'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a07.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).

            WHEN 'RATIO'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a03.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
              lr_column->set_alignment( if_salv_c_alignment=>centered ).
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).

            WHEN 'AGR_TEXT' OR 'PTEXT'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a22.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).

            WHEN 'AGR_NAME' OR 'AUTH'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a26.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
              lr_column->set_cell_type( if_salv_c_cell_type=>hotspot ).

            WHEN 'CLASSIF_CURR'. " Current Role Classification
              IF lines( gt_agr_flags ) = 0. " No roles classified
                lr_column->set_technical( 'X' ). " Hide the column
              ELSE.
                gv_l_text = TEXT-a12.
                lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
              ENDIF.

            WHEN 'CLASSIF_S4'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a01.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).

            WHEN 'TOTAL_USR'.
              IF gv_single_user = 'X'.
                lr_column->set_technical( 'X' ).
              ELSE.
                gv_l_text = TEXT-a05.
                lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
                lr_column->set_optimized( ).
                lr_column->set_cell_type( if_salv_c_cell_type=>hotspot ).
              ENDIF.

            WHEN 'ENGINE' OR 'TYPE'.
              lr_column->set_technical( 'X' ).

            WHEN OTHERS.
              " Engine columns
              lr_column->set_zero( abap_false ).
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).

              TRY.
                  CALL METHOD lr_aggrs->add_aggregation
                    EXPORTING
                      columnname  = <gs_column>-columnname
                      aggregation = if_salv_c_aggregation=>total.
                CATCH cx_salv_data_error .              "#EC NO_HANDLER
                CATCH cx_salv_not_found .               "#EC NO_HANDLER
                CATCH cx_salv_existing .                "#EC NO_HANDLER
              ENDTRY.

              READ TABLE gt_engine_fields ASSIGNING <gs_engine_fields>
                WITH KEY fname = <gs_column>-columnname.
              IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
                gv_l_text = <gs_engine_fields>-text.
              ELSE.
                gv_l_text = <gs_column>-columnname.
              ENDIF.
          ENDCASE.

          lr_column->set_short_text( gv_s_text ).
          lr_column->set_medium_text( gv_m_text ).
          lr_column->set_long_text( gv_l_text ).

        CATCH cx_salv_not_found.                        "#EC NO_HANDLER
      ENDTRY.
    ENDLOOP.

    gr_table402->display( ).

  ELSE.

    lr_display_settings = gr_table402->get_display_settings( ).
    lr_display_settings->set_list_header( gv_title ).
    gr_table402->refresh( refresh_mode = if_salv_c_refresh=>full ).

  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
