FORM pbo_0403 .

  DATA: lr_functions        TYPE REF TO cl_salv_functions_list,
        lr_layout           TYPE REF TO cl_salv_layout,
        lr_display_settings TYPE REF TO cl_salv_display_settings,
        lr_events           TYPE REF TO lcl_handle_events,
        lr_table_events     TYPE REF TO cl_salv_events_table,
        lr_sorts            TYPE REF TO cl_salv_sorts,
        lr_column           TYPE REF TO cl_salv_column_table,
        lr_columns          TYPE REF TO cl_salv_columns_table,
        lt_columns          TYPE salv_t_column_ref,
        lv_text             TYPE string,
        lv_icon             TYPE string,
        lv_key              TYPE salv_s_layout_key.

  IF gr_container403 IS NOT BOUND.
    IF cl_salv_table=>is_offline( ) EQ if_salv_c_bool_sap=>false.
      CREATE OBJECT gr_container403
        EXPORTING
          container_name = 'CONTAINER403'.
    ENDIF.
    TRY.
        cl_salv_table=>factory(
          EXPORTING
            r_container    = gr_container403
            container_name = 'CONTAINER403'
          IMPORTING
            r_salv_table = gr_table403
          CHANGING
            t_table      = gt_object_classif ).
      CATCH cx_salv_msg.                                "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    " Reset filter for unclassified entries
    gv_403_filtered = abap_false.

    lr_functions = gr_table403->get_functions( ).
    lr_functions->set_all( 'X' ).

    lv_text    = TEXT-b06.
    lv_icon    = icon_toggle_display.
    TRY.
        lr_functions->add_function(
          name     = '&TOGGLE'
          icon     = lv_icon
          text     = lv_text
          tooltip  = lv_text
          position = if_salv_c_function_position=>right_of_salv_functions ).
      CATCH cx_salv_existing cx_salv_wrong_call.        "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    lr_display_settings = gr_table403->get_display_settings( ).
    lr_display_settings->set_list_header( gv_title ).
    lr_display_settings->set_striped_pattern( 'X' ).

    lr_table_events = gr_table403->get_event( ).

    CREATE OBJECT lr_events.
    SET HANDLER lr_events->on_user_command FOR lr_table_events.
    SET HANDLER lr_events->on_double_click_0403 FOR lr_table_events.

    lr_layout = gr_table403->get_layout( ).
    lv_key-report = sy-repid.
    lv_key-handle = sy-dynnr.
    lr_layout->set_key( lv_key ).
    lr_layout->set_save_restriction( ).

    lr_sorts = gr_table403->get_sorts( ).
    TRY.
        lr_sorts->add_sort(
                EXPORTING
                  columnname = 'OBJECT'
                  sequence   = if_salv_c_sort=>sort_up ).
      CATCH cx_salv_not_found.                          "#EC NO_HANDLER
      CATCH cx_salv_existing.                           "#EC NO_HANDLER
      CATCH cx_salv_data_error.                         "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    TRY.
        lr_sorts->add_sort(
                EXPORTING
                  columnname = 'TTEXT'
                  sequence   = if_salv_c_sort=>sort_up ).
      CATCH cx_salv_not_found.                          "#EC NO_HANDLER
      CATCH cx_salv_existing.                           "#EC NO_HANDLER
      CATCH cx_salv_data_error.                         "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    TRY.
        lr_sorts->add_sort(
                EXPORTING
                  columnname = 'FIELD'
                  sequence   = if_salv_c_sort=>sort_up ).
      CATCH cx_salv_not_found.                          "#EC NO_HANDLER
      CATCH cx_salv_existing.                           "#EC NO_HANDLER
      CATCH cx_salv_data_error.                         "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    TRY.
        lr_sorts->add_sort(
                EXPORTING
                  columnname = 'LOW'
                  sequence   = if_salv_c_sort=>sort_up ).
      CATCH cx_salv_not_found.                          "#EC NO_HANDLER
      CATCH cx_salv_existing.                           "#EC NO_HANDLER
      CATCH cx_salv_data_error.                         "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    lr_columns = gr_table403->get_columns( ).
    lt_columns = lr_columns->get( ).
    lr_columns->set_optimize( 'X' ).

    " Pre-set the filter to classified entries
    PERFORM show_hide_unclassified_entries USING sy-dynnr CHANGING gv_403_filtered.

    PERFORM get_table_components USING gt_object_classif
                              CHANGING gt_struct_components.

    LOOP AT lt_columns ASSIGNING <gs_column>.
      TRY.
          lr_column ?= lr_columns->get_column( <gs_column>-columnname ).
          CLEAR: gv_l_text, gv_m_text, gv_s_text.
          CASE <gs_column>-columnname.

            WHEN 'COUNT'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a30.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).

            WHEN 'PS_POSID'.
              gv_s_text = TEXT-a23.
              gv_m_text = TEXT-a24.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a25.
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).

            WHEN 'LOW'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a20.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).

            WHEN 'HIGH'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a21.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).

            WHEN 'FIELD_TEXT'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a22.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
              lr_column->set_output_length( '20' ).

            WHEN 'LOW_TEXT' OR 'HIGH_TEXT'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a22.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).

            WHEN 'AGR_NAME' OR
                 'AGR_TEXT' OR
                 'OBJECT'   OR
                 'TTEXT'    OR
                 'FIELD'.

              READ TABLE gt_struct_components ASSIGNING <gs_struct_components>
                WITH KEY name = <gs_column>-columnname.
              IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
                go_elem_descr ?= <gs_struct_components>-type.
                CLEAR gs_flddescr.
                gs_flddescr = go_elem_descr->get_ddic_field( ).

                gv_l_text = gs_flddescr-scrtext_l.
                gv_m_text = gs_flddescr-scrtext_m.
                gv_s_text = gs_flddescr-scrtext_s.
              ENDIF.

              lr_column->set_optimized( abap_false ).

            WHEN 'CLASSIF_S4'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a01.
              gv_m_text = TEXT-a01.
              gv_s_text = TEXT-a02.
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).

            WHEN 'ICON'.
              gv_s_text = 'Tx'.
              lr_column->set_alignment( if_salv_c_alignment=>centered ).
              lr_column->set_icon( ).

            WHEN 'ENGINE_CLASSIF'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a17.
              gv_m_text = TEXT-a18.
              gv_s_text = TEXT-a19.
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).

            WHEN 'INDEX_OBJECT'.
              lr_column->set_technical( if_salv_c_bool_sap=>true ).

          ENDCASE.

          lr_column->set_short_text( gv_s_text ).
          lr_column->set_medium_text( gv_m_text ).
          lr_column->set_long_text( gv_l_text ).

        CATCH cx_salv_not_found.                        "#EC NO_HANDLER
      ENDTRY.
    ENDLOOP.

    gr_table403->display( ).
  ELSE.
    lr_display_settings = gr_table403->get_display_settings( ).
    lr_display_settings->set_list_header( gv_title ).
    gr_table403->refresh( ).
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form pbo_0500
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& PBO of screen 0500
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM pbo_0500 .

  DATA: lr_functions        TYPE REF TO cl_salv_functions_list,
        lr_display_settings TYPE REF TO cl_salv_display_settings,
        lr_layout           TYPE REF TO cl_salv_layout,
        lr_selections       TYPE REF TO cl_salv_selections,
        lr_events           TYPE REF TO lcl_handle_events,
        lr_table_events     TYPE REF TO cl_salv_events_table,
        lr_aggrs            TYPE REF TO cl_salv_aggregations,
        lr_column           TYPE REF TO cl_salv_column_table,
        lr_columns          TYPE REF TO cl_salv_columns_table,
        lt_columns          TYPE salv_t_column_ref,
        lv_title            TYPE lvc_title,
        lv_text             TYPE string,
        lv_icon             TYPE string,
        lv_tooltip          TYPE string,
        lv_display          TYPE boolean,
        lv_key              TYPE salv_s_layout_key.

  SET PF-STATUS ' '.

  IF gr_container500 IS NOT BOUND.
    IF cl_salv_table=>is_offline( ) EQ if_salv_c_bool_sap=>false.
      CREATE OBJECT gr_container500
        EXPORTING
          container_name = 'CONTAINER500'.
    ENDIF.

    TRY.
        cl_salv_table=>factory(
          EXPORTING
            r_container    = gr_container500
            container_name = 'CONTAINER500'
          IMPORTING
            r_salv_table   = gr_table500
          CHANGING
            t_table        = <gt_s4_role>  ).
      CATCH cx_salv_msg.                                "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    lr_functions = gr_table500->get_functions( ).
    lr_functions->set_all( 'X' ).

    " Title for saved datasets
    IF gv_valid_type = gc_valid_type-rules_n_results.
      CONCATENATE gs_info-sysid '/' gs_info-client INTO lv_text.
      CONDENSE lv_text NO-GAPS.

      WRITE gs_info-date TO lv_title LEFT-JUSTIFIED.
      CONCATENATE lv_text lv_title INTO lv_text SEPARATED BY space.

      WRITE gs_info-time TO lv_title LEFT-JUSTIFIED.
      CONCATENATE lv_text lv_title(5) INTO lv_text SEPARATED BY space.

      IF gs_info-version IS NOT INITIAL.
        CONCATENATE lv_text gs_info-version INTO lv_text SEPARATED BY space.
      ENDIF.

      CONCATENATE lv_text gs_info-ruleset INTO lv_text SEPARATED BY space.

      lv_title = lv_text.
    ELSE.
      lv_title = TEXT-t26.
    ENDIF.

    lr_display_settings = gr_table500->get_display_settings( ).
    lr_display_settings->set_list_header( lv_title ).
    lr_display_settings->set_striped_pattern( 'X' ).

    lr_selections = gr_table500->get_selections( ).
    lr_selections->set_selection_mode( if_salv_c_selection_mode=>multiple ).

    lv_text = TEXT-b01.
    lv_icon = icon_export.
    TRY.
        lr_functions->add_function(
          name     = '&EXP_RV'
          icon     = lv_icon
          text     = lv_text
          tooltip  = lv_text
          position = if_salv_c_function_position=>right_of_salv_functions ).
      CATCH cx_salv_existing cx_salv_wrong_call.        "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    lv_text = TEXT-b03.
    lv_icon = icon_export.
    TRY.
        lr_functions->add_function(
          name     = '&EXP_RV_SAP'
          icon     = lv_icon
          text     = lv_text
          tooltip  = lv_text
          position = if_salv_c_function_position=>right_of_salv_functions ).
      CATCH cx_salv_existing cx_salv_wrong_call.        "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    lv_text = TEXT-b05.
    lv_icon = icon_other_object.
    TRY.
        lr_functions->add_function(
          name     = '&ROLECLASS'
          icon     = lv_icon
          text     = lv_text
          tooltip  = lv_text
          position = if_salv_c_function_position=>right_of_salv_functions ).
      CATCH cx_salv_existing cx_salv_wrong_call.        "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    " Check whether the user is authorized to change the role classification
    AUTHORITY-CHECK OBJECT 'S_USER_AGR'
    ID 'ACT_GROUP' DUMMY
    ID 'ACTVT'     FIELD '02'.

    IF sy-subrc <> 0.
      " Disable the Transfer Function if the user is not authorized
      TRY.
          CALL METHOD lr_functions->enable_function
            EXPORTING
              name    = '&ROLECLASS'
              boolean = abap_false.

        CATCH cx_salv_wrong_call.
        CATCH cx_salv_not_found.
      ENDTRY.
    ENDIF.

    LOOP AT gt_user_data ASSIGNING <gs_user_data>.
      IF <gs_user_data>-roles IS NOT INITIAL.
        lv_display = 'X'.
        EXIT.
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.
    IF lv_display EQ 'X'.
      lv_text = TEXT-b02.
      lv_icon = icon_usergroup.
      TRY.
          lr_functions->add_function(
            name     = '&USERS'
            icon     = lv_icon
            text     = lv_text
            tooltip  = lv_text
            position = if_salv_c_function_position=>right_of_salv_functions ).
        CATCH cx_salv_existing cx_salv_wrong_call.      "#EC NO_HANDLER
      ENDTRY.
    ENDIF.

    lv_text    = TEXT-b06.
    lv_icon    = icon_toggle_display.
    TRY.
        lr_functions->add_function(
          name     = '&TOGGLE'
          icon     = lv_icon
          text     = lv_text
          tooltip  = lv_text
          position = if_salv_c_function_position=>right_of_salv_functions ).
      CATCH cx_salv_existing cx_salv_wrong_call.        "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

*    lv_text = TEXT-b07.
*    lv_icon = icon_graphics.
*    TRY.
*        lr_functions->add_function(
*          name     = '&GRAPHICS'
*          icon     = lv_icon
*          tooltip  = lv_text
*          position = if_salv_c_function_position=>right_of_salv_functions ).
*      CATCH cx_salv_existing cx_salv_wrong_call.        "#EC NO_HANDLER
*    ENDTRY.

    lv_icon    = icon_export.
    lv_tooltip = TEXT-tt8.
    TRY.
        lr_functions->add_function(
          name     = '&DETAILS'
          icon     = lv_icon
          tooltip  = lv_tooltip
          position = if_salv_c_function_position=>right_of_salv_functions ).
      CATCH cx_salv_existing cx_salv_wrong_call.        "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    lr_layout = gr_table500->get_layout( ).
    lv_key-report = sy-repid.
    lv_key-handle = sy-dynnr.
    lr_layout->set_key( lv_key ).
    lr_layout->set_save_restriction( ).

    lr_table_events = gr_table500->get_event( ).

    CREATE OBJECT lr_events.
    SET HANDLER lr_events->on_single_click_alv3 FOR lr_table_events.
    SET HANDLER lr_events->on_user_command FOR lr_table_events.

    lr_columns = gr_table500->get_columns( ).
    lt_columns = lr_columns->get( ).
    lr_columns->set_optimize( 'X' ).

    lr_aggrs = gr_table500->get_aggregations( ).
    lr_aggrs->set_aggregation_before_items( ).

    PERFORM get_table_components USING gt_s4_role
                              CHANGING gt_struct_components.

    LOOP AT lt_columns ASSIGNING <gs_column>.
      TRY.
          lr_column ?= lr_columns->get_column( <gs_column>-columnname ).
          CLEAR: gv_l_text, gv_m_text, gv_s_text.
          CASE <gs_column>-columnname.

            WHEN 'REFERENCED'.
              lr_column->set_technical( 'X' ).

            WHEN 'COUNT'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a30.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).

            WHEN 'OBJECT_COUNT'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a07.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).

            WHEN 'RATIO'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a03.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
              lr_column->set_alignment( if_salv_c_alignment=>centered ).
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).

            WHEN 'CLASSIF_S4'. " Target Classification
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a01.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).

            WHEN 'CLASSIF_CURR'. " Current Role Classification
              IF lines( gt_agr_flags ) = 0.
                lr_column->set_technical( 'X' ).
              ELSE.
                gv_s_text = TEXT-a10.
                gv_m_text = TEXT-a11.
                gv_l_text = TEXT-a12.
              ENDIF.

            WHEN 'ENGINE' OR 'TYPE'. " Engine Indicator / Role Type
              lr_column->set_technical( ).

            WHEN 'USER_NUMBERS'.
              gv_l_text = gv_m_text = gv_s_text = TEXT-a05.
              lr_column->set_cell_type( if_salv_c_cell_type=>hotspot ).

            WHEN 'AGR_NAME' OR
                 'AGR_TEXT' OR
                 'AUTH'     OR
                 'PTEXT'.
              READ TABLE gt_struct_components ASSIGNING <gs_struct_components>
                WITH KEY name = <gs_column>-columnname.
              IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
                go_elem_descr ?= <gs_struct_components>-type.
                CLEAR gs_flddescr.
                gs_flddescr = go_elem_descr->get_ddic_field( ).

                gv_l_text = gs_flddescr-scrtext_l.
                gv_m_text = gs_flddescr-scrtext_m.
                gv_s_text = gs_flddescr-scrtext_s.
              ENDIF.

              IF <gs_column>-columnname EQ 'AGR_NAME' OR
                 <gs_column>-columnname EQ 'AUTH'.
                lr_column->set_cell_type( if_salv_c_cell_type=>hotspot ).
              ENDIF.

            WHEN OTHERS.
              " Engine columns
              lr_column->set_zero( abap_false ).
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).

              TRY.
                  CALL METHOD lr_aggrs->add_aggregation
                    EXPORTING
                      columnname  = <gs_column>-columnname
                      aggregation = if_salv_c_aggregation=>total.
                CATCH cx_salv_data_error .              "#EC NO_HANDLER
                CATCH cx_salv_not_found .               "#EC NO_HANDLER
                CATCH cx_salv_existing .                "#EC NO_HANDLER
              ENDTRY.

              READ TABLE gt_engine_fields ASSIGNING <gs_engine_fields>
                WITH KEY fname = <gs_column>-columnname.
              IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
                gv_l_text = <gs_engine_fields>-text.
              ELSE.
                gv_l_text = <gs_column>-columnname.
              ENDIF.

          ENDCASE.

          lr_column->set_short_text( gv_s_text ).
          lr_column->set_medium_text( gv_m_text ).
          lr_column->set_long_text( gv_l_text ).

        CATCH cx_salv_not_found.                        "#EC NO_HANDLER
      ENDTRY.
    ENDLOOP.

    gr_table500->display( ).
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form pbo_0501
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& PBO of screen 0501
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM pbo_0501 .

  DATA: lr_functions        TYPE REF TO cl_salv_functions_list,
        lr_layout           TYPE REF TO cl_salv_layout,
        lr_display_settings TYPE REF TO cl_salv_display_settings,
        lo_sorts            TYPE REF TO cl_salv_sorts,
        lr_column           TYPE REF TO cl_salv_column_table,
        lr_columns          TYPE REF TO cl_salv_columns_table,
        lt_columns          TYPE salv_t_column_ref,
        ls_role_users       LIKE LINE OF gt_role_users,
        lv_key              TYPE salv_s_layout_key.


  IF gr_container501 IS NOT BOUND.
    IF cl_salv_table=>is_offline( ) EQ if_salv_c_bool_sap=>false.
      CREATE OBJECT gr_container501
        EXPORTING
          container_name = 'CONTAINER501'.
    ENDIF.
    TRY.
        cl_salv_table=>factory(
          EXPORTING
            r_container    = gr_container501
            container_name = 'CONTAINER501'
          IMPORTING
            r_salv_table = gr_table501
          CHANGING
            t_table      = gt_role_users ).
      CATCH cx_salv_msg.                                "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    lr_functions = gr_table501->get_functions( ).
    lr_functions->set_all( 'X' ).

    lr_display_settings = gr_table501->get_display_settings( ).
    lr_display_settings->set_list_header( gv_title ).
    lr_display_settings->set_striped_pattern( 'X' ).

    lr_layout = gr_table501->get_layout( ).
    lv_key-report = sy-repid.
    lv_key-handle = sy-dynnr.
    lr_layout->set_key( lv_key ).
    lr_layout->set_save_restriction( ).

    lo_sorts = gr_table501->get_sorts( ).
    TRY.
        lo_sorts->add_sort(
                  EXPORTING
                    columnname = 'BNAME'
                    sequence   = if_salv_c_sort=>sort_up ).
      CATCH cx_salv_not_found.                          "#EC NO_HANDLER
      CATCH cx_salv_existing.                           "#EC NO_HANDLER
      CATCH cx_salv_data_error.                         "#EC NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

    lr_columns = gr_table501->get_columns( ).
    lt_columns = lr_columns->get( ).
    lr_columns->set_optimize( 'X' ).

    PERFORM get_table_components USING gt_role_users
                              CHANGING gt_struct_components.

    LOOP AT lt_columns ASSIGNING <gs_column>.
      TRY.
          lr_column ?= lr_columns->get_column( <gs_column>-columnname ).
          CLEAR: gv_l_text, gv_m_text, gv_s_text.
          CASE <gs_column>-columnname.

            WHEN 'COUNT'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a30.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).

            WHEN 'BNAME'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a08.
              gv_m_text = TEXT-a08.
              gv_s_text = TEXT-a08.

            WHEN 'HASH_BNAME'.
              gv_l_text = TEXT-a13.
              lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
              lr_column->set_optimized( ).

              " Check whether hashed user IDs are included.
              LOOP AT gt_role_users TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS WHERE hash_bname <> ' '.
                EXIT.
              ENDLOOP.
              IF sy-subrc <> 0.
                " If not, we can hide the column
                lr_column->set_visible( abap_false ).
              ENDIF.

            WHEN  'NAME_TEXT'.
              READ TABLE gt_struct_components ASSIGNING <gs_struct_components>
                WITH KEY name = <gs_column>-columnname.
              IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
                go_elem_descr ?= <gs_struct_components>-type.
                CLEAR gs_flddescr.
                gs_flddescr = go_elem_descr->get_ddic_field( ).

                gv_l_text = gs_flddescr-scrtext_l.
                gv_m_text = gs_flddescr-scrtext_m.
                gv_s_text = gs_flddescr-scrtext_s.
              ENDIF.

            WHEN 'CLASSIF_S4'.
              LOOP AT gt_role_users INTO ls_role_users WHERE classif_s4 <> ''.
              ENDLOOP.

              IF sy-subrc <> 0.
                lr_column->set_technical( if_salv_c_bool_sap=>true ).
              ELSE.
                gv_l_text = TEXT-a01.
                gv_m_text = TEXT-a01.
                gv_s_text = TEXT-a02.
              ENDIF.

            WHEN 'CLASSIF_CURR'.
              lr_column->set_technical( if_salv_c_bool_sap=>true ).

            WHEN 'RATIO'.
              LOOP AT gt_role_users INTO ls_role_users WHERE ratio <> ''.
              ENDLOOP.

              IF sy-subrc <> 0.
                lr_column->set_technical( if_salv_c_bool_sap=>true ).
              ELSE.
                gv_l_text = TEXT-a03.
                lr_column->set_fixed_header_text( 'L' ).
                lr_column->set_alignment( if_salv_c_alignment=>centered ).
                lr_column->set_optimized( ).
              ENDIF.

          ENDCASE.

          lr_column->set_short_text( gv_s_text ).
          lr_column->set_medium_text( gv_m_text ).
          lr_column->set_long_text( gv_l_text ).

        CATCH cx_salv_not_found.                        "#EC NO_HANDLER
      ENDTRY.
    ENDLOOP.

    gr_table501->display( ).
  ELSE.
    lr_display_settings = gr_table501->get_display_settings( ).
    lr_display_settings->set_list_header( gv_title ).
    gr_table501->refresh( ).
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form reassign_role_valid_objects
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Technical routine for re-assigning of internal indicies when Role
*& validaton data is downloaded for SAP
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM reassign_role_valid_objects .

  CLEAR: gt_role_result_rv, gt_object_result_rv.

  " New Roles/Objects data-only for selected Roles/Profiles
  LOOP AT gt_role_data ASSIGNING <gs_role_data>.
    READ TABLE gt_role_result ASSIGNING <gs_role_result>
      INDEX <gs_role_data>-index_role.
    IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
      INSERT <gs_role_result> INTO TABLE gt_role_result_rv.

      LOOP AT <gs_role_result>-objects ASSIGNING <gs_objects>.
        READ TABLE gt_object_result ASSIGNING <gs_object_result>
          INDEX <gs_objects>-index_object.
        IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
          INSERT <gs_object_result> INTO TABLE gt_object_result_rv.
        ENDIF.
      ENDLOOP.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.

  " Re-assign indicies
  LOOP AT gt_role_data ASSIGNING <gs_role_data>.
    READ TABLE gt_role_result_rv ASSIGNING <gs_role_result>
      WITH TABLE KEY agr_name = <gs_role_data>-agr_name
                     auth = <gs_role_data>-auth.
    IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
      <gs_role_data>-index_role = sy-tabix.
      LOOP AT <gs_role_result>-objects ASSIGNING <gs_objects>.
        READ TABLE gt_object_result_rv TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS
          WITH TABLE KEY object = <gs_objects>-object
                         field  = <gs_objects>-field
                         low    = <gs_objects>-low
                         high   = <gs_objects>-high.
        IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
          <gs_objects>-index_object = sy-tabix.
        ENDIF.
      ENDLOOP.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form get_system_info
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Get system details
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM get_system_info .
  CLEAR: gv_install_number, gv_sysid.

  CALL FUNCTION 'SLIC_GET_LICENCE_NUMBER'
    IMPORTING
      license_number = gv_install_number.

  CONCATENATE sy-sysid sy-mandt INTO gv_sysid SEPARATED BY '/'.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form password_request
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Password for encryption/decryption
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> CV_ERROR      Error flag
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM password_request CHANGING cv_error TYPE boolean.
  DATA: lv_key TYPE string.

  CLEAR: p_pwde, p_pwdc.
  CALL SELECTION-SCREEN 2000 STARTING AT 20 5.
  IF sy-subrc NE 0.
    CLEAR: p_pwde, p_pwdc.
    cv_error = 'X'.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  " Generate a key for encryption
  IF p_pwde IS NOT INITIAL.
    lv_key = p_pwde.
    PERFORM generate_key USING lv_key.
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form generate_key
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Generate a key for encryption/decryption
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PV_KEY      Source data
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM generate_key USING pv_key  TYPE string.

  " Use proper encryption key length for XSTRING key field
  " It will be:
  " for AES128 - 32 chars
  " for AES192 - 48 chars
  " for AES256 - 64 chars
  DATA: lv_key  TYPE c LENGTH 32. " here we use AES128

  CLEAR gv_key.

  lv_key =  pv_key.

  CLEAR go_conv_xstr.
  TRY.
      go_conv_xstr = cl_abap_conv_out_ce=>create( ignore_cerr = 'X' ).
      go_conv_xstr->write( data = lv_key ).
      gv_key = go_conv_xstr->get_buffer( ).
    CATCH cx_root. "##NO_HANDLER.
  ENDTRY.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form hash_data
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Hash Data
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PV_BNAME       User
*&      <-- CV_HASH_BNAME  Hashed data
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM hash_data  USING    VALUE(pv_bname)
                CHANGING VALUE(cv_hash_bname).
  DATA: lv_data          TYPE string,
        lv_algorithm     TYPE string VALUE gc_hash_algorithm,
        lv_keyx          TYPE xstring,
        lv_hmacb64string TYPE string.

  CLEAR cv_hash_bname.
  lv_data = pv_bname.

  TRY.
      CALL METHOD cl_abap_hmac=>calculate_hmac_for_char
        EXPORTING
          if_algorithm     = lv_algorithm
          if_key           = lv_keyx
          if_data          = lv_data
        IMPORTING
          ef_hmacb64string = lv_hmacb64string.
    CATCH cx_abap_message_digest.
      cv_hash_bname = pv_bname.
      RETURN.
  ENDTRY.

  cv_hash_bname = lv_hmacb64string.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form add_header
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Header data for dataset
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PV_DATASET_TYPE Dataset type
*&      <-- CT_DATASET      Dataset
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM add_header  USING VALUE(pv_dataset_type)
              CHANGING ct_dataset TYPE gty_t_dataset.

  DATA: lv_timestamp TYPE timestamp.

  " Technical information about a dataset type
  APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_dataset ASSIGNING <gs_dataset>.
  <gs_dataset>-bname = pv_dataset_type.
  " Technical information with system details
  APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_dataset ASSIGNING <gs_dataset>.
  CONCATENATE gv_install_number gv_sysid
    INTO <gs_dataset>-bname SEPARATED BY ';'.
  " Timestamp of a dataset
  GET TIME STAMP FIELD lv_timestamp.
  <gs_dataset>-classif_s4 = lv_timestamp.
  CONDENSE <gs_dataset>-classif_s4.
  " Dataset version
  <gs_dataset>-classif_curr = gc_dataset_ver.

  " Note version
  PERFORM get_note_version CHANGING <gs_dataset>-name_text.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form add_user_engines
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Add User Engines
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM add_user_engines .

  DATA: ls_engines      TYPE gty_engines,
        ls_user_engines TYPE gty_user_engines.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_roles>   TYPE gty_user_role,
                 <ls_engines> TYPE gty_engines.

  CLEAR gt_engines.
  " Collect Engine objects
  LOOP AT <gs_user_data>-roles ASSIGNING <ls_roles>.
    READ TABLE gt_role_result ASSIGNING <gs_role_result>
      INDEX <ls_roles>-index_role.
    IF sy-subrc EQ 0 AND <gs_role_result>-engine EQ 'X'.
      LOOP AT <gs_role_result>-objects ASSIGNING <gs_objects>.
        READ TABLE gt_object_result ASSIGNING <gs_object_result>
          INDEX <gs_objects>-index_object.
        IF sy-subrc EQ 0 AND <gs_object_result>-engine_priority IS NOT INITIAL.
          CLEAR ls_engines.
          MOVE-CORRESPONDING <gs_object_result> TO ls_engines.
          INSERT ls_engines INTO TABLE gt_engines.
        ENDIF.
      ENDLOOP.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.
  " Assign Engine objects to User
  LOOP AT gt_engines ASSIGNING <ls_engines>.
    CLEAR ls_user_engines.
    ls_user_engines-bname = <gs_user_data>-bname.
    MOVE-CORRESPONDING <ls_engines> TO ls_user_engines.
    INSERT ls_user_engines INTO TABLE gt_user_engines.

    " Collect Engines as fields for dynamic table creation
    APPEND INITIAL LINE TO gt_engine_fields ASSIGNING <gs_engine_fields>.
    <gs_engine_fields>-fname = <ls_engines>-engine_priority.
    <gs_engine_fields>-text  = <ls_engines>-engine_classif.
  ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form add_role_engines
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Add Role Engines
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM add_role_engines USING pv_agr_name   TYPE c " agr_name
                            pv_auth       TYPE c " xuauth
                            pv_index_role TYPE sytabix.

  DATA: ls_engines      TYPE gty_engines,
        ls_role_engines TYPE gty_role_engines.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_engines> TYPE gty_engines.

  CLEAR gt_engines.

  READ TABLE gt_role_result ASSIGNING <gs_role_result>
    INDEX pv_index_role.
  IF sy-subrc EQ 0 AND <gs_role_result>-engine EQ 'X'.
    LOOP AT <gs_role_result>-objects ASSIGNING <gs_objects>.
      READ TABLE gt_object_result ASSIGNING <gs_object_result>
        INDEX <gs_objects>-index_object.
      IF sy-subrc EQ 0 AND <gs_object_result>-engine_priority IS NOT INITIAL.
        CLEAR ls_engines.
        MOVE-CORRESPONDING <gs_object_result> TO ls_engines.
        INSERT ls_engines INTO TABLE gt_engines.
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.
  ENDIF.

  " Assign Engine objects to Role
  LOOP AT gt_engines ASSIGNING <ls_engines>.
    CLEAR ls_role_engines.
    ls_role_engines-agr_name = pv_agr_name.
    ls_role_engines-auth     = pv_auth.
    MOVE-CORRESPONDING <ls_engines> TO ls_role_engines.
    INSERT ls_role_engines INTO TABLE gt_role_engines.

    " Collect Engines as fields for dynamic table creation
    APPEND INITIAL LINE TO gt_engine_fields ASSIGNING <gs_engine_fields>.
    <gs_engine_fields>-fname = <ls_engines>-engine_priority.
    <gs_engine_fields>-text  = <ls_engines>-engine_classif.
  ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form prepare_user_classif_fields
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Prepare fields for dynamic table creation for User classification ALV
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      <-- CT_FIELD_CAT Field catalog
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM prepare_user_classif_fields  CHANGING ct_field_cat TYPE lvc_t_fcat.

  DATA: lv_col_pos TYPE lvc_colpos.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_field_cat> TYPE lvc_s_fcat.

  SORT gt_engine_fields BY fname.
  DELETE ADJACENT DUPLICATES FROM gt_engine_fields COMPARING fname.

  ADD 1 TO lv_col_pos.
  APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_field_cat ASSIGNING <ls_field_cat>.
  <ls_field_cat>-fieldname = 'BNAME'.
  <ls_field_cat>-inttype   = 'C'.
  <ls_field_cat>-intlen    = 24.
  <ls_field_cat>-col_pos   = lv_col_pos.
  <ls_field_cat>-key       = 'X'.

  ADD 1 TO lv_col_pos.
  APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_field_cat ASSIGNING <ls_field_cat>.
  <ls_field_cat>-fieldname = 'NAME_TEXT'.
  <ls_field_cat>-inttype   = 'C'.
  <ls_field_cat>-intlen    = 80.
  <ls_field_cat>-ref_table = 'ADRP'.
  <ls_field_cat>-ref_field = 'NAME_TEXT'.
  <ls_field_cat>-col_pos   = lv_col_pos.

  ADD 1 TO lv_col_pos.
  APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_field_cat ASSIGNING <ls_field_cat>.
  <ls_field_cat>-fieldname = 'HASH_BNAME'.
  <ls_field_cat>-inttype   = 'C'.
  <ls_field_cat>-intlen    = 24.
  <ls_field_cat>-col_pos   = lv_col_pos.
  <ls_field_cat>-key       = 'X'.

  ADD 1 TO lv_col_pos.
  APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_field_cat ASSIGNING <ls_field_cat>.
  <ls_field_cat>-fieldname = 'LIC_TYPE'.
  <ls_field_cat>-inttype   = 'C'.
  <ls_field_cat>-intlen    = 2.
  <ls_field_cat>-ref_table = 'TUTYP'.
  <ls_field_cat>-ref_field = 'USERTYP'.
  <ls_field_cat>-col_pos   = lv_col_pos.

  ADD 1 TO lv_col_pos.
  APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_field_cat ASSIGNING <ls_field_cat>.
  <ls_field_cat>-fieldname = 'CLASSIF_CURR'.
  <ls_field_cat>-inttype   = 'C'.
  <ls_field_cat>-intlen    = 55.
  <ls_field_cat>-ref_table = 'TUTYP'.
  <ls_field_cat>-ref_field = 'UTYPLONGTEXT'.
  <ls_field_cat>-col_pos   = lv_col_pos.

  ADD 1 TO lv_col_pos.
  APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_field_cat ASSIGNING <ls_field_cat>.
  <ls_field_cat>-fieldname = 'CLASSIF_S4'.
  <ls_field_cat>-inttype   = 'C'.
  <ls_field_cat>-intlen    = 40.
  <ls_field_cat>-ref_table = 'LVC_S_FUNC'.
  <ls_field_cat>-ref_field = 'TEXT'.
  <ls_field_cat>-col_pos   = lv_col_pos.

  ADD 1 TO lv_col_pos.
  APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_field_cat ASSIGNING <ls_field_cat>.
  <ls_field_cat>-fieldname = 'RATIO'.
  <ls_field_cat>-inttype   = 'C'.
  <ls_field_cat>-intlen    = 10.
  <ls_field_cat>-col_pos   = lv_col_pos.

  ADD 1 TO lv_col_pos.
  APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_field_cat ASSIGNING <ls_field_cat>.
  <ls_field_cat>-fieldname = 'REFUSER'.
  <ls_field_cat>-inttype   = 'C'.
  <ls_field_cat>-intlen    = 24.
  <ls_field_cat>-col_pos   = lv_col_pos.

  ADD 1 TO lv_col_pos.
  APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_field_cat ASSIGNING <ls_field_cat>.
  <ls_field_cat>-fieldname = 'CLASS'.
  <ls_field_cat>-inttype   = 'C'.
  <ls_field_cat>-intlen    = 12.
  <ls_field_cat>-col_pos   = lv_col_pos.

  ADD 1 TO lv_col_pos.
  APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_field_cat ASSIGNING <ls_field_cat>.
  <ls_field_cat>-fieldname = 'TRDAT'.
  <ls_field_cat>-inttype   = 'D'.
  <ls_field_cat>-intlen    = 10.
  <ls_field_cat>-col_pos   = lv_col_pos.

  ADD 1 TO lv_col_pos.
  APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_field_cat ASSIGNING <ls_field_cat>.
  <ls_field_cat>-fieldname = 'COUNT'.
  <ls_field_cat>-inttype   = 'I'.
  <ls_field_cat>-col_pos   = lv_col_pos.

  " Engine columns there
  LOOP AT gt_engine_fields ASSIGNING <gs_engine_fields>.
    ADD 1 TO lv_col_pos.
    APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_field_cat ASSIGNING <ls_field_cat>.
    <ls_field_cat>-fieldname = <gs_engine_fields>-fname.
    <ls_field_cat>-inttype   = 'I'.
    <ls_field_cat>-col_pos   = lv_col_pos.
  ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form prepare_hashed_users
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Prepare a hashed value for UserID
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM prepare_hashed_users .
  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_users,
           bname TYPE xubname,
         END OF lty_users.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_usr021,
           bname      TYPE xubname,
           persnumber TYPE ad_persnum,
         END OF lty_usr021.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_persnumber,
           persnumber TYPE ad_persnum,
         END OF lty_persnumber.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_adrp,
           persnumber TYPE ad_persnum,
           name_first TYPE ad_namefir,
           name_last  TYPE ad_namelas,
         END OF lty_adrp.

  DATA: lt_users      TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF lty_users,
        lr_bname      TYPE RANGE OF bname,
        lt_usr021     TYPE SORTED TABLE OF lty_usr021 WITH UNIQUE KEY bname,
        lt_persnumber TYPE SORTED TABLE OF lty_persnumber WITH UNIQUE KEY persnumber,
        ls_persnumber TYPE lty_persnumber,
        lt_adrp       TYPE SORTED TABLE OF lty_adrp WITH UNIQUE KEY persnumber,
        ls_hash_users TYPE gty_hash_users.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_users>  TYPE lty_users,
                 <ls_usr021> TYPE lty_usr021,
                 <ls_adrp>   TYPE lty_adrp.

  CLEAR gt_hash_users.

  SELECT bname
    INTO TABLE lt_users
    FROM usr01
   WHERE bname IN lr_bname.                             "#EC CI_GENBUFF

  IF lt_users IS NOT INITIAL.
    SELECT bname
           persnumber
      FROM usr21
      INTO TABLE lt_usr021
        FOR ALL ENTRIES IN lt_users
     WHERE bname EQ lt_users-bname.                "#EC CI_NO_TRANSFORM
  ENDIF.

  LOOP AT lt_usr021 ASSIGNING <ls_usr021>.
    ls_persnumber-persnumber = <ls_usr021>-persnumber.
    INSERT ls_persnumber INTO TABLE lt_persnumber.
  ENDLOOP.

  IF lt_persnumber IS NOT INITIAL.
    SELECT persnumber
           name_first
           name_last
      FROM adrp
      INTO TABLE lt_adrp
        FOR ALL ENTRIES IN lt_persnumber
     WHERE persnumber EQ lt_persnumber-persnumber
       AND date_from  EQ gc_date_from
       AND nation     EQ space.                    "#EC CI_NO_TRANSFORM
  ENDIF.

  LOOP AT lt_users ASSIGNING <ls_users>.
    CLEAR ls_hash_users.
    PERFORM hash_data USING <ls_users>-bname
                   CHANGING ls_hash_users-hash_bname.
    ls_hash_users-bname = <ls_users>-bname.
    READ TABLE lt_usr021 ASSIGNING <ls_usr021>
      WITH TABLE KEY bname = <ls_users>-bname.
    IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
      READ TABLE lt_adrp ASSIGNING <ls_adrp>
        WITH KEY persnumber = <ls_usr021>-persnumber.
      IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
        CONCATENATE <ls_adrp>-name_first <ls_adrp>-name_last
         INTO ls_hash_users-name_text SEPARATED BY space.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.

    INSERT ls_hash_users INTO TABLE gt_hash_users.
  ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form prepare_role_classif_fields
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*

*&      --> PV_VALID_TYPE Validation type

  <ls_field_cat>-intlen    = 80.
  <ls_field_cat>-col_pos   = lv_col_pos.
  <ls_field_cat>-ref_table = 'AGR_TEXTS'.
  <ls_field_cat>-ref_field = 'TEXT'.

  ADD 1 TO lv_col_pos.
  APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_field_cat ASSIGNING <ls_field_cat>.

  <ls_field_cat>-inttype   = 'C'.
  <ls_field_cat>-col_pos   = lv_col_pos.

  ADD 1 TO lv_col_pos.
  APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_field_cat ASSIGNING <ls_field_cat>.
  <ls_field_cat>-fieldname = 'TYPE'.
  <ls_field_cat>-inttype   = 'C'.
  <ls_field_cat>-intlen    = 1.
  <ls_field_cat>-col_pos   = lv_col_pos.

  ADD 1 TO lv_col_pos.
  APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_field_cat ASSIGNING <ls_field_cat>.
  <ls_field_cat>-fieldname = 'CLASSIF_CURR'.
  <ls_field_cat>-inttype   = 'C'.
  <ls_field_cat>-intlen    = 60.
  <ls_field_cat>-ref_table = 'TUTYP'.
  <ls_field_cat>-ref_field = 'UTYPLONGTEXT'.
  <ls_field_cat>-col_pos   = lv_col_pos.

  ADD 1 TO lv_col_pos.
  APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_field_cat ASSIGNING <ls_field_cat>.
  <ls_field_cat>-fieldname = 'CLASSIF_S4'.
  <ls_field_cat>-inttype   = 'C'.
  <ls_field_cat>-intlen    = 40.
  <ls_field_cat>-ref_table = 'LVC_S_FUNC'.
  <ls_field_cat>-ref_field = 'TEXT'.
  <ls_field_cat>-col_pos   = lv_col_pos.

  ADD 1 TO lv_col_pos.
  APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_field_cat ASSIGNING <ls_field_cat>.
  <ls_field_cat>-fieldname = 'ENGINE'.
  <ls_field_cat>-inttype   = 'C'.
  <ls_field_cat>-intlen    = 1.
  <ls_field_cat>-col_pos   = lv_col_pos.

  ADD 1 TO lv_col_pos.
  APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_field_cat ASSIGNING <ls_field_cat>.
  <ls_field_cat>-fieldname = 'RATIO'.
  <ls_field_cat>-inttype   = 'C'.
  <ls_field_cat>-intlen    = 20.
  <ls_field_cat>-col_pos   = lv_col_pos.

  ADD 1 TO lv_col_pos.
  APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_field_cat ASSIGNING <ls_field_cat>.
  <ls_field_cat>-fieldname = 'OBJECT_COUNT'.
  <ls_field_cat>-inttype   = 'I'.
  <ls_field_cat>-col_pos   = lv_col_pos.

  ADD 1 TO lv_col_pos.
  APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_field_cat ASSIGNING <ls_field_cat>.
  <ls_field_cat>-fieldname = 'COUNT'.
  <ls_field_cat>-inttype   = 'I'.
  <ls_field_cat>-col_pos   = lv_col_pos.

  " Engine columns there
  LOOP AT gt_engine_fields ASSIGNING <gs_engine_fields>.
    ADD 1 TO lv_col_pos.
    APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_field_cat ASSIGNING <ls_field_cat>.
    <ls_field_cat>-fieldname = <gs_engine_fields>-fname.
    <ls_field_cat>-inttype   = 'I'.

  ENDLOOP.

  ADD 1 TO lv_col_pos.

  IF pv_valid_type EQ gc_valid_type-user_validation.
    <ls_field_cat>-fieldname = 'TOTAL_USR'.
