  <ls_field_cat>-inttype   = 'I'.
  <ls_field_cat>-col_pos   = lv_col_pos.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form encrypt_dataset
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Dataset encryption
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PV_DATA       Source data
*&      <-- CV_DATA_ENCR  Encrypted data
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM encrypt_dataset  USING pv_data      TYPE xstring
                   CHANGING cv_data_encr TYPE xstring.

  CLEAR cv_data_encr.

  " Encrypt source value
  TRY.
      CALL METHOD cl_sec_sxml_writer=>encrypt
        EXPORTING
          plaintext  = pv_data
          key        = gv_key
          algorithm  = gc_algorithm
        IMPORTING
          ciphertext = cv_data_encr.
    CATCH cx_sec_sxml_encrypt_error.
      cv_data_encr = pv_data.
  ENDTRY.

  CLEAR: gv_key.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form decrypt_dataset
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Dataset decryption
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PV_DATA_ENCR    Encrypted data
*&      <-- CV_DATA         Decrypted data
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM decrypt_dataset  USING pv_data_encr TYPE xstring
                   CHANGING cv_data      TYPE xstring.

  CLEAR cv_data.
  " Decrypt source value
  TRY.
      cl_sec_sxml_writer=>decrypt(
        EXPORTING
          ciphertext = pv_data_encr
          key        = gv_key
          algorithm  = gc_algorithm
        IMPORTING
          plaintext =  cv_data ).
    CATCH cx_sec_sxml_encrypt_error.
      cv_data = pv_data_encr.
  ENDTRY.

  CLEAR gv_key.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form compress_data
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Compress downloaded data
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PT_DATASET       Dataset
*&      <-- CT_DATASET_COMP  Compressed data
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM compress_data  USING    pt_dataset      TYPE gty_t_dataset
                    CHANGING pt_dataset_comp TYPE stringtab.

  DATA: lv_row   TYPE string,
        lv_bname TYPE string.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_field> TYPE any.

  LOOP AT pt_dataset ASSIGNING <gs_dataset>.
    CLEAR lv_row.

    DO.
      ASSIGN COMPONENT sy-index OF STRUCTURE <gs_dataset> TO <ls_field>.
      IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
        IF sy-index EQ 1.
          " do not compress UserID
          CONCATENATE <gs_dataset>-bname gc_field_separator
            INTO lv_bname RESPECTING BLANKS.
        ELSE.
          IF sy-index EQ 2.
            lv_row = <ls_field>.
          ELSE.
            CONCATENATE lv_row gc_field_separator <ls_field> INTO lv_row.
          ENDIF.
        ENDIF.
      ELSE.
        EXIT.
      ENDIF.

    ENDDO.

    CONCATENATE lv_bname lv_row INTO lv_row.
    APPEND lv_row TO pt_dataset_comp.

  ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form uncompress_dataset
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Convert uploaded data to dataset fromat
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> LT_DATASET_COMP Uploaded data
*&      <-- CT_DATASET      Dataset
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM uncompress_dataset  USING    pt_dataset_comp TYPE stringtab
                         CHANGING ct_dataset      TYPE gty_t_dataset.

  DATA: lv_bname(24) TYPE c,
        lt_fields    TYPE stringtab.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_row>   TYPE string,
                 <ls_field> TYPE string,
                 <lv_value> TYPE any.

  " Convert data to target dataset format
  LOOP AT pt_dataset_comp ASSIGNING <ls_row>.
    APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_dataset ASSIGNING <gs_dataset>.
    " UserID(in case of a hashed value) might have a character
    " that is used as a separator below
    " to prevent a wrong data splitting take a UserID value
    " before splitting and clear it value
    CLEAR lv_bname.
    lv_bname = <ls_row>(gc_user_length).
    SHIFT <ls_row> LEFT BY gc_user_length PLACES.

    CLEAR lt_fields.
    SPLIT <ls_row> AT gc_field_separator INTO TABLE lt_fields.

    LOOP AT lt_fields ASSIGNING <ls_field>.
      ASSIGN COMPONENT sy-tabix OF STRUCTURE <gs_dataset> TO <lv_value>.
      IF sy-subrc = 0.
        <lv_value> = <ls_field>.
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.

    <gs_dataset>-bname = lv_bname.

  ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form import_ruleset
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Import the ruleset from the file system
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM import_ruleset USING    iv_file  TYPE text255
                    CHANGING ct_rules TYPE gty_t_rules_file.

  DATA: lv_filename      TYPE string,
        lt_records       TYPE solix_tab,
        lv_headerxstring TYPE xstring,
        lv_filelength    TYPE i.

  DATA: lo_excel_ref  TYPE REF TO cl_fdt_xl_spreadsheet,
        lo_data_ref   TYPE REF TO data,
        lt_worksheets TYPE if_fdt_doc_spreadsheet=>t_worksheet_names,
        ls_worksheet  LIKE LINE OF lt_worksheets.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <lt_data>  TYPE STANDARD TABLE,
                 <ls_data>  TYPE any,
                 <lv_field> TYPE any,
                 <ls_rule>  LIKE LINE OF ct_rules.

  REFRESH ct_rules.

  CHECK iv_file IS NOT INITIAL.

  lv_filename = iv_file.

  " ... if there's no ruleset yet, we load the ruleset
  CLEAR gv_percent.
  PERFORM show_indicator USING TEXT-t14 gv_percent.

  " Upload the selected file
  CALL FUNCTION 'GUI_UPLOAD'
    EXPORTING
      filename                = lv_filename
      filetype                = 'BIN'
    IMPORTING
      filelength              = lv_filelength
      header                  = lv_headerxstring
    TABLES
      data_tab                = lt_records
    EXCEPTIONS
      file_open_error         = 1
      file_read_error         = 2
      no_batch                = 3
      gui_refuse_filetransfer = 4
      invalid_type            = 5
      no_authority            = 6
      unknown_error           = 7
      bad_data_format         = 8
      header_not_allowed      = 9
      separator_not_allowed   = 10
      header_too_long         = 11
      unknown_dp_error        = 12
      access_denied           = 13
      dp_out_of_memory        = 14
      disk_full               = 15
      dp_timeout              = 16
      OTHERS                  = 17.

  IF sy-subrc <> 0.
    CASE sy-subrc.
      WHEN 6.
        " File could not be imported
        MESSAGE 'You are not authorized to import the ruleset (S_GUI/ACTVT/60)'(e14) TYPE 'I'.

      WHEN OTHERS.
        " File could not be imported
        MESSAGE 'File could not be imported'(e11) TYPE 'I'.

    ENDCASE.

    REFRESH ct_rules.
    FREE MEMORY ID 'RULESET'.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  " Convert binary data to xstring
  CALL FUNCTION 'SCMS_BINARY_TO_XSTRING'
    EXPORTING
      input_length = lv_filelength
    IMPORTING
      buffer       = lv_headerxstring
    TABLES
      binary_tab   = lt_records
    EXCEPTIONS
      failed       = 1
      OTHERS       = 2.

  IF sy-subrc <> 0.
    " File could not be converted
    MESSAGE 'Binary data could not be converted'(e12) TYPE 'I'.
    REFRESH ct_rules.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  TRY.
      CREATE OBJECT lo_excel_ref
        EXPORTING
          document_name = lv_filename
          xdocument     = lv_headerxstring.

    CATCH cx_fdt_excel_core.
      " Object could not be created
      MESSAGE 'Excel object could not be created'(e13) TYPE 'I'.
      REFRESH ct_rules.
      RETURN.
  ENDTRY.

  " Get List of Worksheets
  lo_excel_ref->if_fdt_doc_spreadsheet~get_worksheet_names(
                IMPORTING
                  worksheet_names = lt_worksheets ).

  IF NOT lt_worksheets IS INITIAL.
    " Use the data from the first sheet
    READ TABLE lt_worksheets INTO ls_worksheet INDEX 1.

    lo_data_ref = lo_excel_ref->if_fdt_doc_spreadsheet~get_itab_from_worksheet(
                                             ls_worksheet ).
    " Data from the excel work sheet is in the internal dynamic table now
    ASSIGN lo_data_ref->* TO <lt_data>.
  ENDIF.

  IF lines( <lt_data> ) = 0.
    " No valid ruleset file selected
    MESSAGE TEXT-e08 TYPE 'I'.
    REFRESH ct_rules.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  " Remove header row
  DELETE <lt_data> INDEX 1.

  " Transfer data to internal ruleset table
  LOOP AT <lt_data> ASSIGNING <ls_data>.

    APPEND INITIAL LINE TO ct_rules ASSIGNING <ls_rule>.
    ASSIGN COMPONENT 1 OF STRUCTURE <ls_data> TO <lv_field>.
    <ls_rule>-step = <lv_field>.

    ASSIGN COMPONENT 2 OF STRUCTURE <ls_data> TO <lv_field>.
    <ls_rule>-check_rule = <lv_field>.

    ASSIGN COMPONENT 3 OF STRUCTURE <ls_data> TO <lv_field>.
    <ls_rule>-final_step = <lv_field>.

    ASSIGN COMPONENT 4 OF STRUCTURE <ls_data> TO <lv_field>.
    <ls_rule>-type = <lv_field>.

    ASSIGN COMPONENT 5 OF STRUCTURE <ls_data> TO <lv_field>.
    <ls_rule>-tcode = <lv_field>.

    ASSIGN COMPONENT 6 OF STRUCTURE <ls_data> TO <lv_field>.
    <ls_rule>-objct = <lv_field>.

    ASSIGN COMPONENT 7 OF STRUCTURE <ls_data> TO <lv_field>.
    <ls_rule>-field = <lv_field>.

    ASSIGN COMPONENT 8 OF STRUCTURE <ls_data> TO <lv_field>.
    <ls_rule>-von = <lv_field>.

  ENDLOOP.

  " Save the filename
  SET PARAMETER ID 'DXFILENAME' FIELD iv_file.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form zip_data
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Archive dataset
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PT_DATASET_COMP Source data
*&      --> PV_FILENAME     File name
*&      <-- CV_ZIP_DATA     Archived data
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM zip_data  USING    pv_type    TYPE c
                        pt_dataset_comp TYPE stringtab
                        pv_filename     TYPE string
               CHANGING cv_zip_data     TYPE xstring
                        ev_error TYPE flag.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_objects,
           object TYPE agobject,
           oclss  TYPE xuobjclass,
         END OF lty_objects.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_fields,
           field TYPE xufield,
           text  TYPE as4text,
         END OF lty_fields.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_agr_name,
           agr_name TYPE agr_name,
         END OF lty_agr_name.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_prof,
           profn TYPE xuprofname,
         END OF lty_prof.
  TYPES: BEGIN OF lty_value_text,
           actvt TYPE activ_auth,
           ltext TYPE xutxt30,
         END OF lty_value_text.

  DATA: lt_objects_class TYPE SORTED TABLE OF lty_objects
          WITH UNIQUE KEY object,
        lt_fields        TYPE SORTED TABLE OF lty_fields
          WITH UNIQUE KEY field,
        lt_value_text    TYPE SORTED TABLE OF lty_value_text
          WITH UNIQUE KEY actvt,
        ls_fields        TYPE lty_fields,
        lt_agr_text      TYPE gty_t_agr_text,
        lt_prof_text     TYPE gty_t_prof_text,
        lt_object_text   TYPE gty_t_object_text.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_objects>     TYPE lty_objects,
                 <ls_fields>      TYPE lty_fields,
                 <ls_agr_text>    TYPE gty_agr_text,
                 <ls_prof_text>   TYPE gty_prof_text,
                 <ls_object_text> TYPE gty_object_text,
                 <ls_value_text>  TYPE lty_value_text.

  CLEAR ev_error.

  " Roles/Profiles texts
  IF gc_dataset_ver CS 'V3.'.
    " Role texts
    SELECT agr_name spras text
      INTO TABLE lt_agr_text
      FROM agr_texts                                    "#EC CI_GENBUFF
        FOR ALL ENTRIES IN gt_role_result
      WHERE agr_name EQ gt_role_result-agr_name
        AND spras    IN gr_languages
        AND line     EQ '00000'.

    SORT lt_agr_text BY agr_name spras.

    " Profile texts
    SELECT profn langu ptext
     INTO TABLE lt_prof_text
     FROM usr11                                         "#EC CI_GENBUFF
       FOR ALL ENTRIES IN gt_role_result
     WHERE langu IN gr_languages
       AND profn EQ gt_role_result-auth
       AND aktps EQ 'A'.

    SORT lt_prof_text BY profn langu.

    " Values texts
    SELECT actvt
           ltext
     FROM tactt
     INTO TABLE lt_value_text
     WHERE spras EQ 'E'.

    " Additional data for authorization objects
    SELECT objct AS object
            oclss
      INTO TABLE lt_objects_class
      FROM tobj AS obj
        FOR ALL ENTRIES IN gt_object_result
      WHERE obj~objct EQ gt_object_result-object.

    " Authorization Object texts
    SELECT object
           ttext
      FROM tobjt                                        "#EC CI_GENBUFF
      INTO TABLE lt_object_text
        FOR ALL ENTRIES IN gt_object_result
      WHERE langu  EQ 'E'
        AND object EQ gt_object_result-object.

    " Authorization fields description
    LOOP AT gt_object_result ASSIGNING <gs_object_result>.
      CLEAR ls_fields.
      ls_fields-field = <gs_object_result>-field.
      INSERT ls_fields INTO TABLE lt_fields.
    ENDLOOP.
    LOOP AT lt_fields ASSIGNING <ls_fields>.
      CALL FUNCTION 'AUTH_FIELD_GET_INFO'
        EXPORTING
          fieldname = <ls_fields>-field
          langu     = 'E'
        IMPORTING
          text      = <ls_fields>-text.
    ENDLOOP.
  ENDIF.

  DATA: lv_dataset   TYPE string,
        lv_datasetx  TYPE xstring,
        lv_name      TYPE string,
        lv_text      TYPE string,
        lv_ext       TYPE string, "##NEEDED

        lt_user_data TYPE gty_t_user_data,
        ls_user_data TYPE gty_user_data,
        lt_user_role TYPE gty_t_user_role,
        ls_user_role TYPE gty_user_role,
        lt_role_data TYPE gty_t_role_data,
        ls_role_data TYPE gty_role_data,
        lt_role_user TYPE gty_t_role_user,
        ls_role_user TYPE gty_role_user.

  DATA: lv_size             TYPE abap_msize,
        lv_size_char(10)    TYPE c,
        lc_max_size         TYPE abap_msize VALUE 2000000000,
        lc_parameter        TYPE tpara-paramid VALUE 'ALV_EXPORT',
        lv_ratio            TYPE f,
        lv_parts            TYPE i,
        lv_lines            TYPE i,
        lv_package_size     TYPE i,
        lv_count(2)         TYPE n,
        lv_filename         TYPE string,
        lt_role_result      LIKE gt_role_result,
        lt_role_result_rv   LIKE gt_role_result_rv,
        lt_object_result    LIKE gt_object_result,
        lt_object_result_rv LIKE gt_object_result_rv,
        lt_user_data_tmp    LIKE lt_user_data,
        lt_role_data_tmp    LIKE lt_role_data.

  DATA: lr_error TYPE REF TO cx_sy_compression_error.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_row>              TYPE string,
                 <ls_role_result_rv>   LIKE LINE OF gt_role_result_rv,
                 <ls_object_result_rv> LIKE LINE OF gt_object_result_rv,
                 <ls_user_data>        LIKE LINE OF lt_user_data,
                 <ls_role_data>        LIKE LINE OF lt_role_data.

  " SET/GET parameter to adjust the max. size for the data packages
  GET PARAMETER ID lc_parameter FIELD lv_size_char.
  IF sy-subrc = 0 AND lv_size_char CO ' 0123456789'.
    lc_max_size = lv_size_char.
  ENDIF.

  " Convert dataset to string
  LOOP AT pt_dataset_comp ASSIGNING <ls_row>.
    IF lv_dataset IS INITIAL.
      lv_dataset = <ls_row>.
    ELSE.
      CONCATENATE lv_dataset <ls_row>
        INTO lv_dataset SEPARATED BY gc_row_separator.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.

  CLEAR go_conv_xstr.
  TRY.
      go_conv_xstr = cl_abap_conv_out_ce=>create( ignore_cerr = 'X' ).

      go_conv_xstr->write( data = lv_dataset ).
      lv_datasetx = go_conv_xstr->get_buffer( ).
    CATCH cx_root.
      MESSAGE ID sy-msgid TYPE 'I' NUMBER sy-msgno
              WITH sy-msgv1 sy-msgv2 sy-msgv3 sy-msgv4.

      RETURN.
  ENDTRY.

  SPLIT pv_filename AT '.' INTO lv_name lv_ext.
  lv_name = lv_name && '.' && 'txt'.

  CLEAR go_zip.
  CREATE OBJECT go_zip.

  " Add file to zip
  CALL METHOD go_zip->add
    EXPORTING
      name    = lv_name
      content = lv_datasetx.

  CLEAR lv_datasetx.

  " Add global tables for Users, Roles and Objects
  IF gc_dataset_ver CS 'V3.'.

    "---------------------------------------------
    " Object Data
    "---------------------------------------------
    LOOP AT gt_object_result ASSIGNING <gs_object_result>.
      READ TABLE lt_objects_class ASSIGNING <ls_objects>
        WITH TABLE KEY object = <gs_object_result>-object.
      IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
        <gs_object_result>-oclass = <ls_objects>-oclss.
      ENDIF.
      READ TABLE lt_fields ASSIGNING <ls_fields>
        WITH TABLE KEY field = <gs_object_result>-field.
      IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
        <gs_object_result>-fieldtext = <ls_fields>-text.
      ENDIF.
      READ TABLE lt_object_text ASSIGNING <ls_object_text>
        WITH TABLE KEY object = <gs_object_result>-object.
      IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
        <gs_object_result>-objecttext = <ls_object_text>-ttext.
      ENDIF.
      READ TABLE lt_value_text ASSIGNING <ls_value_text>
        WITH TABLE KEY actvt = <gs_object_result>-low.
      IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
        <gs_object_result>-valuetext = <ls_value_text>-ltext.
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.

    TRY.
        lv_filename = 'OBJECT_RESULT.bin'.

        " We need to know how much data we are talking about here...
        CALL METHOD cl_abap_memory_utilities=>get_memory_size_of_object
          EXPORTING
            object          = gt_object_result
          IMPORTING
            bound_size_used = lv_size.

        lv_ratio = lv_size / lc_max_size + '0.5'.

        CALL FUNCTION 'ROUND'
          EXPORTING
            input  = lv_ratio
          IMPORTING
            output = lv_parts.

        IF lv_parts > 1. " We need to split the data

          lv_lines = lines( gt_object_result ) / lv_parts. " Lines per part
          lv_count = 0.

          DO lv_parts TIMES.

            ADD 1 TO lv_count.
            CONCATENATE 'OBJECT_RESULT_' lv_count '.bin' INTO lv_filename.

            " Split the data
            DO lv_lines TIMES.
              READ TABLE gt_object_result ASSIGNING <gs_object_result> INDEX 1.
              IF sy-subrc = 0.
                " Shift record to 2nd table
                APPEND <gs_object_result> TO lt_object_result. "#EC CI_APPEND_OK
                " Remove record from original table
                DELETE gt_object_result INDEX 1.
              ENDIF.
            ENDDO.

            " Export data
            EXPORT object_result = lt_object_result TO DATA BUFFER lv_datasetx COMPRESSION ON.

            " Add the exported data to the zip file
            CALL METHOD go_zip->add
              EXPORTING
                name    = lv_filename " 'OBJECT_RESULT_xx.bin'
                content = lv_datasetx.

            CLEAR: lv_datasetx, lt_object_result.

          ENDDO.

        ENDIF.

        " Export the (remaining) data to add it to the zip file
        EXPORT object_result = gt_object_result TO DATA BUFFER lv_datasetx COMPRESSION ON.

      CATCH cx_sy_compression_error INTO lr_error.
        " Error Handling
        CONCATENATE 'Compressing Object Results:' lv_filename INTO lv_text SEPARATED BY space.
        MESSAGE lv_text TYPE 'I'.
        ev_error = 'X'.
        RETURN.
    ENDTRY.

    CALL METHOD go_zip->add
      EXPORTING
        name    = 'OBJECT_RESULT.bin'
        content = lv_datasetx.

    CLEAR lv_datasetx.

    "-------------------------------------------------
    " Role Results - Add Role / Profile descriptions
    "-------------------------------------------------
    IF lines( gt_role_result ) = 0.
      " Something went wrong, we have no data, maybe due to a previous error.
      lv_text = 'Export not possible, please restart the evaluation'.
      MESSAGE lv_text TYPE 'I'.
      ev_error = 'X'.
      RETURN.
    ENDIF.

    LOOP AT gt_role_result ASSIGNING <gs_role_result>.
      IF <gs_role_result>-agr_name IS NOT INITIAL.
        READ TABLE lt_agr_text ASSIGNING <ls_agr_text>
             WITH KEY agr_name = <gs_role_result>-agr_name
             BINARY SEARCH.

        IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
          <gs_role_result>-roletext = <ls_agr_text>-text.
        ENDIF.
      ELSEIF <gs_role_result>-auth IS NOT INITIAL.
        READ TABLE lt_prof_text ASSIGNING <ls_prof_text>
             WITH KEY profn = <gs_role_result>-auth
             BINARY SEARCH.

        IF sy-subrc EQ 0.
          <gs_role_result>-roletext = <ls_prof_text>-ptext.
        ENDIF.
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.

    TRY.
        lv_filename = 'ROLE_RESULT.bin'.

        " We need to know how much data we are talking about here...
        CALL METHOD cl_abap_memory_utilities=>get_memory_size_of_object
          EXPORTING
            object          = gt_role_result
          IMPORTING
            bound_size_used = lv_size.

        lv_ratio = lv_size / lc_max_size + '0.5'.

        CALL FUNCTION 'ROUND'
          EXPORTING
            input  = lv_ratio
          IMPORTING
            output = lv_parts.

        IF lv_parts > 1. " We need to split the data

          lv_lines = lines( gt_role_result ) / lv_parts. " Lines per part
          lv_count = 0.

          DO lv_parts TIMES.

            ADD 1 TO lv_count.
            CONCATENATE 'ROLE_RESULT_' lv_count '.bin' INTO lv_filename.

            " Split the data
            CLEAR lv_package_size.
*            DO lv_lines TIMES.
            DO.
              READ TABLE gt_role_result ASSIGNING <gs_role_result> INDEX 1.
              IF sy-subrc <> 0.
                EXIT.
              ELSE.
                " Shift record to 2nd table
                APPEND <gs_role_result> TO lt_role_result. "#EC CI_APPEND_OK

                " Add the line size to the total size of the data package
                lv_package_size = lv_package_size + 800 + lines( <gs_role_result>-objects ) * 860.

                " Remove record from original table
                DELETE gt_role_result INDEX 1.

                IF lv_package_size >= lc_max_size.
                  EXIT.
                ENDIF.

              ENDIF.
            ENDDO.

            " Export data
            EXPORT role_result = lt_role_result TO DATA BUFFER lv_datasetx COMPRESSION ON.

            " Add the exported data to the zip file
            CALL METHOD go_zip->add
              EXPORTING
                name    = lv_filename " 'ROLE_RESULT_xx.bin'
                content = lv_datasetx.

            CLEAR: lv_datasetx, lt_role_result.

          ENDDO.

        ENDIF.

        " Take care of the (remaining) Role Results
        IF lines( gt_role_result ) > 0.

          ADD 1 TO lv_count.
          CONCATENATE 'ROLE_RESULT_' lv_count '.bin' INTO lv_filename.

          " Export the (remaining) data to add it to the zip file
          EXPORT role_result = gt_role_result TO DATA BUFFER lv_datasetx COMPRESSION ON.

          " Add the (remaining) data to the zip file
          CALL METHOD go_zip->add
            EXPORTING
              name    = lv_filename " 'ROLE_RESULT.bin'
              content = lv_datasetx.
        ENDIF.

      CATCH cx_sy_compression_error INTO lr_error.
        " Error Handling
        CONCATENATE 'Compressing Role Results:' lv_filename INTO lv_text SEPARATED BY space.
        MESSAGE lv_text TYPE 'I'.
        ev_error = 'X'.
        RETURN.

    ENDTRY.

    CLEAR lv_datasetx.

    "---------------------------------------------
    " User Data
    "---------------------------------------------
    IF gv_export_type = gc_export_type-sap.
      " Export result for SAP - Hashed user
      LOOP AT gt_user_data INTO ls_user_data.
        PERFORM hash_data USING ls_user_data-bname
                       CHANGING gv_hash_bname.
        ls_user_data-bname = gv_hash_bname.
        CLEAR ls_user_data-name_text.

        IF NOT ls_user_data-refuser IS INITIAL.
          PERFORM hash_data USING ls_user_data-refuser
                         CHANGING gv_hash_bname.
          ls_user_data-refuser = gv_hash_bname.
        ENDIF.

        IF pv_type EQ gc_valid_type-role_validation.
          CLEAR lt_user_role.
          LOOP AT ls_user_data-roles INTO ls_user_role.
            READ TABLE gt_role_result ASSIGNING <gs_role_result>
              WITH TABLE KEY agr_name = ls_user_role-agr_name
                                 auth = ls_user_role-auth.
            IF sy-subrc = 0.
              ls_user_role-index_role = sy-tabix.
              INSERT ls_user_role INTO TABLE lt_user_role.
            ENDIF.
          ENDLOOP.
          ls_user_data-roles[] = lt_user_role[].
        ENDIF.
        INSERT ls_user_data INTO TABLE lt_user_data.
      ENDLOOP.

      TRY.
          lv_filename = 'USER_DATA.bin'.

          " We need to know how much data we are talking about here...
          CALL METHOD cl_abap_memory_utilities=>get_memory_size_of_object
            EXPORTING
              object          = lt_user_data
            IMPORTING
              bound_size_used = lv_size.

          lv_ratio = lv_size / lc_max_size + '0.5'.

          CALL FUNCTION 'ROUND'
            EXPORTING
              input  = lv_ratio
            IMPORTING
              output = lv_parts.

          IF lv_parts > 1. " We need to split the data

            lv_lines = lines( lt_user_data ) / lv_parts. " Lines per part
            lv_count = 0.

            DO lv_parts TIMES.

              ADD 1 TO lv_count.
              CONCATENATE 'USER_DATA_' lv_count '.bin' INTO lv_filename.

              " Split the data
              DO lv_lines TIMES.
                READ TABLE lt_user_data ASSIGNING <ls_user_data> INDEX 1.
                IF sy-subrc = 0.
                  " Shift record to 2nd table
                  APPEND <ls_user_data> TO lt_user_data_tmp. "#EC CI_APPEND_OK
                  " Remove record from original table
                  DELETE lt_user_data INDEX 1.
                ENDIF.
              ENDDO.

              " Export data
              EXPORT user_data = lt_user_data_tmp TO DATA BUFFER lv_datasetx COMPRESSION ON.

              " Add the exported data to the zip file
              CALL METHOD go_zip->add
                EXPORTING
                  name    = lv_filename " 'USER_DATA_xx.bin'
                  content = lv_datasetx.

              CLEAR: lv_datasetx, lt_user_data_tmp.

            ENDDO.

          ENDIF.

          " Export the (remaining) data to add it to the zip file
          EXPORT user_data = lt_user_data TO DATA BUFFER lv_datasetx COMPRESSION ON.

        CATCH cx_sy_compression_error INTO lr_error.
          " Error Handling
          CONCATENATE 'Compressing User Data:' lv_filename INTO lv_text SEPARATED BY space.
          MESSAGE lv_text TYPE 'I'.
          ev_error = 'X'.
          RETURN.
      ENDTRY.

      CLEAR lt_user_data.

    ELSE.

      CLEAR lt_user_data.

      TRY.
          lv_filename = 'USER_DATA.bin'.

          " We need to know how much data we are talking about here...
          CALL METHOD cl_abap_memory_utilities=>get_memory_size_of_object
            EXPORTING
              object          = gt_user_data
            IMPORTING
              bound_size_used = lv_size.

          lv_ratio = lv_size / lc_max_size + '0.5'.

          CALL FUNCTION 'ROUND'
            EXPORTING
              input  = lv_ratio
            IMPORTING
              output = lv_parts.

          IF lv_parts > 1. " We need to split the data

            lv_lines = lines( gt_user_data ) / lv_parts. " Lines per part
            lv_count = 0.

            DO lv_parts TIMES.

              ADD 1 TO lv_count.
              CONCATENATE 'USER_DATA_' lv_count '.bin' INTO lv_filename.

              " Split the data
              DO lv_lines TIMES.
                READ TABLE gt_user_data ASSIGNING <ls_user_data> INDEX 1.
                IF sy-subrc = 0.
                  " Shift record to 2nd table
                  APPEND <ls_user_data> TO lt_user_data. "#EC CI_APPEND_OK
                  " Remove record from original table
                  DELETE gt_user_data INDEX 1.
                ENDIF.
              ENDDO.

              " Export data
              EXPORT user_data = lt_user_data TO DATA BUFFER lv_datasetx COMPRESSION ON.

              " Add the exported data to the zip file
              CALL METHOD go_zip->add
                EXPORTING
                  name    = lv_filename " 'USER_DATA_xx.bin'
                  content = lv_datasetx.

              CLEAR: lv_datasetx, lt_user_data.

            ENDDO.

          ENDIF.

          " Export the (remaining) data to add it to the zip file
          EXPORT user_data = gt_user_data TO DATA BUFFER lv_datasetx COMPRESSION ON.

        CATCH cx_sy_compression_error INTO lr_error.
          " Error Handling
          CONCATENATE 'Compressing User Data:' lv_filename INTO lv_text SEPARATED BY space.
          MESSAGE lv_text TYPE 'I'.
          ev_error = 'X'.
          RETURN.
      ENDTRY.

    ENDIF.

    " Add the (remaining) data to the zip file
    CALL METHOD go_zip->add
      EXPORTING
        name    = 'USER_DATA.bin'
        content = lv_datasetx.

    CLEAR lv_datasetx.

    "---------------------------------------------
    " Role Data
    "---------------------------------------------
    IF pv_type EQ gc_valid_type-role_validation.
      IF gv_export_type EQ gc_export_type-sap.
        " Export result for SAP - Hashed user
        LOOP AT gt_role_data INTO ls_role_data.
          CLEAR lt_role_user.
          LOOP AT ls_role_data-users INTO ls_role_user.
            PERFORM hash_data USING ls_role_user-bname
                           CHANGING gv_hash_bname.
            ls_role_user-bname = gv_hash_bname.
            INSERT ls_role_user INTO TABLE lt_role_user.
          ENDLOOP.
          ls_role_data-users[] = lt_role_user[].
          INSERT ls_role_data INTO TABLE lt_role_data.
        ENDLOOP.

        TRY.
            lv_filename = 'ROLE_DATA.bin'.

            " We need to know how much data we are talking about here...
            CALL METHOD cl_abap_memory_utilities=>get_memory_size_of_object
              EXPORTING
                object          = lt_role_data
              IMPORTING
                bound_size_used = lv_size.

            lv_ratio = lv_size / lc_max_size + '0.5'.

            CALL FUNCTION 'ROUND'
              EXPORTING
                input  = lv_ratio
              IMPORTING
                output = lv_parts.

            IF lv_parts > 1. " We need to split the data

              lv_lines = lines( lt_role_data ) / lv_parts. " Lines per part
              lv_count = 0.

              DO lv_parts TIMES.

                ADD 1 TO lv_count.
                CONCATENATE 'ROLE_DATA_' lv_count '.bin' INTO lv_filename.

                " Split the data
                DO lv_lines TIMES.
                  READ TABLE lt_role_data ASSIGNING <ls_role_data> INDEX 1.
                  IF sy-subrc = 0.
                    " Shift record to 2nd table
                    APPEND <ls_role_data> TO lt_role_data_tmp. "#EC CI_APPEND_OK
                    " Remove record from original table
                    DELETE lt_role_data INDEX 1.
                  ENDIF.
                ENDDO.

                " Export data
                EXPORT role_data = lt_role_data_tmp TO DATA BUFFER lv_datasetx COMPRESSION ON.

                " Add the exported data to the zip file
                CALL METHOD go_zip->add
                  EXPORTING
                    name    = lv_filename " 'ROLE_DATA_xx.bin'
                    content = lv_datasetx.

                CLEAR: lv_datasetx, lt_role_data_tmp.

              ENDDO.

            ENDIF.

            " Export the (remaining) data to add it to the zip file
            EXPORT role_data = lt_role_data TO DATA BUFFER lv_datasetx COMPRESSION ON.

          CATCH cx_sy_compression_error INTO lr_error.
            " Error Handling
            CONCATENATE 'Compressing Role Data:' lv_filename INTO lv_text SEPARATED BY space.
            MESSAGE lv_text TYPE 'I'.
            ev_error = 'X'.
            RETURN.
        ENDTRY.

        CLEAR lt_role_data.

      ELSE.

        CLEAR lt_role_data.

        TRY.
            lv_filename = 'ROLE_DATA.bin'.

            " We need to know how much data we are talking about here...
            CALL METHOD cl_abap_memory_utilities=>get_memory_size_of_object
              EXPORTING
                object          = gt_role_data
              IMPORTING
                bound_size_used = lv_size.

            lv_ratio = lv_size / lc_max_size + '0.5'.

            CALL FUNCTION 'ROUND'
              EXPORTING
                input  = lv_ratio
              IMPORTING
                output = lv_parts.

            IF lv_parts > 1. " We need to split the data

              lv_lines = lines( gt_role_data ) / lv_parts. " Lines per part
              lv_count = 0.

              DO lv_parts TIMES.

                ADD 1 TO lv_count.
                CONCATENATE 'ROLE_DATA_' lv_count '.bin' INTO lv_filename.

                " Split the data
                DO lv_lines TIMES.
                  READ TABLE gt_role_data ASSIGNING <ls_role_data> INDEX 1.
                  IF sy-subrc = 0.
                    " Shift record to 2nd table
                    APPEND <ls_role_data> TO lt_role_data. "#EC CI_APPEND_OK
                    " Remove record from original table
                    DELETE gt_role_data INDEX 1.
                  ENDIF.
                ENDDO.

                " Export data
                EXPORT role_data = lt_role_data TO DATA BUFFER lv_datasetx COMPRESSION ON.

                " Add the exported data to the zip file
                CALL METHOD go_zip->add
                  EXPORTING
                    name    = lv_filename " 'ROLE_DATA_xx.bin'
                    content = lv_datasetx.

                CLEAR: lv_datasetx, lt_role_data.

              ENDDO.

            ENDIF.

            " Export the (remaining) data to add it to the zip file
            EXPORT role_data = gt_role_data TO DATA BUFFER lv_datasetx COMPRESSION ON.

          CATCH cx_sy_compression_error INTO lr_error.
            " Error Handling
            CONCATENATE 'Compressing Role Data:' lv_filename INTO lv_text SEPARATED BY space.
            MESSAGE lv_text TYPE 'I'.
            ev_error = 'X'.
            RETURN.
        ENDTRY.

      ENDIF.

      CALL METHOD go_zip->add
        EXPORTING
          name    = 'ROLE_DATA.bin'
          content = lv_datasetx.

    ENDIF.
  ENDIF.

  " Save the zip archive
  CLEAR lv_datasetx.
  cv_zip_data = go_zip->save( ).

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form unzip_data
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Unzip uploaded data
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PV_DATA     Source data
*&      <-- CT_DATASET  Unzipped data(or decrypted txt data)
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM unzip_data  USING    pv_data    TYPE xstring
                 CHANGING cv_dataset TYPE xstring.

  DATA: lv_datasetx      TYPE xstring,

        lt_user_data     TYPE gty_t_user_data,
        ls_user_data     TYPE gty_user_data,
        lt_role_data     TYPE gty_t_role_data,
        ls_role_data     TYPE gty_role_data,
        lt_role_user     TYPE gty_t_role_user,
        ls_role_user     TYPE gty_role_user,

        lt_object_result LIKE gt_object_result,
        lt_role_result   LIKE gt_role_result.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_file> TYPE cl_abap_zip=>t_file.

  " Clear the table we are about to fill now
  CLEAR: gt_object_result, gt_role_result, gt_user_data.

  CLEAR go_zip.
  CREATE OBJECT go_zip.
  go_zip->load( pv_data ).

  READ TABLE go_zip->files INDEX 1 ASSIGNING <ls_file>.
  IF sy-subrc = 0. " We have a ZIP file
    go_zip->get(
      EXPORTING name    = <ls_file>-name
      IMPORTING content = cv_dataset ).
  ELSE. " No ZIP file, plain text instead
    cv_dataset = pv_data.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  " Object Results
  LOOP AT go_zip->files ASSIGNING <ls_file> WHERE name CS 'OBJECT_RESULT'.
    go_zip->get(
      EXPORTING name    = <ls_file>-name
      IMPORTING content = lv_datasetx ).
    IMPORT object_result = lt_object_result FROM DATA BUFFER lv_datasetx
      ACCEPTING PADDING
      ACCEPTING TRUNCATION
      IGNORING CONVERSION ERRORS REPLACEMENT CHARACTER ''.
    INSERT LINES OF lt_object_result INTO TABLE gt_object_result.
    CLEAR lt_object_result.
  ENDLOOP.

  " Role Results
  LOOP AT go_zip->files ASSIGNING <ls_file> WHERE name CS 'ROLE_RESULT'.
    go_zip->get(
      EXPORTING name    = <ls_file>-name
      IMPORTING content = lv_datasetx ).
    IMPORT role_result = lt_role_result FROM DATA BUFFER lv_datasetx
      ACCEPTING PADDING
      ACCEPTING TRUNCATION
      IGNORING CONVERSION ERRORS REPLACEMENT CHARACTER ''.
    INSERT LINES OF lt_role_result INTO TABLE gt_role_result.
    CLEAR lt_role_result.
  ENDLOOP.

  " User Data
  LOOP AT go_zip->files ASSIGNING <ls_file> WHERE name CS 'USER_DATA'.
    go_zip->get(
      EXPORTING name    = <ls_file>-name
      IMPORTING content = lv_datasetx ).
    IMPORT user_data = lt_user_data FROM DATA BUFFER lv_datasetx
      ACCEPTING PADDING
      ACCEPTING TRUNCATION
      IGNORING CONVERSION ERRORS REPLACEMENT CHARACTER ''.

    LOOP AT lt_user_data INTO ls_user_data.
      READ TABLE gt_hash_users ASSIGNING <gs_hash_users>
        WITH TABLE KEY hash_bname = ls_user_data-bname.
      IF sy-subrc = 0.
        ls_user_data-bname      = <gs_hash_users>-bname.
        ls_user_data-name_text  = <gs_hash_users>-name_text.
        ls_user_data-hash_bname = <gs_hash_users>-hash_bname.
      ENDIF.
      INSERT ls_user_data INTO TABLE gt_user_data.
    ENDLOOP.
    CLEAR lt_user_data.
  ENDLOOP.

  LOOP AT go_zip->files ASSIGNING <ls_file> WHERE name CS 'ROLE_DATA'.
    go_zip->get(
      EXPORTING name    = <ls_file>-name
      IMPORTING content = lv_datasetx ).
    IMPORT role_data = lt_role_data FROM DATA BUFFER lv_datasetx
      ACCEPTING PADDING
      ACCEPTING TRUNCATION
      IGNORING CONVERSION ERRORS REPLACEMENT CHARACTER ''.

    LOOP AT lt_role_data INTO ls_role_data.
      CLEAR lt_role_user.
      LOOP AT ls_role_data-users INTO ls_role_user.
        READ TABLE gt_hash_users ASSIGNING <gs_hash_users>
          WITH TABLE KEY hash_bname = ls_role_user-bname.
        IF sy-subrc = 0.
          ls_role_user-bname      = <gs_hash_users>-bname.
        ENDIF.
        INSERT ls_role_user INTO TABLE lt_role_user.
      ENDLOOP.

      ls_role_data-users[] = lt_role_user[].
      INSERT ls_role_data INTO TABLE gt_role_data.
    ENDLOOP.
    CLEAR lt_user_data.
  ENDLOOP.

  CLEAR lv_datasetx.

ENDFORM.
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form convert_to_dataset
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Convert a data string to a dataset format
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> PV_DATASET       Data string
*&      <-- CT_DATASET_COMP  Dataset
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM convert_to_dataset  USING    pv_dataset      TYPE xstring
                         CHANGING ct_dataset_comp TYPE stringtab.

  DATA: lv_dataset TYPE string.

  CLEAR go_conv_str.

  TRY.
      go_conv_str = cl_abap_conv_in_ce=>create(
        ignore_cerr = 'X'
        input       = pv_dataset ).

      go_conv_str->read( IMPORTING data = lv_dataset ).
    CATCH cx_root.
      MESSAGE ID sy-msgid TYPE 'I' NUMBER sy-msgno
              WITH sy-msgv1 sy-msgv2 sy-msgv3 sy-msgv4.
      RETURN.
  ENDTRY.

  SPLIT lv_dataset AT gc_row_separator INTO TABLE ct_dataset_comp.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form get_note_version
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Get note version and status for the export file
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM get_note_version CHANGING cv_version TYPE c.

  DATA: ls_note       TYPE bcwbn_note,
        lt_components TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF cvers_sdu,
        ls_component  LIKE LINE OF lt_components.

  " Get Basis Release and SP
  CALL FUNCTION 'DELIVERY_GET_INSTALLED_COMPS'
    TABLES
      tt_comptab       = lt_components
    EXCEPTIONS
      no_release_found = 1
      OTHERS           = 2.

  IF sy-subrc = 0.
    READ TABLE lt_components WITH KEY component = 'SAP_BASIS' INTO ls_component.
  ENDIF.

  " Get Note Version
  ls_note-key-numm = '0003113382'.

  CALL FUNCTION 'SCWB_NOTE_READ'
    EXPORTING
      iv_read_attributes          = 'X'
      iv_read_customer_attributes = 'X'
    CHANGING
      cs_note                     = ls_note
    EXCEPTIONS
      note_not_found              = 1
      language_not_found          = 2
      unreadable_text_format      = 3
      corr_instruction_not_found  = 4
      OTHERS                      = 5.

  IF sy-subrc <> 0.
    CONCATENATE '<not available>'
                'SAP_BASIS'
                ls_component-release
                ls_component-extrelease
                INTO cv_version SEPARATED BY ';'.
  ELSE.
    CONCATENATE ls_note-key-versno
                'SAP_BASIS'
                ls_component-release
                ls_component-extrelease
                INTO cv_version SEPARATED BY ';'.
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form transfer_role_classifications
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Transfer the role classifications to Tx license_attributes
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM transfer_role_classifications.

  DATA: lr_selections    TYPE REF TO cl_salv_selections,
        lt_rows          TYPE salv_t_row,
        lv_count         TYPE i,
        lv_text          TYPE text60,
        lv_question(400) TYPE c,
        lv_answer(1)     TYPE c,
        lv_attribute     TYPE tutypa-usertyp.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <lt_table>          TYPE STANDARD TABLE,
                 <ls_record>         TYPE any,
                 <lv_role>           TYPE any,
                 <lv_classification> TYPE any,
                 <lv_current>        TYPE any,
                 <ls_row>            LIKE LINE OF lt_rows.

  " Authorization Check to perform role updates: S_USER_AGR: ACT_GROUP * / ACTVT 02

  " Get the selected rows
  CASE sy-dynnr.
    WHEN 402. " Role Overview
      lr_selections = gr_table402->get_selections( ).
      ASSIGN <gt_role_classif> TO <lt_table>.
    WHEN 500. " Role Validation Results
      lr_selections = gr_table500->get_selections( ).
      ASSIGN <gt_s4_role> TO <lt_table>.
    WHEN OTHERS.
      RETURN.
  ENDCASE.

  " Get the selected rows
  lt_rows = lr_selections->get_selected_rows( ).

  " Any rows selected at all?
  CHECK lt_rows[] IS NOT INITIAL.

  lv_question = TEXT-t16.

  " Do you want to proceed?
  CALL FUNCTION 'POPUP_TO_CONFIRM'
    EXPORTING
      titlebar              = 'Warning' "##NO_TEXT
      text_question         = lv_question
      text_button_1         = 'Yes' "##NO_TEXT
      text_button_2         = 'No'  "##NO_TEXT
      display_cancel_button = ' '
      default_button        = '2'
    IMPORTING
      answer                = lv_answer
    EXCEPTIONS
      text_not_found        = 1
      OTHERS                = 2.

  IF sy-subrc <> 0 OR lv_answer = '2'.
    RETURN.
  ENDIF.

  LOOP AT lt_rows ASSIGNING <ls_row>.
    " Read the selected entry
    READ TABLE <lt_table> ASSIGNING <ls_record> INDEX <ls_row>.
    IF sy-subrc = 0.

      UNASSIGN: <lv_role>, <lv_classification>.

      ASSIGN COMPONENT 'AGR_NAME'   OF STRUCTURE <ls_record> TO <lv_role>.
      ASSIGN COMPONENT 'CLASSIF_S4' OF STRUCTURE <ls_record> TO <lv_classification>.

      IF ( <lv_role> IS ASSIGNED AND <lv_classification> IS ASSIGNED ).

        IF <lv_role> <> space. " Only possible for roles, not for profiles

          CASE <lv_classification>.
            WHEN TEXT-t07 OR TEXT-t24. " Not classified / Engine
              CLEAR lv_attribute.
            WHEN OTHERS.
              lv_attribute = <lv_classification>(2).
          ENDCASE.

          AUTHORITY-CHECK OBJECT 'S_USER_AGR'
          ID 'ACT_GROUP' FIELD <lv_role>
          ID 'ACTVT'     FIELD '02'.

          IF sy-subrc <> 0.
            " User not authorized
            CONCATENATE TEXT-s11 <lv_role> INTO lv_text SEPARATED BY space.
            MESSAGE lv_text TYPE 'I'.
          ELSE.

            " Update the classification
            CALL FUNCTION 'SLIM_SET_LICENSE_ATTRIBUTE_2'
              EXPORTING
                activity_group                = <lv_role>
                license_attribute             = lv_attribute
              EXCEPTIONS
                activity_group_does_not_exist = 1
                db_write_error                = 2
                error                         = 3
                OTHERS                        = 4.

            IF sy-subrc = 0.
              ADD 1 TO lv_count.

              " Update the classification in the ALV table
              ASSIGN COMPONENT 'CLASSIF_CURR' OF STRUCTURE <ls_record> TO <lv_current>.
              IF <lv_current> IS ASSIGNED.

                CLEAR <lv_current>.

                SELECT SINGLE utyptext FROM tutyp INTO <lv_current>
                       WHERE usertyp = lv_attribute
                         AND langu   = sy-langu.

                IF sy-subrc = 0.
                  CONCATENATE lv_attribute <lv_current> INTO <lv_current> SEPARATED BY space.
                ENDIF.
              ENDIF.
            ENDIF.
          ENDIF.
        ENDIF.
      ENDIF.
    ENDIF.

  ENDLOOP.

  IF lv_count = 0.
    " No need to update the ALV if not roles have been updated
    lv_text = '0'.
  ELSE.
    " Update the corresponding ALV Table
    CASE sy-dynnr.
      WHEN 402.
        gr_table402->refresh( ).
      WHEN 500.
        gr_table500->refresh( ).
    ENDCASE.

    WRITE lv_count TO lv_text LEFT-JUSTIFIED NO-ZERO.
  ENDIF.

  " Show the number of updated roles
  CONCATENATE TEXT-s10 lv_text INTO lv_text SEPARATED BY space.
  MESSAGE lv_text TYPE 'S'.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form transfer_user_classifications
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Transfer the user classifications to USR06
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM transfer_user_classifications.

  DATA: lr_selections    TYPE REF TO cl_salv_selections,
        lt_rows          TYPE salv_t_row,
        lv_count         TYPE i,
        lv_text          TYPE text60,
        lv_string        TYPE string,
        lv_question(400) TYPE c,
        lv_answer(1)     TYPE c,
        lv_attribute     TYPE tutypa-usertyp,
        lt_return        TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF bapiret2,
        ls_return        LIKE LINE OF lt_return,
        ls_uclass        TYPE bapiuclass,
        ls_uclassx       TYPE bapiuclassx,
        lv_uname         TYPE bapibname-bapibname.

  DATA: lt_user_return TYPE bapirettab,
        ls_user_return LIKE LINE OF lt_user_return.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_record>         TYPE any,
                 <lv_user>           TYPE any,
                 <lv_class>          TYPE any,
                 <lv_classification> TYPE any,
                 <lv_classif_curr>   TYPE any,
                 <lv_current>        TYPE any,
                 <ls_row>            LIKE LINE OF lt_rows,
                 <ls_user_data>      LIKE LINE OF gt_user_data.

  " Authorization Check to perform role updates: S_USER_GRP: CLASS * / ACTVT 02

  IF <gt_user_classif> IS NOT ASSIGNED.

    " Background processing
    LOOP AT gt_user_data ASSIGNING <ls_user_data>.

      CASE <ls_user_data>-classif_s4.
        WHEN TEXT-t07. " Not classified
          CLEAR lv_attribute.
        WHEN OTHERS.
          lv_attribute = <ls_user_data>-classif_s4(2).
      ENDCASE.

      " Only proceed with the current record if there are changes...
      CHECK lv_attribute <> <ls_user_data>-lic_type.

      " Authorization to change users in the selected user group?
      AUTHORITY-CHECK OBJECT 'S_USER_GRP'
      ID     'CLASS' FIELD <ls_user_data>-class
      ID     'ACTVT' FIELD '02'.

      IF sy-subrc <> 0.
        " User not authorized, collect messages
        CLEAR ls_return.
        ls_return-type = 'E'.
        ls_return-row  = 1.
        IF <ls_user_data>-class IS INITIAL.
          lv_string = '<empty>'.
        ELSE.
          lv_string = <ls_user_data>-class.
        ENDIF.
        CONCATENATE text-s16 lv_string INTO ls_return-message SEPARATED BY space.
        CONCATENATE ls_return-message ':' INTO ls_return-message.
        COLLECT ls_return INTO lt_return.
      ELSE.

        CLEAR: ls_uclassx,
               ls_uclass.

        REFRESH: lt_user_return.

        ls_uclassx-uclass  = 'X'.
        ls_uclass-lic_type = lv_attribute.
        lv_uname           = <ls_user_data>-bname.

        CALL FUNCTION 'BAPI_USER_CHANGE'
          EXPORTING
            username = lv_uname
            uclass   = ls_uclass
            uclassx  = ls_uclassx
          TABLES
            return   = lt_user_return.

        READ TABLE lt_user_return INTO ls_user_return INDEX 1.

        IF ls_user_return-type = 'E'.

          CLEAR ls_return.
          ls_return-type    = 'E'.
          ls_return-row     = 1.
          ls_return-message = ls_user_return-message.
          COLLECT ls_return INTO lt_return.

        ELSE.
          " Collect success message
          CLEAR ls_return.
          ls_return-type    = 'S'.
          ls_return-row     = 1.
          ls_return-message = 'Successfully updated:'.
          COLLECT ls_return INTO lt_return.

          " Update the user data
          <ls_user_data>-lic_type     = lv_attribute.
          <ls_user_data>-classif_curr = <ls_user_data>-classif_s4+2.

        ENDIF.
      ENDIF.
    ENDLOOP.

  ELSE.

    " Get the selected rows
    lr_selections = gr_table401->get_selections( ).
*    ASSIGN <gt_user_classif> TO <lt_table>.
    lt_rows = lr_selections->get_selected_rows( ).

    " Any rows selected at all?
    CHECK lt_rows[] IS NOT INITIAL.

    lv_question = TEXT-t17.

    " Do you want to proceed?
    CALL FUNCTION 'POPUP_TO_CONFIRM'
      EXPORTING
        titlebar              = 'Warning' "##NO_TEXT
        text_question         = lv_question
        text_button_1         = 'Yes' "##NO_TEXT
        text_button_2         = 'No'  "##NO_TEXT
        display_cancel_button = ' '
        default_button        = '2'
      IMPORTING
        answer                = lv_answer
      EXCEPTIONS
        text_not_found        = 1
        OTHERS                = 2.

    IF sy-subrc <> 0 OR lv_answer = '2'.
      RETURN.
    ENDIF.

    LOOP AT lt_rows ASSIGNING <ls_row>.
      " Read the selected entry
      READ TABLE <gt_user_classif> ASSIGNING <ls_record> INDEX <ls_row>.
      IF sy-subrc = 0.

        UNASSIGN: <lv_user>, <lv_classification>, <lv_class>, <lv_current>.
        CLEAR lv_attribute.

        ASSIGN COMPONENT 'BNAME'        OF STRUCTURE <ls_record> TO <lv_user>.
        ASSIGN COMPONENT 'CLASS'        OF STRUCTURE <ls_record> TO <lv_class>.
        ASSIGN COMPONENT 'CLASSIF_S4'   OF STRUCTURE <ls_record> TO <lv_classification>.
        ASSIGN COMPONENT 'LIC_TYPE'     OF STRUCTURE <ls_record> TO <lv_current>.
        ASSIGN COMPONENT 'CLASSIF_CURR' OF STRUCTURE <ls_record> TO <lv_classif_curr>.

        IF ( <lv_user> IS ASSIGNED AND <lv_classification> IS ASSIGNED ).

          CASE <lv_classification>.
            WHEN TEXT-t07. " Not classified
              CLEAR lv_attribute.
            WHEN OTHERS.
              lv_attribute = <lv_classification>(2).
          ENDCASE.

          " Only proceed with the current record if there are changes...
          CHECK lv_attribute <> <lv_current>.

          " Authorization to change users in the selected user group?
          AUTHORITY-CHECK OBJECT 'S_USER_GRP'
          ID     'CLASS' FIELD <lv_class>
          ID     'ACTVT' FIELD '02'.

          IF sy-subrc <> 0.
            " User not authorized, collect messages
            CLEAR ls_return.
            ls_return-type = 'E'.
            ls_return-row  = 1.
            IF <lv_class> IS INITIAL.
              lv_string = '<empty>'.
            ELSE.
              lv_string = <lv_class>.
            ENDIF.
            CONCATENATE text-s16 lv_string INTO ls_return-message SEPARATED BY space.
            CONCATENATE ls_return-message ':' INTO ls_return-message.
            COLLECT ls_return INTO lt_return.
          ELSE.

            CLEAR: ls_uclassx,
                   ls_uclass.

            REFRESH: lt_user_return.

            ls_uclassx-uclass  = 'X'.
            ls_uclass-lic_type = lv_attribute.
            lv_uname           = <lv_user>.

            CALL FUNCTION 'BAPI_USER_CHANGE'
              EXPORTING
                username = lv_uname
                uclass   = ls_uclass
                uclassx  = ls_uclassx
              TABLES
                return   = lt_user_return.

            READ TABLE lt_user_return INTO ls_user_return INDEX 1.

            IF ls_user_return-type = 'E'.

              CLEAR ls_return.
              ls_return-type    = 'E'.
              ls_return-row     = 1.
              ls_return-message = ls_user_return-message.
              COLLECT ls_return INTO lt_return.

            ELSE.

              ADD 1 TO lv_count.

              " Collect success message
              CLEAR ls_return.
              ls_return-type    = 'S'.
              ls_return-row     = 1.
              ls_return-message = 'Successfully updated:'.
              COLLECT ls_return INTO lt_return.

              " Update the classification in the ALV table
              IF <lv_current> IS ASSIGNED.

                <lv_current> = lv_attribute.
                CLEAR: <lv_classif_curr>.

                IF <lv_current> IS INITIAL.
                  " Not classified
                  <lv_classif_curr> = TEXT-t04.
                ELSE.
                  <lv_classif_curr> = <lv_classification>+2.
                ENDIF.
              ENDIF.

            ENDIF. " successfully updated

          ENDIF. " Authorization Check

        ENDIF.
      ENDIF.

    ENDLOOP.

    IF lv_count > 0.
      " Update the corresponding ALV Table
      gr_table401->refresh( ).
    ENDIF.

  ENDIF.

  " Show any error
  LOOP AT lt_return INTO ls_return WHERE type = 'E'.
    WRITE ls_return-row TO lv_text LEFT-JUSTIFIED.
    IF ls_return-row = 1.
      CONCATENATE lv_text 'User' INTO lv_text SEPARATED BY space.
    ELSE.
      CONCATENATE lv_text 'Users' INTO lv_text SEPARATED BY space.
    ENDIF.
    CONCATENATE ls_return-message lv_text INTO lv_text SEPARATED BY space.
    MESSAGE lv_text TYPE 'I'.
  ENDLOOP.

  " Show the number of updated users
  READ TABLE lt_return INTO ls_return WITH KEY type = 'S'.
  IF sy-subrc = 0.
    WRITE ls_return-row TO lv_text LEFT-JUSTIFIED.
    CONCATENATE ls_return-message lv_text INTO lv_text SEPARATED BY space.
  ELSE.
    lv_text = 'No users could be updated'.
  ENDIF.
  MESSAGE lv_text TYPE 'S'.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form show_hide_unclassified_entries
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Show / Hide unclassified entries (Objects / Roles)
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      --> Current dynpro number
*&      --> Current filter flag
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM show_hide_unclassified_entries USING iv_dynnr    TYPE sydynnr
                                 CHANGING cv_filtered TYPE flag.

  DATA: lr_filters TYPE REF TO cl_salv_filters,
        lv_value   TYPE salv_de_selopt_low.

  " Get Filters
  CASE iv_dynnr.
    WHEN 403.
      lr_filters = gr_table403->get_filters( ).
    WHEN 402.
      lr_filters = gr_table402->get_filters( ).
    WHEN 500.
      lr_filters = gr_table500->get_filters( ).
    WHEN OTHERS.
      RETURN.
  ENDCASE.

  IF cv_filtered = 'X'. " Remove existing filter
    TRY.
        lr_filters->remove_filter(
          EXPORTING
            columnname = 'CLASSIF_S4' ).
      CATCH cx_salv_not_found.  "##NO_HANDLER
      CATCH cx_salv_data_error. "##NO_HANDLER
      CATCH cx_salv_existing.   "##NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

  ELSE. " Set filter

    lv_value = TEXT-t07. " Not classified
    TRY.
        lr_filters->add_filter(
          EXPORTING
            columnname = 'CLASSIF_S4'
            sign       = 'E'
            option     = 'EQ'
            low        = lv_value ).
      CATCH cx_salv_not_found.  "##NO_HANDLER
      CATCH cx_salv_data_error. "##NO_HANDLER
      CATCH cx_salv_existing.   "##NO_HANDLER
    ENDTRY.

  ENDIF.

  " Set filter flag
  IF cv_filtered = 'X'.
    cv_filtered = abap_false.
  ELSE.
    cv_filtered = 'X'.
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form get_role_based_classification
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Read the role-based classification
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM get_role_based_classification  USING it_sel_users TYPE gty_t_user_sel
                                          ct_rbc       TYPE gty_t_rbc.

  TYPES: ty_law2_usertypes(2) TYPE c.
  TYPES: ty_law2_t_usertypes TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF ty_law2_usertypes.

  DATA: lt_data        TYPE gty_t_rbc,
        lt_user_types  TYPE ty_law2_t_usertypes,
        lv_usertype    TYPE ty_law2_usertypes,
        lv_tabix       TYPE sy-tabix,
        lv_combination TYPE char100.

  DATA: lr_user_types TYPE REF TO lcl_user_types.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_rbc> LIKE LINE OF ct_rbc.

  CLEAR gv_percent.
  " Preparing Data for User Validation...
  PERFORM show_indicator USING 'Reading Role-based Classifications...' gv_percent. "##NO_TEXT

  CREATE OBJECT lr_user_types.

  SELECT agr_users~uname
         agr_users~agr_name
         agr_flags~flag_value AS usertyp
         FROM agr_users INNER JOIN agr_flags ON agr_users~agr_name = agr_flags~agr_name
         INTO TABLE lt_data
         WHERE agr_users~uname IN so_user
           AND agr_flags~flag_type = 'LICENSE_01'
           AND agr_flags~flag_value <> ''
           AND agr_users~from_dat <= sy-datum
           AND agr_users~to_dat   >= sy-datum
         GROUP BY agr_users~uname agr_users~agr_name flag_value
         ORDER BY agr_users~uname.     "#EC CI_BUFFJOIN "#EC CI_GENBUFF

  LOOP AT lt_data ASSIGNING <ls_rbc>.

    AT NEW uname.

      CLEAR lt_user_types.

    ENDAT.

    lv_usertype = <ls_rbc>-usertyp.
    COLLECT lv_usertype INTO lt_user_types.

    AT END OF uname.

      DESCRIBE TABLE lt_user_types LINES lv_tabix.

      IF lv_tabix = 1.
        APPEND <ls_rbc> TO ct_rbc.
      ELSE.
        " Try to consolidate
        CALL METHOD lr_user_types->consolidate_user_types
          EXPORTING
            it_user_types  = lt_user_types
          IMPORTING
            ev_combination = lv_combination.

        IF lv_combination+2 = space.
          " We received a unique result
          <ls_rbc>-usertyp = lv_combination.
        ELSE.
          " The combination could not be resolved
          <ls_rbc>-usertyp = '##'.
        ENDIF.

        <ls_rbc>-agr_name = '*** MULTIPLE ***'.
        APPEND <ls_rbc> TO ct_rbc.

      ENDIF.

    ENDAT.

  ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form get_ref_user_classification
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Get the reference user classification
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM get_ref_user_classification USING it_sel_users TYPE gty_t_user_sel
                                       ct_refusers  TYPE gty_t_refusers.

  TYPES: BEGIN OF tys_role_cnt,
           uname   TYPE agr_users-uname,
           counter TYPE i,
         END OF tys_role_cnt.

  DATA: lt_ref_role_cnt TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF tys_role_cnt.

  FIELD-SYMBOLS: <ls_refuser> LIKE LINE OF ct_refusers.

  CLEAR gv_percent.
  " Preparing Data for User Validation...
  PERFORM show_indicator USING 'Reading Reference User Classifications...' gv_percent. "##NO_TEXT

  " Check classification via reference user (USREFUS)
  SELECT a~bname a~refuser b~lic_type              "#EC CI_NO_TRANSFORM
         INTO CORRESPONDING FIELDS OF TABLE ct_refusers
         FROM usrefus AS a LEFT OUTER JOIN usr06 AS b  "#EC CI_BUFFJOIN
         ON a~refuser = b~bname
         FOR ALL ENTRIES IN it_sel_users
         WHERE a~bname = it_sel_users-bname
           AND a~refuser  <> ''.

  " Select the number of roles per user
  SELECT uname COUNT( * )
         FROM agr_users INNER JOIN usr02 ON agr_users~uname = usr02~bname
         INTO TABLE lt_ref_role_cnt
         WHERE agr_users~uname IN so_user
           AND usr02~class     IN so_class
           AND agr_users~from_dat <= sy-datum
           AND agr_users~to_dat   >= sy-datum
         GROUP BY uname
         ORDER BY uname.               "#EC CI_BUFFJOIN "#EC CI_GENBUFF

  LOOP AT ct_refusers ASSIGNING <ls_refuser> WHERE lic_type IS NOT INITIAL.
    " Remove users from lt_refusers who have roles assigned
    " (same logic as in USMM)
    READ TABLE lt_ref_role_cnt WITH KEY uname = <ls_refuser>-bname TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS BINARY SEARCH.
    IF sy-subrc = 0.
      DELETE ct_refusers WHERE bname = <ls_refuser>-bname.
    ENDIF.
  ENDLOOP.

  CLEAR lt_ref_role_cnt.

ENDFORM.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Form add_field
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*& Add a field to the field catalog
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM add_field TABLES ct_fields   STRUCTURE dfies
               USING iv_tabname   TYPE ddobjname
                     iv_fieldname TYPE fieldname
                     iv_label     TYPE reptext
                     iv_pos       TYPE tabfdpos
                     iv_offset    TYPE i.

  DATA: ls_field      TYPE dfies,
        lv_fieldname  TYPE dfies-fieldname,
        lv_lfieldname TYPE dfies-lfieldname.

  lv_fieldname  = iv_fieldname.
  lv_lfieldname = iv_fieldname.

  CALL FUNCTION 'DDIF_FIELDINFO_GET'
    EXPORTING
      tabname        = iv_tabname
      fieldname      = lv_fieldname
      lfieldname     = lv_lfieldname
    IMPORTING
      dfies_wa       = ls_field
    EXCEPTIONS
      not_found      = 1
      internal_error = 2
      OTHERS         = 3.

  IF sy-subrc = 0.
    ls_field-scrtext_s = iv_label.
    ls_field-scrtext_m = iv_label.
    ls_field-scrtext_l = iv_label.
    ls_field-reptext   = iv_label.
    ls_field-position  = iv_pos.
    ls_field-offset    = iv_offset.
    APPEND ls_field TO ct_fields.
  ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    "add_field
